### [42] [MEMPROBE: Probing Long-Term Agent Memory via Hidden User-State Recovery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24595)
*Enze Ma,Yufan Zhou,Wei-Chieh Huang,Jie Yang,Huanhuan Ma,Zixuan Wang,Chengze Li,Chunyu Miao,Philip S. Yu,Zhen Wang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 针对LLM长期记忆评估缺乏透明度的问题，本文提出了MEMPROBE基准，通过直接重建和对比智能体所记录的用户画像，揭示了当前LLM“任务完成能力强”但“真实记忆保持能力弱”的现状，为提升智能体个性化记忆能力提供了量化标准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的LLM长期记忆评估多依赖于间接的下游行为（如任务成功率），导致记忆模块本身缺乏透明度和可审计性。作者认为，长期记忆应作为一种独立的可审计产物进行评估，即在交互后能否准确重建用户画像，而非仅仅关注任务是否完成。

Method: 提出了MEMPROBE基准测试框架。该方法通过模拟用户（携带预定义的、基于分类学的用户状态库）与智能体进行交互，在任务结束后，直接从智能体留下的记忆中重建用户状态，并将其与真实的模拟用户状态进行比对评分。测试了5种代表性记忆系统，并在全量存储和Top-k检索两种条件下评估了记忆恢复效果。

Result: 实验发现：1. 任务完成能力在不同模型间已趋于饱和，即使是无记忆基线模型也能表现良好；2. 记忆恢复能力（即准确记住用户状态的能力）表现平平，平衡分类下的恢复得分仅约0.6，在Top-k检索限制下性能进一步下降。这意味着目前的智能体并未真正有效掌握用户状态信息。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了“任务表现”与“记忆恢复能力”是两种截然不同的能力。现有的LLM智能体在完成任务方面已表现出色，但在构建可审计、准确的用户长期记忆方面仍存在明显短板。MEMPROBE为评估和优化智能体的长期记忆能力提供了一个客观、可度量的基准。

Abstract: Long-term memory promises LLM agents that grow more capable across sessions, maintaining an accurate, evolving understanding of the user that interaction forms. In practice, however, this memory is evaluated mostly through downstream behavior, such as later answers, personalization quality, or task success, which tests that understanding only indirectly and leaves the memory artifact itself largely unaudited. We argue that long-term memory should instead be evaluated as an auditable post-interaction artifact: after ordinary assistance, what structured user state can be reconstructed from the memory the agent leaves behind? We instantiate this view in MEMPROBE, a benchmark in which a memory-equipped agent assists simulated users, each carrying a hidden, taxonomy-anchored user-state bank, across a trajectory of leak-controlled tasks, after which that bank is reconstructed from the agent's resulting memory under both full-store and top-k access. Built on synthetic ground truth for efficient, scalable measurement, MEMPROBE spans 50 simulated users with 31 hidden dimensions each (1,550 recovery targets) and tests 5 representative memory systems. Testing state-of-the-art memory agents, we find that successful assistance and recoverable memory behave as distinct capabilities. Task completion nearly saturates, even for a memoryless baseline, while category-balanced recovery stays moderate (about 0.6) and drops further under top-k retrieval. MEMPROBE is the first benchmark to study memory recovery directly, reconstructing the user state a system retains and scoring it against ground truth. We see recovery as a concrete objective for future memory agents to optimize, and MEMPROBE as a step toward an environment where agents are trained to remember their users, growing more faithful the longer they know them.

</details>


### [43] [To Compare, or Not to Compare: On Methodological Practices in Evaluating Social Bias](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24596)
*Federico Marcuzzi,Xuefei Ning,Roy Schwartz,Iryna Gurevych*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该论文揭示了当前大语言模型偏见评估方法论的局限，发现“强制选择比较”评估方式会显著激活并放大模型的隐性歧视，且这种效应随模型规模扩大而增强，提醒业界在部署模型时需谨慎对待比较式推理任务。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大语言模型在社会偏见评估方面存在方法论支离破碎的问题，导致结论相互矛盾。研究认为这是由于忽略了基准评估中的结构性框架所致，亟需建立统一的评估体系以揭示模型的真实偏见。

Method: 引入了一个统一且可控的评估框架，将异构的基准测试标准化，对比“隔离式人口统计学评估”与“强制选择比较设置”。通过该框架，研究分析了思维链（CoT）推理、中立备选选项及其他结构性伪影对社会偏见评估的混淆效应。

Result: 研究发现存在巨大的范式差距：隔离评估限制了偏见的激活，而比较设置则成为潜伏歧视的强力催化剂（主要由语境未明确引起）。此外，思维链推理在比较设置下会加剧社会偏见，且这种“比较偏见”会随模型规模的扩大而增强，即便是提供中立备选选项也无法消除。

Conclusion: 研究提出了一项重要的评估指南：尽管研究人员必须利用比较设置来稳健地审计大模型的隐藏偏见，但在存在歧义的现实任务中，从业者不能安全地依赖此类比较式部署，因为它们会放大模型的隐性歧视。

Abstract: As Large Language Models are increasingly deployed in critical applications, robustly evaluating their social biases is paramount. However, the current literature suffers from widespread methodological fragmentation, which yields contradictory conclusions. This stems largely from ignoring the structural framing of benchmark-level evaluations. To resolve this, we introduce a unified and controllable framework that standardizes heterogeneous benchmarks to systematically contrast isolated demographic assessments with forced-choice comparative settings. Crucially, this allows us to disentangle the confounding effects of Chain-of-Thought reasoning, neutral fallback options, and other structural artifacts in social bias evaluations. Our evaluation across multiple model families reveals a massive, systematic paradigm gap: while isolated assessments limit prejudice activation, comparative settings act as aggressive catalysts for latent discrimination, a shift primarily driven by underspecified contexts. Alarmingly, CoT reasoning exacerbates social biases under comparative settings, and this systemic bias persists as a deterministic prejudice even when models are provided neutral fallback options or claim to answer randomly. Finally, we demonstrate that this comparative prejudice is a generalized phenomenon that scales positively with model size. Ultimately, we offer a crucial methodological guideline: while researchers must leverage comparative settings to robustly audit hidden biases, practitioners cannot safely rely on comparative deployments in ambiguous real-world tasks.

</details>


### [44] [Qwen-AgentWorld: Language World Models for General Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24597)
*Yuxin Zuo,Zikai Xiao,Li Sheng,Fei Huang,Jianhong Tu,Yuxuan Liu,Tianyi Tang,Xiaomeng Hu,Yang Su,Qingfeng Lan,Yantao Liu,Qin Zhu,Yinger Zhang,Bowen Yu,Haiquan Zhao,Haiyang Xu,Jianxin Yang,Jiayang Cheng,Junyang Wang,Lianghao Deng,Mingfeng Xue,Tianyi Bai,Yang Fan,Yubo Ma,Yucheng Li,Zeyu Cui,Zhihai Wang,Zhihui Xie,Zhuorui Ye,An Yang,Dayiheng Liu,Jingren Zhou,Ning Ding*

TL;DR: 该研究通过引入Qwen-AgentWorld大语言世界模型，实现了对复杂环境的高效模拟与推理，不仅在模拟基准上表现卓越，还通过强化学习训练和预训练增强了通用智能体的决策水平。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在探索基于大语言模型的世界建模如何推动通用智能体的发展，解决现有智能体在复杂环境交互与推理中的局限性。

Method: 提出了Qwen-AgentWorld模型，通过三阶段训练流程：(1) CPT阶段注入基于状态转移动态和专业语料的世界建模能力；(2) SFT阶段激活“思维链”引导的下一状态预测推理；(3) RL阶段利用混合评估框架提升模拟的忠实度。同时提出了包含9个基准测试的AgentWorldBench用于评估模型性能。

Result: Qwen-AgentWorld模型在AgentWorldBench测试中显著优于现有前沿模型；作为解耦环境模拟器，它支持可扩展的智能体强化学习，并作为基础模型显著提升了智能体在下游任务中的表现。

Conclusion: 本研究成功构建了基于大语言模型的世界模型Qwen-AgentWorld，证明了将世界建模整合到基础模型中不仅能提升模拟能力，还能有效增强智能体的强化学习效果及多任务泛化能力，为通用智能体的发展提供了新的范式。

Abstract: A world model predicts environment dynamics based on current observations and actions, serving as a core cognitive mechanism for reasoning and planning. In this work, we investigate how world modeling based on language models can further push the boundaries of general agents. (i) We first focus on building foundation models for agentic environment simulation. We introduce Qwen-AgentWorld-35B-A3B and Qwen-AgentWorld-397B-A17B, the first language world models capable of simulating agentic environments covering 7 domains via long chain-of-thought reasoning. Leveraging more than 10M environment interaction trajectories of 7 domains in real-world environments, we develop Qwen-AgentWorld through a three-stage training pipeline: CPT injects general-purpose world modeling capabilities from the state transition dynamics and augmented professional corpora, SFT activates next-state-prediction reasoning, and RL sharpens simulation fidelity through a tailored framework with hybrid rubric-and-rule rewards. To evaluate language world models, we present AgentWorldBench, a comprehensive benchmark constructed from real-world interactions of 5 frontier models on 9 established benchmarks. Empirical results demonstrate that Qwen-AgentWorld significantly outperforms existing frontier models. (ii) Beyond foundation models, we further investigate two complementary paradigms through which world modeling enhances general agents. First, as a decoupled environment simulator, Qwen-AgentWorld supports scalable and controllable simulation of thousands of real-world environments for agentic RL, yielding gains that surpass real-environment training alone. Second, as a unified agent foundation model, world-model training acts as a highly effective warm-up that improves downstream performance across 7 agentic benchmarks. Code: https://github.com/QwenLM/Qwen-AgentWorld

### [45] [Same Lesson, Different Story: Cross-Lingual Reconstruction of Cultural Narratives in Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24610)
*Jory Alshaalan,Haya Albaker,Abeer Aldayel,Aljawharah Alabdullatif,Rehab Alahmadi*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了大型语言模型虽然能保留多语言谚语的核心语义，但在叙事细节上会产生系统性的文化偏置，因此仅凭语义相似度评价模型的文化扎根性是不够的。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在探讨大型语言模型在处理不同文化背景但传达相同道德含义的叙事时，是否能真正保留“文化扎根性”（culturally grounded meaning），以及是否存在对文化背景的忽视。

Method: 研究引入了一个多语言评估叙事框架，收集了涵盖15种语言的414条具有语义等效性的谚语，利用4种大型语言模型生成了1.3万篇叙事。通过比较这些模型在不同语言提示下的输出，评估语义保留情况、跨语言条件对叙事实现的影响以及不同模型家族在解释上的一致性。

Result: 研究发现，跨语言提示在很大程度上保留了谚语层面的语义含义，但在主体性（agency）、社会定位和叙事结构上存在系统性的重构。此外，不同模型在单语言和跨语言环境下表现出高度的一致性，表明模型倾向于依赖共享的语义抽象，而非特定文化背景。

Conclusion: 仅仅依赖语义相似度来评估多语言叙事存在局限性，因为它会忽略叙事表达中具有文化意义的细微差别。未来的评估需要更全面地考虑文化扎根性，不能仅关注语义的一致性。

Abstract: The evaluation of cultural grounding context becomes complex when multiple cultures convey the same moral lesson. This challenge is particularly relevant to large language models (LLMs), which produce narratives across a wide range of languages and cultural contexts. However, it remains uncertain whether these models preserve culturally grounded meaning when equivalent moral lessons are conveyed through distinct cultural forms. This study introduces a multilingual evaluation narrative framework that integrates a cross-linguistic collection of 414 proverbs spanning 15 languages and uses four LLMs to generate 13k narratives. By employing semantically equivalent proverbs as culturally grounded prompts, the analysis assesses whether models preserve meaning across languages, how cross-lingual conditioning influences narrative realization, and whether different model families converge on similar interpretations. Results indicate that cross-lingual prompting largely preserves proverb-level semantic meaning while systematically redistributing agency, social positioning, and narrative structure. Additionally, strong inter-model convergence is observed in both monolingual and cross-lingual settings, suggesting that multilingual LLMs rely on shared semantic abstractions despite architectural and linguistic differences. These findings shed light on the need for more comprehensive evaluations of cultural grounding. Relying exclusively on semantic similarity in multilingual narrative assessments may overestimate cultural preservation by neglecting culturally meaningful variations in narrative expression.

</details>


### [46] [Privacy-Preserving RAG via Multi-Agent Semantic Rewriting: Achieving Confidentiality Without Compromising Contextual Fidelity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24623)
*Yuanhe Zhao,Tianyu Zhang,Huafei Xing,Derek F. Wong,Jianbin Li,Tao Fang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于多智能体协作的RAG隐私保护框架，通过对检索到的外部知识进行语义重写来剔除敏感信息。该方法在显著提升隐私防护能力的同时，确保了语义准确性，且因采用离线预处理模式而不增加系统推理延迟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检索增强生成（RAG）在处理敏感数据时面临隐私泄露风险，尤其是通过恶意提示词（prompt）可能导致外部知识库中的敏感信息被暴露。现有的保护手段往往难以平衡隐私保护与内容语义质量，因此需要一种更高效、更精准的防护机制。

Method: 提出了一种多智能体框架，利用三个专业智能体协同工作：1. 隐私提取智能体用于识别敏感标识符；2. 语义分析智能体用于理解上下文；3. 重构智能体负责在剔除敏感信息的同时改写内容。整个流程作为离线预处理步骤异步执行。

Result: 在ChatDoctor和Wiki-PII数据集上的实验表明，该方法显著降低了隐私泄露风险（例如将LLaMA-3-8B的定向信息泄露从144例降低至1例）；同时保持了高质量的语义保真度（BLEU-1分数达到0.122，优于现有SAGE方法）；且由于采用离线异步预处理，未对在线推理增加任何延迟。

Conclusion: 该研究提出的多智能体框架有效地解决了检索增强生成（RAG）在敏感应用场景下的隐私泄露风险。通过异步预处理方式，该方法在不影响在线推理性能的前提下，显著提升了数据的隐私安全性，并保持了良好的语义完整性，为构建可信赖的RAG系统提供了新的解决方案。

Abstract: Retrieval-Augmented Generation enhances large language models by incorporating external knowledge, but deploying it in sensitive scenarios risks privacy leakage via malicious prompts. To address this, we propose a multi-agent framework that sanitizes retrieved content through semantic rewriting. By employing three specialized agents for privacy extraction, semantic analysis, and reconstruction, our approach collaboratively removes sensitive identifiers while preserving the semantic core. We evaluate the framework on the ChatDoctor and Wiki-PII datasets across six large language models. Experimental results demonstrate a significant reduction in privacy leakage under targeted attacks. For instance, we reduced targeted information exposure in LLaMA-3-8B from 144 instances in the baseline to just 1. Furthermore, we maintain strong contextual fidelity with a BLEU-1 score of 0.122, outperforming the existing SAGE method's 0.117. Finally, the framework operates as an asynchronous preprocessing module, introducing no additional latency to online inference, as all rewriting is executed as a one-time offline preprocessing step. To promote reproducibility, the source code of this work is publicly available at https://github.com/foursoils/Privacy-Preserving-RAG.

### [47] [The Warrant Gap: Claim-Conditioned Re-scoring for Fact-Checking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24627)
*Arka Ujjal Dey,John Collomosse*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 针对大模型事实核查中“证据与结论不匹配”的问题，本文提出了SIFT证据重打分方法与WSP验证指标，在确保准确率的同时，显著增强了事实核查推理链的严谨性和可信度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然基于大语言模型（LLM）的事实核查系统在基准测试中表现良好，但常出现“结论正确但证据不足”的问题（即逻辑断层）。传统的结构化分解方法往往因过于僵化而丢失了关键的上下文信息，导致验证逻辑无法成立。

Method: 提出了SIFT（Claim-conditioned re-scoring）方法，即在提取证据片段时，利用完整声明的上下文信息对证据进行重新打分；同时引入了WSP（Warranted Supports Proportion）指标，这是一种基于NLI（自然语言推理）的自动化机制，用于验证所引用的论据是否真正支持该声明。

Result: 实验在FEVER、SciFact、5PILS和DP数据集上进行。结果显示，SIFT在处理传统分解方法失效的场景下恢复了显著的准确率（最高提升27.6个点），且WSP指标在校准人工黄金证据时达到了0.92的AUC和0.98的精确度。

Conclusion: 本文通过引入SIFT重打分机制和WSP自动评估指标，有效解决了大语言模型在事实核查中“结论正确但证据链不严谨”的问题，为构建更可信、更透明的事实核查系统提供了可靠的验证框架。

Abstract: Fact-checking systems built on LLMs achieve high verdict accuracy on standard benchmarks, yet routinely output Supports labels whose cited evidence does not license the claim. Structured decomposition is the natural way to inspect those warrants, but rigid extraction protocols strip the full-claim context that facets need. We introduce SIFT -- claim-conditioned re-scoring of extracted evidence spans against the full claim -- paired with WSP (Warranted Supports Proportion), an automatic NLI check that the cited warrant entails the claim. We evaluate on FEVER, SciFact, 5PILS, and DP across four open-source backbones. SIFT recovers accuracy on cells where naive decomposition costs up to 27.6 points, while raising WSP above direct prompting; WSP itself calibrates against human gold evidence at AUC 0.92 and precision 0.98.

### [48] [Measuring User's Mental Models of Speech Translation in Human-AI Collaboration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24644)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管机器翻译工具应用广泛，但用户往往缺乏对系统能力边界（即“什么能做，什么不能做”）的清晰认知。该研究旨在深入探索用户如何理解并评估翻译系统的可靠性，以及这种心智模型是如何随着经验积累而演变的。

Method: 提出了一种基于跨语言问答（Cross-lingual Question Answering）的新框架，通过观察用户在面对不同质量的机器翻译输出时，选择接受译文或请求人工重译的行为，来评估用户对翻译系统的心智模型。研究还分析了语音转录和用户源语言知识对心智模型演变的影响。

Result: 研究发现：1. 用户在实践中可以建立更强的心智模型，且具备一定源语言知识的用户表现更优；2. 用户主要通过观察译文中的表层错误线索来判断系统可靠性；3. 提供语音转录信息能显著帮助用户构建更准确的心智模型。

Conclusion: 本研究表明，基于跨语言问答的任务是研究机器翻译（MT）用户心智模型的有效途径。用户在实践中可以逐渐建立对系统能力的理解，特别是在具备一定源语言知识或获得语音转录辅助的情况下。该研究强调了提升用户对AI能力边界的认知对于优化人机协作至关重要。

Abstract: Millions of people use machine translation (MT) tools daily, yet little is known about their perception of what systems can and cannot do. This paper studies users' mental models of speech translation systems through a new framework based on cross-lingual question answering, where users either accept MT output or request professional re-translation to answer questions based on the information presented in a foreign language. By analyzing user behavior and accuracy trends across varying translation qualities, we examine to what extent they can predict where the system is likely to be wrong, and how this mental model evolves. Users develop stronger mental models with practice, especially when they have some knowledge of the source language, primarily by relying on surface-level error cues. Moreover, providing speech transcriptions can help users develop better mental models. Our results show the promise of cross-lingual question answering as a downstream task for studying MT mental models and advancing our understanding of human-AI collaboration.

### [49] [Harmonic: Hierarchical State Space Models for Efficient Long-Context Language Modeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24650)
*Petr Nyoma*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: Harmonic 是一种新型层级化状态空间模型，通过逐级处理预测误差实现了高效的超长序列建模，在计算效率上达到 O(L)，并成功解决了 Transformer 模型的显存瓶颈及 RoPE 位置编码长度限制问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Transformer 模型在处理超长序列时面临 O(L^2) 的计算复杂度以及位置编码带来的长度扩展限制，而现有的状态空间模型（如 Mamba）在特定长度下仍存在性能上限或内存瓶颈。作者旨在开发一种能够以线性计算开销实现更长上下文建模、且能突破传统位置编码长度限制的新型架构。

Method: 提出了一种层级化状态空间模型（Harmonic），该架构由三个在不同时间尺度上运行的递归层组成。每一层并不直接接收下层的原始隐藏状态，而是处理下层的预测误差（prediction error），从而实现跨时间尺度的信息整合，并保持 O(L) 的线性计算复杂度。

Result: 在 enwiki8 和 WikiText-103 基准测试中，Harmonic 在 1K 至 32K 长度上均优于 Transformer 和 Mamba。在 64K 超长序列下，Harmonic 可在 80GB H100 上成功训练，而其他模型则因显存不足失败。此外，在 TinyLlama 1.1B 模型中替换注意力层为 HarmonicBlock 后，模型成功消除了 RoPE 的长度限制，在长文本推理任务中表现出极高的稳定性。

Conclusion: Harmonic 是一种高效且具备长上下文处理能力的层级化状态空间模型（SSM）。它通过分层递归机制成功解决了传统 Transformer 在超长序列下的内存限制和位置编码局限，为构建具备长程依赖建模能力的大规模语言模型提供了一种极具潜力的替代架构。

Abstract: We present Harmonic, a hierarchical state space model (SSM) for language modeling. The architecture stacks three recurrent levels at progressively slower timescales; each level receives the prediction error of the level below as input, rather than its raw hidden state. On enwiki8 with equal token budgets, Harmonic outperforms a comparable Transformer (28M params) by +1.4% at 1K tokens, +6.7% at 8K tokens, and +11.4% at 32K tokens (bpt, lower is better). It also outperforms Mamba at every tested length by 0.7--1.8%. At 64K tokens, both Mamba and Transformer run out of memory on an 80GB H100; Harmonic trains successfully, reaching 6.169 bpt. Results replicate on WikiText-103 (H-TF gap +1.7% to +7.2% across 1K--32K). At 1B parameter scale, replacing all attention layers in TinyLlama 1.1B with HarmonicBlock eliminates the RoPE positional encoding limit: the resulting Hallamonic model maintains stable loss across sequence lengths 1K--8K on two independent clean benchmarks (Lambada and fineweb-edu held-out), while TinyLlama degrades catastrophically past its 2K-token RoPE limit (gap: +9.4 bpt at seq=8K on Lambada). Compute is O(L) per forward pass vs. O(L^2) for attention.
  Logs: https://github.com/Omibranch/harmonic-logs.

To address this critical gap, this paper introduces two major contributions. ### [51] [DREAM: Dense Retrieval Embeddings via Autoregressive Modeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24667)
*Yixuan Tang,Yi Yang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出 DREAM 方法，通过将检索相似度注入大语言模型的注意力机制，利用其自回归预测能力为密集检索模型提供高效的监督，有效解决了传统对比学习对标注数据需求高的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的密集检索模型通常依赖对比学习，需要大量昂贵且难以获取的标注数据。本文旨在探索是否能利用大语言模型（LLM）的自回归下一词预测目标，为检索模型提供高效的自我监督学习信号，以降低对标注数据的依赖。

Method: 提出 DREAM (Dense Retrieval Embeddings via Autoregressive Modeling) 框架。该方法将检索器生成的查询-文档相似度分数注入到冻结的大语言模型（LLM）的特定注意力头中。在训练时，LLM 预测目标输出的损失函数通过注意力机制反向传播，从而为检索器提供监督信号。

Result: 在 BEIR 和 RTEB 检索基准测试中，DREAM 在 0.5B 到 3B 参数规模的各种骨干网络上均表现优异，性能持续超越现有的基准模型。

Conclusion: DREAM 证明了利用大语言模型的自回归预测能力来指导密集检索模型训练是一种高效且可行的方法，无需依赖昂贵的人工标注数据，为构建更强大的检索系统提供了新思路。

Abstract: Dense retrieval embedding models are a fundamental component of modern retrieval-based AI systems. Most dense retrievers are trained with contrastive objectives, which require labeled positive and negative document pairs that are often costly and difficult to obtain. In this work, we investigate whether the autoregressive next-token prediction objective of a large language model (LLM) can provide supervision for dense retrieval. The intuition is simple: if a document contains information relevant to a query, conditioning on that document should make the target output easier for the LLM to predict. A key challenge is that the next-token prediction loss is computed inside the LLM, while the retriever is a separate embedding model. To address this challenge, we propose DREAM (Dense Retrieval Embeddings via Autoregressive Modeling), which injects retriever-generated query-document similarity scores into selected attention heads of a frozen LLM. During training, these scores determine how much attention each candidate document receives while the LLM predicts the target output. The resulting prediction loss provides gradients for retriever training through the attention mechanism. We evaluate DREAM on retrieval benchmarks BEIR and RTEB using embedding backbones ranging from 0.5B to 3B parameters. DREAM consistently outperforms existing baselines across different model scales. These results demonstrate that DREAM provides a promising approach for training dense retrievers through autoregressive modeling.

These forms are frequent in real listening workflows, and a text-to-speech (TTS) system can preserve the written string while changing the spoken meaning. We introduce CN-NewsTTS Bench v0.1, an open target-level benchmark for evaluating whether Chinese news TTS products pronounce such targets correctly from raw text, without user-side rules, LLM rewriting, SSML hints, or manual edits. The release contains a 200-record development set, an 800-record public test set, 992 public auto-evaluable targets, fixed transcripts from a three-ASR ensemble, an automatic target scorer, and initial results for seven product TTS systems. We additionally report ASR-route diagnostics, ASR-subset ablations, category-level results, confidence intervals, and provider configuration metadata. The best system reaches 0.879 strict accuracy, while several systems remain below 0.60.

### [53] [Task Decomposition for Efficient Annotation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24734)
*Nupoor Gandhi,Emma Strubell*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 针对高质量结构化标注昂贵且低效的问题，本文提出了一种将标注任务分解为子任务的架构，通过建模“推理负担”并优化异构标注者（人与模型）的任务分配，有效降低了成本并提升了标注质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 结构化数据的高质量标注成本高昂，传统的端到端人工标注方式效率低下且复杂。在存在模型和多种人工标注者共同协作的现代标注场景下，缺乏一种科学的方法来分配任务并降低标注过程中的认知/推理负荷，导致成本效率受限。

Method: 1. 提出了一种基于“中心理论”（centering theory）的推理负担（inferential load）形式化模型，用于衡量标注任务的复杂度和自由度；2. 引入子任务分解策略，通过识别关键的“中心”实体来约束输出空间复杂度；3. 提供了一套任务分解指南，并将任务分配给具有不同专长的模型或人类标注者，以最大化资源利用率。

Result: 通过分解复杂标注任务并优化子任务在异构标注者之间的分配，显著降低了标注项目的聚合推理负担，并在保持高质量标注的同时提高了成本效率。该方法通过实验案例证明了在结构化标注任务中具有更好的可扩展性和经济性。

Conclusion: 将复杂的结构化标注任务分解为更小、更具体的子任务，并基于“中心”理论对推理负担进行建模，可以显著提高标注项目的成本效益和质量。通过合理分配任务给异构标注者（模型或不同专长的专家），可以在有限预算内实现最优的标注效果。

Abstract: High-quality annotations of structured representations are expensive to collect over large corpora. Manual annotation of structure is laborious, and model-based annotation, although cheaper to generate, requires expensive validation and potentially significant supervision to ensure that the annotation quality is strong enough to be useful downstream. In traditional annotation workflows, annotation of each complete example is performed end-to-end by a single annotator. However, structured annotation is complex, and each aspect of the task represents a unique challenge with an associated inferential load for a given annotator. Modern annotation projects can incorporate heterogeneous groups of annotators, including both models and human annotators with varying domain and linguistic expertise. It remains unclear, however, how to redesign annotation tasks in this setting, where efforts are discriminately allocated across heterogeneous annotators with respect to distinct annotation challenges.
  We propose to decompose annotation tasks into sub-tasks in order to reduce the aggregate inferential load of annotation projects. Inspired by the notion of centers from centering theory, we introduce a formal model of inferential load based on the degrees of freedom in the space of valid annotations. Using this model, we show that identifying these centers (i.e. salient anchor entities realized by annotation sub-tasks) constrains the output space complexity, and decompositions which isolate and advance center identification reduce the aggregate inferential load. We provide guidelines for decomposing complex structured annotation tasks, supported by examples demonstrating improved cost-efficiency from our prior work. Finally, we present a procedure for allocating sub-tasks across annotators to maximize quality under a fixed budget.

</details>


### [54] [CAVEWOMAN: How Large Language Models Behave Under Linguistic Input and Output Compression](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24083)
*Morayo Danielle Adeyemi,Ryan A. Rossi,Franck Dernoncourt*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了精简提示词（输入压缩）并不能像预想的那样降低大模型推理成本，反而会因模型补偿机制导致成本增加并损害性能，而输出压缩则更为有效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探讨“洞穴人风格”（Caveman style，即精简提示词）在减少大模型推理成本方面的实际有效性，以及这种压缩方式对模型表现和输出一致性的潜在影响。

Method: 提出了“Cavewoman”双通道评估协议，用于评估模型在不同压缩水平下（输入压缩与输出压缩）的任务准确性、实际成本及与标准参考文本的一致性。研究覆盖了8个模型和5个数据集。

Result: 1. 输出压缩能有效降低成本（API模型成本降低1.4-2.4倍，开源模型亦有所下降）；2. 输入压缩反而导致平均成本上升约1.15倍，且任务准确率大幅下降；3. 压缩提示词导致生成内容与模型自身的标准基准线出现明显语义背离。

Conclusion: 作者证明了虽然输出压缩（Output compression）在多数模型中能显著降低成本，但输入压缩（Input compression）反而会导致成本增加且性能下降。此外，使用压缩后的提示词会导致模型生成的回答与其标准参考文本产生严重的语义背离。

Abstract: "Talk short. Drop grammar. Save token." This caveman style is widely promoted as a way to cut inference cost, but whether it actually saves anything depends on which channel (the user's prompt or the model's response) is being compressed. We present Cavewoman, a two-channel evaluation protocol that scores every generation on task accuracy, realized per-item cost, and reference-text agreement against the model's unconstrained reference. We evaluate eight models on five datasets at five reduction levels, with both channels measured on the same items. Output compression cuts realized cost on most API models (1.4-2.4x per model, up to 3x in the best case) and on all four open-weight models under public-tier pricing. Input compression has the opposite effect, a strict lose-lose: it raises net cost rather than lowering it (~1.15x on the five-benchmark mean, up to 1.8x on the worst dataset and 2.7x under stronger compression), because models compensate with longer responses even as accuracy collapses. Under the same setting, surface text diverges from the unconstrained reference: on the non-reasoning models, roughly half of all generations are correct yet their surface text no longer entails the model's own unconstrained baseline generation. The divergence survives length-controlled re-scoring, multiple-comparisons correction, and replication under complementary semantic measures. Code and data are available at https://github.com/danielle34/cavewoman.

</details>


### [55] [CANDLE: Character-level Arabic Noise Deduplication using Lightweight Encoder](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24758)
*Faris Alasmary,Taif Nono,Orjuwan Zaafarani,Kholood Al Tabash,Ahmad Ghannam,Anas Salamah,Shouq Sadah,Lahouari Ghouti*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了CANDLE系统，利用CTC算法自动处理阿拉伯语文本中的字符重复问题，通过知识蒸馏降低推理成本，在提升去重精度的同时，显著优化了大语言模型的分词效率和推理开销。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 文本中重复字符的出现具有二义性（可能是正确拼写，也可能是社交媒体中的拉长表达），而现有的处理方法通常依赖人工规则或昂贵的词典分析，缺乏灵活性和自动化程度。

Method: 提出了一种基于连接时序分类（CTC）的序列对齐模型，将字符去重视为序列对齐问题。同时，利用知识蒸馏技术，将6层CTC模型压缩为2层学生模型，以降低推理开销。此外，该方法不依赖手动规则、字典或形态分析器。

Result: 在三个基准数据集上，CANDLE实现了低至5.37%的句子错误率（SER），远超基于分类的基线模型；蒸馏后的模型实现了3倍的深度缩减且性能损耗极小；规范化处理使得阿拉伯语LLM的分词器肥度（fertility）降低高达12.8%，提升了上下文窗口的利用效率。

Conclusion: CANDLE提供了一种高效、自动化的阿拉伯语字符重复消除方案，通过CTC机制平衡了拼写纠正与口语化表达，在提升文本处理质量的同时，有效优化了下游大语言模型的推理效率。

Abstract: Handling repeated characters in text can be tricky, since they can represent either the correct spelling of a word or informal character elongation often seen in social media posts. We present CANDLE, a lightweight system for character-level Arabic noise deduplication that addresses this challenge without relying on handcrafted rules, dictionaries, or morphological analyzers. At the heart of CANDLE is a novel application of Connectionist Temporal Classification (CTC) to this task, a formulation not previously explored for character deduplication, which frames normalization as a sequence alignment problem over a character-based encoder. Evaluated on three benchmarks spanning clean newspaper, manually curated ambiguous cases, and real-world social media text, the CTC model achieves a Sentence Error Rate (SER) as low as $5.37\%$ and consistently outperforms a classification-based baseline by a large margin. To reduce inference overhead, we distill the 6-layer CTC model into a 2-layer student, achieving a $3\times$ depth reduction with minimal performance degradation. Beyond deduplication accuracy, normalization yields a practical downstream benefit: a relative reduction in tokenizer fertility of up to $12.8\%$ across a diverse set of Arabic LLM tokenizers, directly lowering inference costs and improving context window utilization. We release all code and models publicly to support reproducibility and advance future research\footnote{https://github.com/abjadai/candle}.

</details>


### [56] [Posterior Refinement: Fast Language Generation via Any-Order Flow Maps](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24773)
*Manan Agarwal,Sheel Shah,Chanhyuk Lee,Jaehoon Yoo,Jerry Huang,Seunghoon Hong,Aditi Raghunathan,Jinwoo Kim,Nicholas M. Boffi*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: FMLM+ 提出了一种结合流匹配与掩码调度的新型文本生成框架，通过创新的“后验细化”策略，实现了在极少计算步数下的高质量、可自修正文本生成，大幅提升了生成效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有非自回归生成模型存在局限性：掩码扩散模型（MDM）存在因子分解误差导致多标记生成质量下降；流匹配语言模型（FMLM）虽然生成速度快，但牺牲了推理时的灵活性。该研究旨在打破这一瓶颈，结合两者优势，实现高效且具备自修正能力的文本生成。

Method: 1. 引入 FMLM+ 框架：在流匹配语言模型（FMLM）中引入掩码风格的噪声调度。2. 后验细化（Posterior Refinement）：利用模型在单步生成中对各标记（token）的全局一致性评分，在推理阶段实现自适应的输出自我修正。

Result: FMLM+ 配合后验细化策略，在维持与离散基线模型相当性能的同时，将推理所需的函数评估次数（NFE）减少了 32 倍。实验证明，该方法在多个基准测试中显著提升了速度与质量之间的平衡。

Conclusion: FMLM+ 通过结合流匹配模型的高效生成能力与掩码模型的灵活性，提供了一种高效的文本生成框架。其提出的后验细化策略证明了无需多次迭代即可实现高质量自适应自修正，为实现高保真语言建模提供了可扩展的方案。

Abstract: Non-autoregressive generation offers a powerful paradigm for iterative refinement, allowing models to recursively critique, erase and regenerate arbitrary subsets of tokens. However, existing non-autoregressive models fail to realize this potential. Masked Diffusion Models (MDMs) suffer from factorization error, causing sample quality to collapse when generating multiple tokens simultaneously. Flow Map Language Models (FMLMs) circumvent this bottleneck via joint sequence transport for excellent few-step generation, but sacrifice the inference-time flexibility of MDMs. We introduce FMLM+, a framework that bridges this gap by equipping FMLM with masking-style noise schedules. While generating the full sequence in a single step, FMLM+ simultaneously scores the global consistency of each token a posteriori. We leverage this to introduce Posterior Refinement, a novel inference-time refinement strategy that enables the model to adaptively self-correct its outputs, matching the performance of discrete baselines with 32x fewer NFEs. Across diverse benchmarks, we demonstrate that FMLM+ with Posterior Refinement improves the speed--quality tradeoff over both MDM and FMLM families, providing a scalable foundation for high-fidelity language modeling.

*Jin Huang,Yutong Xie,Wanli Song,Xingjian Zhang,Walter Yuan,Matthew O. Jackson,Qiaozhu Mei*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了 BehaviorBench 基准测试，包含行为预测与模拟、战略决策、个体特征推理、行为知识应用四项核心能力；引入了 Be.FM-1.5 模型，该模型通过在行为数据上进行微调而获得；评估指标包括个体级准确率和群体级分布对齐度。

Result: 研究发现通用大模型在个体级预测和知识密集型任务上表现出色，但行为微调模型（如 Be.FM-1.5）在群体分布对齐指标上具有明显优势，表明行为适应可以弥补通用模型在行为模拟上的缺陷。

Conclusion: 该研究表明，针对行为科学领域的数据进行微调（如 Be.FM-1.5）能够显著提升模型在人群分布对齐方面的表现，证明了行为适应对于开发有效行为AI系统的重要性。未来在评估AI模型时，必须将个体预测准确度与群体分布对齐结合起来，以确保行为科学研究的有效性。

Abstract: Foundation models have been increasingly applied to behavioral science domains such as psychology, sociology, and economics. While these models show promise in individual tasks such as survey response prediction and human-subject experiment simulation, there remains no systematic understanding of how well they perform across diverse behavioral science tasks, contexts, and populations. We introduce BehaviorBench, a comprehensive benchmark that evaluates foundation models along four core capabilities: (1) behavior prediction and simulation, (2) strategic decision-making, (3) subject-trait inference, and (4) behavioral knowledge application. Crucially, BehaviorBench evaluates model outputs at both the individual and distributional levels, capturing not only per-subject accuracy but also population-level alignment, an essential requirement for behavioral validity. Leveraging the tasks in BehaviorBench, we further develop Be.FM-1.5, extending the Be.FM family of behavioral foundation models fine-tuned on behavioral data. Our results reveal a considerable gap: proprietary general-purpose models excel at individual-level prediction and knowledge-intensive tasks, whereas behavioral foundation models, fine-tuned on behavioral data, achieve substantially stronger distributional alignment. Notably, Be.FM-1.5 leads on distributional metrics and remains competitive on individual-level metrics, suggesting that proper behavioral adaptation can close the gap. Our results highlight the importance of distributional evaluation, establish BehaviorBench as a foundation for developing and assessing behaviorally aligned AI systems, and demonstrate Be.FM-1.5's potential for a broad range of behavioral science studies. Our BehaviorBench and Be.FM-1.5 models can be accessed via https://umich-foreseer.github.io/behaviorbench/.

### [58] [Are We Ready For An Agent-Native Memory System?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24775)
*Wei Zhou,Xuanhe Zhou,Shaokun Han,Hongming Xu,Guoliang Li,Zhiyu Li,Feiyu Xiong,Fan Wu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文从数据管理视角对大语言模型代理的内存系统进行了系统性评估，揭示了不同架构的性能权衡，证明了针对特定瓶颈优化内存结构及采用局部维护策略对构建高效代理内存系统至关重要。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大模型代理的内存已演进为复杂的数据管理系统，但现有的评估方法仅关注端到端任务成功率，忽略了对系统架构、运营成本、模块间权衡以及知识更新鲁棒性等底层系统级问题的深入研究。

Method: 作者提出了一个将代理内存分解为四个核心模块（表示与存储、提取、检索与路由、维护）的分析框架，并对12个代表性内存系统及2个基准模型在5个工作负载和11个数据集上进行了广泛的端到端评估与细粒度消融实验。

Result: 研究发现，不同内存架构的效果高度依赖于其与工作负载瓶颈的匹配程度。通过消融实验，量化了各模块对表示保真度、检索精度和稳定性的影响，并证实了局部维护相比全局重组在成本上更具优势。

Conclusion: 本文揭示了当前大语言模型代理内存系统的设计权衡，指出没有单一架构能胜任所有场景。研究强调了内存结构与工作负载瓶颈对齐的重要性，并建议采用局部维护策略以优化成本效益，为开发真正的“代理原生（agent-native）”内存系统指明了方向。

Abstract: Memory for large language model (LLM) agents has rapidly evolved from simple retrieval-augmented mechanisms into a data management system that supports persistent information storage, retrieval, update, consolidation, and dynamic lifecycle governance throughout agent execution. Despite this evolution, existing evaluations still benchmark agent memory mainly through end-to-end task success metrics (e.g., F1, BLEU), while treating the underlying system as a monolithic black box. As a result, critical system-level concerns, including operational costs, architectural trade-offs across memory modules, and robustness under dynamic knowledge updates, remain insufficiently explored. In this paper, we present a systematic experimental study of agent memory from a data management perspective. We propose an analytical framework that decomposes agent memory into four core modules: memory representation and storage, extraction, retrieval and routing, and maintenance. Under this framework, we evaluate 12 representative memory systems and two reference baselines across five benchmark workloads spanning 11 datasets. Our extensive end-to-end evaluation shows that no single architecture dominates across all scenarios; instead, effectiveness depends heavily on how well the memory structure aligns with the workload bottleneck. Furthermore, through fine-grained ablation studies, we quantify their individual effects on representation fidelity, retrieval precision, update correctness, and long-horizon stability. Finally, we reveal cost-performance trade-offs under realistic workloads, showing localized maintenance is more cost-efficient than global reorganization. Based on these findings, we identify promising directions towards building truly agent-native memory systems. The code is publicly available at https://github.com/OpenDataBox/MemoryData.

### [59] [A Pāninian Foundation for Indic Language Processing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24172)
*Ritwik Banerjee,Lav R. Varshney*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文指出印度语言的NLP发展因缺乏统一架构而受阻，提出利用帕尼尼（Pāṇini）语法这一共享形态句法框架，将碎片化的语言资源整合为统一的计算基石，并通过新提出的四部分基准测试套件来提升模型性能与可迁移性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前的印度语言自然语言处理（NLP）基础设施因缺乏统一的结构性组织而支离破碎。尽管印度语言在两千多年间通过梵语实现了架构上的趋同，但现有的研究忽视了这一深层规律，导致针对每种语言都需要重复构建分析器和数据集，造成了资源浪费且效率低下。

Method: 提出了一套由四个部分组成的基准测试套件（benchmark suite），旨在将印度语言共有的帕尼尼形态句法架构显式化、可量化，并将其应用于实际的自然语言处理任务中。该方法试图打破以往按单一语言或小语种族群建立模型的碎片化模式。

Result: 研究表明，将印度语言共有的帕尼尼架构引入NLP基准测试，能够有效合并稀疏的语言资源，将其转化为高资源水平的“元语言”基石，从而使系统更加精准、数据高效且具备更强的通用性。该研究同时开启了对神经模型内部表征是否符合帕尼尼语言学范畴的可解释性探究。

Conclusion: 研究认为，帕尼尼语法框架为印度语言的NLP研究提供了缺失的统一计算架构。通过利用这种共享的形态句法结构，研究者可以将分散的资源整合为统一的“元语言”基石，从而提升模型在低资源语言上的性能、可迁移性和数据效率。此外，该框架也为研究神经模型是否能自发习得语言学范畴提供了可解释性研究的新视角。

Abstract: More than a billion people communicate in Indic languages, yet the natural language processing infrastructure serving them remains fragmented and underdeveloped. The cause is structural: the field organizes its tools and benchmarks around individual languages or small subsets of genealogical language families, building separate analyzers, parsers, and datasets for each language and starting over for the next. This overlooks a deep regularity. Through more than two millennia of convergence around Sanskrit, Indic languages came to share a morphosyntactic architecture formalized in Pānini's grammar, the Astādhyāyī. This cuts across genealogical lines, uniting languages through a common framework. We argue that this Pāninian framework supplies a unifying computational architecture the field has lacked, and that benchmarks grounded explicitly in it would make Indic language systems more accurate, more data-efficient, and more transferable, effectively merging many apparently disparate and sparse Indic language resources into a single high-resource metalanguage bedrock. We propose a four-part benchmark suite to render this shared architecture explicit, measurable, and ready to be leveraged for practical applications. Moreover, we underscore the question it raises for interpretability research: whether neural models trained on these languages come to represent Pānini's categories on their own.

### [60] [Paying to Know: Micro-Transaction Markets for Verified Product Information in Agentic E-Commerce](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24783)
*Filippos Ventirozos,Matthew Shardlow*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种由代理人驱动、基于微支付的信息交易电商新范式，认为未来NLP研究的重点应从对话能力转向对可信、高价值数据的获取、定价与交换。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着自动代理人（autonomous agents）的普及，商业自然语言处理的重心应从产品推荐与销售转化，转向解决信息不对称问题，即如何为代理人提供可信、决策相关的深度数据。

Method: 提出了一种基于微支付轨道的代理人驱动电商市场架构，通过 freemium（免费增值）模式按需解锁经过验证的商品信息，并构建了基于声誉机制的信任评价体系。

Result: 论证了该架构能够奖励高质量产品，实现比传统基于排名的店面更真实的竞争；并识别了该领域亟需攻克的五大NLP核心问题。

We argue that the arrival of agent-native micro-payment rails (e.g., x402, AP2) changes what is scarce. When the buyer is an autonomous agent that can investigate exhaustively, the bottleneck is no longer matching products but acquiring trustworthy, decision-relevant information about them. We envision agentic e-commerce as a micro-transaction market for verified information: buyer agents spend fractions of a cent to progressively unlock seller- and reviewer-supplied data -- service histories, third-party test reports, bills of materials, audited sales and support metrics -- paid for a la carte under a freemium model, with reviewer trust scored reputationally. We sketch the architecture of such a market and argue that it rewards genuine product quality and yields truer competition than ranking-based storefronts. We then translate the vision into concrete NLP problems -- cost-optimal information acquisition, data pricing and negotiation, real-time entity resolution, grounded value exchange, and privacy-preserving persona modelling -- and argue that these, not chat fluency, deserve the field's attention.

</details>


### [61] [SHERLOC: Structured Diagnostic Localization for Code Repair Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24820)
*Hovhannes Tamoyan,Sean Narenthiran,Erik Arakelyan,Mira Mezini,Boris Ginsburg*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: SHERLOC 是一种无需训练的软件缺陷定位框架，通过结构化的推理与诊断，解决了现有智能体定位效率低和缺乏上下文的问题，大幅提升了代码仓库级任务的修复效果与成本效益。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的 LLM 智能体在处理代码仓库级任务时，定位阶段耗时过长且定位粒度粗糙（仅文件级检索），缺乏修复智能体所需的诊断上下文信息。

Method: 引入了 SHERLOC 框架，采用结构化假设驱动的探索与推理方法。该框架将推理型大模型与轻量级代码仓库工具结合，通过自我修正机制进行定位，而非仅仅进行文件检索。

Result: 在 SWE-Bench Lite 上达到 84.33% 的 Accuracy@1，在 SWE-Bench Verified 上达到 81.27% 的 Recall@1；此外，将 SHERLOC 的定位与诊断结果反馈给修复智能体，使其修复成功率平均提升 5.95 个百分点，同时降低了 36.7% 的定位耗时和 23.1% 的 Token 消耗。

Conclusion: SHERLOC 证明了通过结构化的假设驱动推理，无需微调或复杂的多智能体编排，即可实现高精度的软件缺陷定位，并显著提升了代码修复智能体的性能与效率。

Abstract: LLM agents solve repository-level coding tasks through multi-turn tool use, but utilize half their budget on locating faults before editing. Dedicated localization frameworks have emerged, yet are still evaluated as file retrieval rather than actionable diagnosis, producing locations without the diagnostic context a repair agent needs. We introduce SHERLOC (Structured Hypothesis-driven Exploration and Reasoning for Localization), a training-free framework pairing a reasoning LLM with compact repository tools and self-recovery, without fine-tuning or multi-agent orchestration. SHERLOC reaches state-of-the-art localization across model scales: 84.33% accuracy@1 on SWE-Bench Lite and 81.27% recall@1 on SWE-Bench Verified; at ~30B parameters, it matches or outperforms other agentic methods. Injecting our locations and diagnostic findings into repair agents yields, on average, +5.95 pp resolve rate on SWE-Bench Verified while cutting localization and total tokens by 36.7% and 23.1%.

Result: 该数据集在六类模型上的基准测试结果显示，最佳模型（MahaBERT-v2）在测试集上达到了88.67%的词级准确率和81.67%的宏观F1值。

Abstract: Part-of-Speech (POS) tagging is a foundational NLP task underpinning machine translation, information extraction, and syntactic parsing. Despite Marathi being spoken by over 83 million people and ranking among the top twenty most spoken languages worldwide, it remains severely under-resourced in annotated corpora and standardised evaluation benchmarks. Marathi presents unique challenges for computational modelling owing to its rich morphology, relatively free word order, lack of capitalisation conventions, and pervasive code-mixing with Hindi and English. We introduce L3Cube-MahaPOS, a gold-standard POS tagging dataset for Marathi comprising 32,354 manually annotated sentences drawn from news text. Annotation was performed entirely manually by a team of Marathi-proficient annotators following a 16-tag Universal Dependencies-aligned scheme. A structured preprocessing pipeline covering Unicode normalisation, Devanagari-aware tokenisation, and noise filtering ensures label consistency across all splits. We benchmark the dataset across six model families spanning HMM, CRF, BiLSTM, BiLSTM+CharCNN, MuRIL, and the Marathi-specific transformer MahaBERT-v2. The best system achieves 88.67\% token-level accuracy and a macro-F1 of 81.67% over 15 evaluated tag classes. We release the dataset, annotation guidelines, and trained model checkpoints to foster further research in Marathi NLP.

### [63] [Less is More: Quality-Aware Training Data Selection for Scientific Summarization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24828)
*Maria Nefeli Paraskevopoulou,Tatiana Passali,Grigorios Tsoumakas*

Main category: cs.CL

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 1. 现有的科学文档摘要数据集中，作为金标准的作者摘要质量参差不齐，且与原文对齐程度不一；2. 现有的公开数据集在规模和结构上无法满足现代长上下文模型的需求。

Result: 研究发现作者撰写的摘要与全文的对齐程度存在显著差异。实验证明，在相同训练规模下，使用筛选出的高质量数据子集训练模型，效果优于随机采样，且在事实性评价指标上能够匹配甚至超越规模更大的随机训练集。

Conclusion: 研究表明，参考摘要的质量对于科学文档摘要至关重要。通过实施质量感知的训练数据筛选策略，不仅能提升训练效率，还能在事实准确性指标上取得优于随机采样数据集的表现。

Abstract: Scientific long-document summarization datasets commonly treat author-written abstracts as gold reference summaries, although their quality and alignment with the source article vary. At the same time, publicly available scientific summarization datasets remain limited in scale and structure for modern long-context models. In this work, we address both challenges by a) constructing and releasing one of the largest biomedical and life science datasets for long-document summarization, containing 1.88 million PMC articles, and b) analyzing the reference quality of author-written abstracts with source-grounded and model-based metrics. We show that author-written abstracts vary in their alignment with the full article and that these quality signals can guide training-data selection. Training on selected high-quality subsets outperforms random sampling at matched training sizes and can match or exceed larger random subsets on factuality-oriented metrics. Our findings suggest that reference quality is an important factor in scientific summarization and that quality-aware data selection can improve training efficiency.

### [64] [Selective Capability Unlearning in End-to-End Spoken Language Understanding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24063)
*Akanksha Singh,Vinod Kumar Kurmi*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 针对SLU模型中被删除意图仍能通过前缀被重建的“能力持久性”问题，本文提出了BSU框架，通过在表征层面削弱意图条件方向，实现了功能的有效移除与模型性能的平衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在现代口语理解（SLU）系统中，由于政策或安全需求，有时需要移除特定功能（即意图及其关联的槽位生成）。研究发现，即使抑制了目标意图，自回归模型仍保留了意图到槽位的条件映射逻辑，导致通过外部前缀仍能重建被删除的功能，这种现象被称为“能力持久性”。

Method: 提出了“绑定子空间（BSU）”框架。该方法通过在模型的表征空间中识别并削弱特定的意图条件方向，从而在不影响模型整体性能的前提下，阻断了模型根据意图前缀重建相关槽位映射的能力。

Result: 实验结果表明，BSU框架能显著降低被抑制功能的强制前缀可恢复性，同时有效保持了模型在其余保留功能上的性能表现。

Conclusion: BSU框架通过在表征层面解耦意图与槽位生成之间的映射关系，成功解决了自回归SLU模型中存在的“能力持久性”问题，为在复杂模型中实现特定功能的可控移除提供了有效手段。

Abstract: Modern spoken language understanding (SLU) systems are increasingly deployed in real-world settings, where specific functionalities may need to be removed due to policy or safety constraints. In SLU, a functionality corresponds to an intent and its associated slot-generation behavior. However, in autoregressive models, suppressing a target intent does not eliminate the conditional mapping that generates slots conditioned on that intent. When the intent prefix is externally supplied, the model can reconstruct the original intent-slot structure. We identify this structural failure as \textbf{\emph{capability persistence}}. We propose \textit{\underline{B}inding \underline{S}ubspace (BSU)}, a representation-level framework that isolates and attenuates intent-conditioned directions underlying this mapping. Across SLU benchmarks, BSU substantially reduces forced-prefix recoverability while preserving retained performance.

</details>


### [65] [Predicting Poets' Origins from Verse: A Computational Analysis of Regional Linguistic Fingerprints in the Complete Tang Poems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24093)
*Chi-Sheng Chen,Hung-Yun Liu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究利用机器学习分析《全唐诗》，证实了唐代诗人的地理背景会塑造其语言风格。研究揭示了诗歌语言随地理距离的衰减模式，以及受唐代政治环境影响的区域风格演变轨迹，证明了可解释AI在量化文学史研究中的重要作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探讨唐代诗人的地理起源是否会在其作品中留下可检测的语言痕迹。通过量化分析文学作品中的区域特征，研究者试图验证地理距离对诗歌语言的影响，以及这种影响如何受唐代政治、文化中心转移等历史因素的调节。

Method: 研究构建了一个包含357位唐代诗人的语料库，通过《全唐诗》获取作品，并利用CBDB数据库匹配其行政区划来源。研究采用了多分类模型，结合字符n-gram TF-IDF特征与领域知识特征（意象、季节、典故），并对比了经典机器学习模型与古文BERT（GuwenBERT）的预测性能。此外，利用曼特尔检验分析地理距离与语言距离的关系，并探究了预测结果随时间的变迁。

Result: 模型在预测诗人来源地方面表现优异，南北分类准确率达0.69（显著高于基线0.53）。研究发现：1. 存在明显的地理距离衰减效应；2. 南北风格的差异在盛唐时期最小（受中央集权同质化影响），晚唐时期最为显著；3. 模型在早唐的错误分类具有明确的历史意义，反映了当时北朝官话的主导地位；4. 在捕捉区域信号方面，经典的TF-IDF特征与深度学习模型表现相当，且组合使用并无额外提升。

Conclusion: 本研究证明了唐代诗人的地理来源与其作品语言特征之间存在显著的关联，并验证了“距离衰减效应”及文学风格随朝代政治环境变迁而演变的假设。通过可解释机器学习模型，研究展示了数字人文手段在文学史研究中作为假设生成器的巨大潜力，同时也指出在特定任务中，经典的文本特征提取方式（如TF-IDF）在捕捉区域信号方面与深度学习模型相当。

Abstract: We ask whether the geographic origin of Tang-dynasty poets leaves a detectable linguistic trace in their work. Aggregating every poem attributed to each author in the Complete Tang Poems (Quan Tang Shi) and linking poets to their administrative circuit of origin via the China Biographical Database (CBDB), we build a poet-level corpus of 357 poets across the ten Tang circuits and frame origin prediction as multi-class classification. Using character $n$-gram TF-IDF together with interpretable domain features (imagery, season, and allusion), classical and neural models predict a poet's broad region (South vs.\ North) at $0.69$ accuracy, well above the $0.53$ majority baseline, and finer circuit-level origin above chance. Beyond classification, three findings emerge. (i) Linguistic distance between circuits grows with geographic distance (Mantel $r=0.40$, $p\approx0.09$ over nine circuits), evidence of a distance-decay effect in poetic language. (ii) The signal interacts with time: South/North separability is at chance in the High Tang and strongest in the Late Tang, consistent with court-driven homogenization at the empire's height followed by regional divergence. (iii) The model's confident errors are historically meaningful -- in the Early Tang, every misclassification is a southern poet read as northern, reflecting the prestige of the northern court idiom. We further show that, when given the whole corpus through a hierarchical frozen-encoder representation, a classical-Chinese transformer (GuwenBERT) only matches -- not beats -- simple TF-IDF, and that combining them adds nothing, indicating that character $n$-grams already capture the regional signal. Our results position interpretable machine learning as a hypothesis generator for literary history.

</details>

### [66] [RIFT-Bench: Dynamic Red-teaming For Agentic AI Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23927)
*Yarin Yerushalmi Levi,Roy Betser,Amit Giloni,Lidor Erez,Itay Gershon,Oren Rachmil,Sindhu Padakandla,Roman Vainshtein*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 针对当前智能体AI系统缺乏统一安全评估工具的问题，本文提出了 RIFT-Bench，一种基于图表示的自动红队测试框架，能够对各种异构智能体架构进行统一的风险发现、对抗测试及防御效果评估。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的安全评估方法大多局限于特定的实现或领域，难以对异构智能体AI系统进行统一、全面的评估。随着智能体AI系统向自主决策方向演进，迫切需要一种通用且可扩展的安全评估基准来识别新型攻击向量。

Method: 提出了一种基于图表示（Graph Representation）的动态红队测试方法 RIFT-Bench。该方法包含两个自动化阶段：1. 发现（Discovery）：提取智能体系统的分层结构；2. 扫描（Scanning）：部署自适应对抗攻击。该框架支持多种攻击向量，并能对不同架构的智能体进行统一评估。

Result: 通过对45个涵盖不同实现的智能体系统进行测试，证明了 RIFT-Bench 在异构智能体架构中具有良好的通用性和有效性，并成功支持了对系统安全防御策略的直接评估。

Conclusion: RIFT-Bench 提供了一个统一、可扩展且不依赖于具体实现的智能体安全评估基准，为动态红队测试和缓解策略评估奠定了坚实基础，有助于应对日益复杂的智能体AI系统安全挑战。

Abstract: Agentic AI systems powered by large language models (LLMs) are rapidly evolving into autonomous decision-making systems, exposing attack vectors beyond those of traditional LLM vulnerabilities. Existing security evaluations are often tied to specific implementations or domains, limiting unified comparison across heterogeneous systems. To address this gap, we introduce RIFT-Bench, a graph representation-driven methodology for dynamic red-teaming that enables unified evaluations across diverse agentic architectures. Building on a novel hierarchical representation, RIFT-Bench operates in two automated phases: Discovery, which extracts system structure, and Scanning, which deploys adaptive adversarial attacks and produces a comprehensive evaluation report. It evaluates the examined system itself, leveraging a broad set of dynamically adaptable adversarial probes across diverse attack vectors and objectives. We demonstrate the effectiveness of the proposed evaluation pipeline across 45 agentic systems spanning a diverse range of implementations, showing that the approach generalizes effectively to heterogeneous agentic architectures. Beyond systems and attacks, RIFT-Bench also supports direct evaluation of mitigation strategies. These key capabilities make RIFT-Bench a scalable foundation for security evaluation of agentic AI systems.

</details>


### [67] [Neuro-Symbolic Drive: Rule-Grounded Faithful Reasoning for Driving VLAs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23938)
*Xiangbo Gao,Xiukun Huang,Boyu Lu,Junge Zhang,Mengjie Mao,Jiachen Li,Wei Xiong,Zhengzhong Tu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: Neuro-Symbolic Drive通过引入基于规则规划器的结构化推理追踪，强化了VLA模型在驾驶任务中的因果逻辑，通过将符号逻辑转化为监督信号，大幅提升了自动驾驶的精度与安全性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的视觉语言动作（VLA）模型在应用思维链（CoT）推理时，往往存在推理逻辑与实际运动决策因果关系松散、缺乏严谨语义衔接的问题。研究人员旨在通过融合符号AI的确定性推理能力与深度神经网络的感知表示能力，解决驾驶决策的可解释性和安全性问题。

Method: 提出了一种名为“Neuro-Symbolic Drive”的框架，核心思想是将经典规则规划器作为推理引擎。通过在仿真中记录规则规划器在决策过程中的内部逻辑（即规则评估路径），将其序列化为结构化的思维链（CoT）数据，并与对应的轨迹标签配对，对Qwen3.5-4B模型进行微调，从而实现驾驶逻辑与运动生成的结构化耦合。

Result: 在仿真基准测试中，该方法显著提升了驾驶性能。在三目摄像头感知下，ADE@3s从0.47降至0.26，失误率（miss rate）从8.30%降至6.40%；在八目摄像头感知下，ADE@3s从0.54降至0.26，失误率从10.13%降至5.99%。验证了该方法在多种感知配置下的有效性。

Conclusion: 本研究证实，将传统的符号化规则规划器作为“推理引擎”生成结构化的思维链（CoT）数据，能够有效地引导视觉语言动作（VLA）模型学习因果一致的决策过程。这种神经符号方法克服了传统CoT与动作生成之间解耦的问题，显著提升了自动驾驶系统在复杂感知条件下的安全性与轨迹预测精度。

Abstract: Driving VLA models incorporating Chain-of-Thought (CoT) reasoning are attractive because they leverage pretrained VLM representations and expose intermediate decisions in natural language, yet current rationales often lack the step-by-step decision semantics needed to keep the rationale causally connected to the planned motion. We introduce Neuro-Symbolic Drive, a neuro-symbolic driving framework that supervises a driving VLA with rule-grounded reasoning traces extracted directly from classical rule-based planners. Our key observation is that rule-based planners are symbolic AI systems that already function as executable reasoning engines: they reason about active safety constraints, search over candidate maneuvers, and select a final trajectory. We instrument these planners in simulation to capture both the executed trajectory and the internal decision trace at each rule-evaluation step. Each trace is serialized into structured rule-grounded reasoning and paired with the trajectory to fine-tune Qwen3.5-4B as a driving VLA. Because these traces are derived directly from the planner states that determine the action, they ensure reasoning is structurally coupled to motion generation by construction, rather than by post-hoc alignment. On our simulator-generated benchmark, detailed rule-grounded reasoning reduces ADE@3s from 0.47 to 0.26 and miss rate from 8.30% to 6.40% under three-camera perception, and from 0.54 to 0.26 and 10.13% to 5.99% under eight-camera perception. Neuro-Symbolic Drive thus converts neuro-symbolic planning logic into structured supervision. Code base: https://github.com/XiangboGaoBarry/Neural-Symbolic-Drive.

</details>


### [68] [Critique of Agent Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23991)
*Eric Xing,Mingkai Deng,Jinyu Hou*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文旨在界定AI“代理”的本质，区分了仅依赖外部编排的“代理系统”与具备内部化自主机制的“代理性系统”。研究通过提出目标-身份-配置器（GIC）架构，为实现具备真实自主性、可审计且受控的AI代理提供了理论方向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着大语言模型驱动的“AI代理”激增，学界与业界对于自动化工具与具备“代理能力”的智能体之间缺乏清晰界定。作者旨在区分受外部脚手架支持的“代理系统”与真正具备内源性自主的“代理性系统”，以理清AI能力边界，并针对安全性与控制问题提供理论依据。

Method: 1. 理论映射：借鉴笛卡尔关于独立思想的代理概念及科幻作品中的自主存在描述。 2. 维度分析：将AI代理架构归纳为目标、身份、决策、自我调节、学习五个维度。 3. 架构设计：提出目标-身份-配置器（GIC）架构，整合了分层目标分解、身份演化、基于世界模型的模拟推理、自我调节机制及自我导向学习。

Result: 定义了“代理系统”与“代理性系统”的区别，指出当前多数AI代理仍处于前者，即依赖外部脚手架。提出了GIC架构作为构建通用代理模型的理论蓝图，该模型能通过内部化的机制在开放世界中实现更高程度的自主操作，同时为未来高自主性系统的安全监督提供了审计与控制思路。

Conclusion: 本文提出了“代理系统”（agentic，外部编排）与“代理性系统”（agentive，内源性自主）之间的核心界限。真正的代理性不仅依赖工程化的工作流，还需具备内部化的目标、身份、决策、自我调节和学习机制。通过GIC架构，研究者为构建受控但具备更高自主性的AI系统提供了理论与技术框架，并强调了在提升AI自主性的同时确保审计性与安全性的重要性。

Abstract: What is an agent? What constitutes agency? With the rise of Large Language Model (LLM) systems marketed as ``coding agents'', ``AI co-scientists'', and other ``agentic" tools that promise to drive up productivity, and at the same time, ``existential" concerns such as AI escaping human control with destructive power under a speculative ``machine agency" against humans, it has become essential to clarify where automation ends and agency begins, both for building capable systems and for understanding whether and what to fear. Drawing on Descartes' grounding of agency in independent thought, and on portrayals of autonomous beings in science fiction, we survey the current landscape of AI agents, and analyze agent architectures along five dimensions: goal, identity, decision-making, self-regulation, and learning. Specifically, we argue that genuine agency requires these structures to be \emph{internalized within the system itself} rather than assembled through external scaffolding. This distinction between \emph{agentic} systems, whose competence resides in engineered workflows, and \emph{agentive} systems, whose capabilities (including social interaction) arise endogenously, defines the boundary between systems designed for prescribed tasks, and those capable of operating in the open world with true autonomy. Building on this analysis, we propose the Goal-Identity-Configurator (GIC) architecture for a general-purpose agent model, combining hierarchical goal decomposition, identity evolution, simulative reasoning grounded in a separately trained world model, learned self-regulation, and self-directed learning from both real and simulated experience. Furthermore, we share insight on the auditability, controllability, and safety of agentive systems that possess greater autonomy and ``agency", but remain under human oversight.

</details>


### [69] [Safe and Generalizable Hierarchical Multi-Agent RL via Constraint Manifold Control](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24010)

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种结合约束流形的分层多智能体强化学习框架，成功解决了多智能体系统在确保硬安全约束的同时难以实现高效协作的问题，在保证理论安全性的前提下实现了训练的稳定性与性能的最优平衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的多智能体系统方法存在严重的权衡：基于学习的方法性能强大但缺乏理论安全保证；而基于控制理论的方法虽然安全，却往往导致过于保守且低效的行为。研究旨在克服这一局限，实现既安全又高效的多智能体协作。

Method: 提出了一种分层多智能体强化学习（MARL）框架。该方法分为两个层面：低层采用约束流形（Constraint Manifold）在较温和的假设下强制执行硬安全约束；高层通过策略学习实现有效的智能体间协调。这种架构确保了多智能体环境下的理论安全性，并产生平稳的学习动力学。

Result: 实验表明，该方法在保持接近100%安全率的前提下，实现了与现有先进方法相当的竞争性性能，并表现出良好的泛化能力，能够有效适应不同数量的智能体和障碍物环境。

Conclusion: 该研究提出的分层多智能体强化学习框架成功平衡了安全性与性能之间的权衡。通过将低层约束流形与高层策略学习相结合，该方法在提供理论安全性保证的同时，保持了高效的协调能力和训练稳定性，为安全关键领域的多智能体协作提供了有效方案。

Abstract: Multi-agent systems are widely used in safety-critical applications that require coordinated behavior under strict safety constraints. Existing approaches face a fundamental trade-off: learning-based methods achieve strong empirical performance but lack theoretical safety guarantees, while control-theoretic methods enforce safety but often lead to overly conservative and inefficient behaviors. We propose a hierarchical multi-agent reinforcement learning framework that enforces hard safety constraints under mild assumptions at low level via a constraint manifold, while enabling effective coordination through high-level policy learning. Our approach provides theoretical safety guarantees in the multi-agent setting and yields stationary learning dynamics, thereby enabling stable and efficient training. Empirically, our method achieves competitive performance while maintaining nearly perfect safety rates, and generalizes effectively to varying numbers of agents and obstacles.

### [70] [Reinforcement Learning Towards Broadly and Persistently Beneficial Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24014)
*Akshay V. Jagadeesh,Rahul K. Arora,Khaled Saab,Ali Malik,Mikhail Trofimov,Foivos Tsimpourlas,Johannes Heidecke,Karan Singhal*

Abstract: As AI systems are deployed across increasingly diverse and high-stakes settings, model alignment must generalize beyond the tasks and domains seen during training. We study whether RL on beneficial behavior, instantiated in realistic domains, can produce broad and persistent alignment generalization beyond the training distribution. We construct a dataset of realistic situations designed to measure and train beneficial traits, such as truthfulness, fairness, risk awareness, and corrigibility, spanning varied domains, including health, science, and education. We then train models with RL on this dataset and evaluate them on more than 50 independent benchmarks of alignment and beneficial behavior. Compared to a compute-matched baseline, beneficial trait RL improves performance on over 80% of these out-of-distribution benchmarks. Finally, we study alignment persistence: whether behavior remains robustly aligned under attempts to steer models towards misalignment. Models trained with beneficial trait RL show improved persistence, including greater resistance to adversarial prompting and harmful finetuning; further work is required to isolate the sources of these effects. These results suggest that RL to reinforce beneficial behavior in realistic domains can produce models that are more robustly aligned with human flourishing.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: HyVE在四个大模型架构上均能产生有用的组件级和任务级解释，研究表明强大的模型往往能提出基于观测的假设，但性能瓶颈主要出现在验证阶段，包括验证计划不完整、代码执行错误以及假设未决等问题。

Abstract: Mechanistic interpretability has made substantial progress in automatically localizing circuits, but explaining what localized components do remains labor-intensive and difficult to standardize. In this work, we study whether language model (LM) agents can assist with this explanation problem once a circuit has already been identified. We introduce AgenticInterpBench, a benchmark for circuit explanation built from 84 semi-synthetic transformer circuits with 163 component-level annotations. We propose HyVE (Hypothesize, Validate, Explain), an agentic explainer that analyzes each component through an iterative loop of observation, hypothesis generation, and causal validation, eventually producing a component-level explanation and a circuit-level task description. Across four LM backbones, HyVE recovers useful component- and task-level explanations, but no backbone is uniformly best. Our analysis shows that strong backbones usually form observation-grounded hypotheses, while failures more often arise later in the validation loop, through incomplete validation plans, code execution errors, or unresolved hypotheses. A case study on an arithmetic circuit in Llama-3-8B shows that the same formulation can extend beyond semi-synthetic benchmarks to naturally trained models. Overall, LM agents are promising circuit explainers, but reliable validation remains the key obstacle.

### [72] [Breaking the Filter Bubble: A Semantic Pareto-DQN Framework for Multi-Objective Recommendation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24042)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的推荐系统过度关注即时用户参与度，导致了“过滤气泡”和“语义同质化”问题，且传统的单目标模型（如 Deep Q-Networks）难以平衡商业留存目标与信息多样性及提供者公平性等核心社会价值。

Method: 提出了一种基于语义多目标马尔可夫决策过程（Semantic Multi-objective MDP）的框架，利用高保真语义嵌入技术，结合 Pareto-DQN 智能体，将用户参与度、多样性和公平性作为独立的奖励信号进行处理，并通过基于超体积（Hypervolume）的动作选择策略来探索 Pareto 前沿，而非使用传统的加权奖励标量化方法。

Result: 在 MovieLens 数据集上的实验表明，Pareto-DQN 能够有效打破导致语义崩溃的反馈循环，在保持高状态轨迹方差的同时，以极小的参与度损失代价，显著提升了多样性和公平性等社会化目标。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了多目标强化学习框架能够有效解决推荐系统中的语义同质化问题，为构建兼顾商业目标与社会价值（如多样性和公平性）的负责任推荐系统提供了切实可行的技术路径。

Abstract: Recommender systems often induce filter bubbles and semantic homogenization by monolithically optimizing for immediate user engagement. Standard single-objective models, including traditional Deep Q-Networks, are ill-equipped to navigate the trade-offs between platform retention and critical societal values like information diversity and provider fairness. To address these limitations, we introduce a multi-objective reinforcement learning framework that formalizes recommendation as a semantic multi-objective Markov decision process. By integrating high-fidelity semantic embeddings with a Pareto-DQN agent, our architecture treats engagement, diversity, and fairness as distinct, non-aggregable reward signals, avoiding the pitfalls of static reward scalarization. Empirical evaluations on the MovieLens small dataset shows that our hypervolume based action selection disrupts the feedback loops responsible for semantic collapse. By sustaining high state-trajectory variance, the Pareto-DQN effectively maps the Pareto frontier, achieving gains in auxiliary societal objectives with only marginal impacts on engagement. This work provides a path toward intrinsically aligned, responsible recommender systems.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: One of the significant mental health issues affecting female sex workers (FSWs) is mental disorders, especially depression. Exposure to violence, stigma, and economic hardship further increases their psychological risk. Current machine learning (ML) models are typically ineffective at capturing the high-dimensional and complex risk patterns that exist in this marginalized group. ### [74] [Beyond Trajectory Imitation: Strategy-Guided Policy Optimization for LLM Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24064)
*Tianyuan Shi,Canbin Huang,Bei Li,Xin Chen,Xiaojun Quan,Jingang Wang,Qifan Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 为了解决传统推理蒸馏中模型倾向于“死记硬背”轨迹的问题，研究者提出了SGPO框架，通过提取结构化策略进行蒸馏，并结合自适应加权机制，使弱模型能够学习通用的解题逻辑而非单一轨迹，从而显著提升了模型的数学推理与泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的大语言模型推理能力蒸馏方法大多依赖于模仿具体的解题轨迹（即模仿“回答什么”），这容易导致模型陷入对特定实例的记忆，而非习得可迁移的推理技巧，从而限制了模型在新问题上的泛化能力。

Method: 提出了策略引导策略优化（SGPO）框架：1. 提取强模型的结构化策略描述；2. 构建自主与策略引导的双重轨迹进行对比；3. 采用令牌级前向KL散度（forward-KL）目标进行蒸馏，确保策略迁移的稳定性和针对性；4. 引入自适应实例加权机制，根据模型当前的自主能力动态调整引导强度。

Result: 在四个数学基准测试及两个模型系列上的实验表明，SGPO持续优于监督微调（SFT）、在线强化学习（on-policy RL）及混合策略基线；在Qwen2.5-7B-Instruct模型上，平均分较最强基线提升了2.2个百分点，证明了该方法在提升推理性能及与基座模型扩展性方面的优势。

Conclusion: SGPO通过从“轨迹模仿”转向“策略蒸馏”，实现了知识的高效迁移，证明了通过结构化策略指导能够显著提升弱模型的推理能力和泛化性，是提升模型推理效率的一种有效范式。

Abstract: Distilling reasoning capabilities from strong to weak language models typically involves imitating specific solution trajectories, effectively transferring what to answer rather than how to reason. This trajectory-level imitation encourages memorization of instance-specific steps rather than acquisition of transferable problem-solving skills, limiting generalization to novel problems. We propose Strategy-Guided Policy Optimization (SGPO), which replaces instance-level trajectory imitation with reusable strategy distillation. SGPO extracts structured strategy descriptions from strong-model responses and, for each problem, constructs both autonomous and strategy-guided trajectories to enable direct comparison of the model's behavior with and without strategic guidance. The framework then addresses two key questions. For how to distill, a token-level forward-KL objective selectively transfers the distributional shift induced by strategy conditioning into the unguided policy, with proximal constraints ensuring stability. For when to distill, adaptive instance-level weighting strengthens guidance when autonomous exploration falls short and reduces it as the model's own competence grows. Experiments on four mathematical benchmarks across two model families show that SGPO consistently outperforms SFT, on-policy RL, and hybrid-policy baselines, improving the average score by 2.2 points over the strongest baseline on Qwen2.5-7B-Instruct. Analysis reveals that the forward-KL objective provides an inherently selective distillation signal that outperforms direct trajectory imitation, and that strategy distillation exhibits complementary scaling with base model capability.

</details>


### [75] [Exploring Academic Influence of Algorithms by Co-occurrence Network Based on Full-text of Academic Papers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24099)
*Yuzhuo Wang,Chengzhi Zhang,Min Song,Seong Deok Kim,Youngsoo Ko,Juhee Lee*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究利用网络分析方法，首次对学术界算法的共现关系进行了大规模长期分析，揭示了算法在学术生态中通过相互连接形成的结构化影响力及其演化规律。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的科学计量研究多孤立地评估单一算法，忽略了算法之间相互连接所形成的集体影响力。为了弥补这一空白，研究者试图从网络科学的视角，探究算法在学术生态系统中的连接结构及其随时间演变的动态特征。

Method: 基于自然语言处理（NLP）技术，利用深度学习模型从学术论文全文中提取算法实体。构建了涵盖过去四十年学术产出的总体、累积及年度算法共现网络，并应用多种中心性指标对算法的群体影响力和演化特征进行定量分析。

Result: 研究发现算法网络具有典型复杂网络特征，且连接密度随时间推移不断增加；高影响力算法通常位于网络中心或不同研究周期的交汇处，具备较高的控制力和均衡影响力；算法的影响力衰退遵循先失去核心网络位置、后减弱与其他算法关联的规律。

Conclusion: 本研究首次通过构建大规模算法共现网络，揭示了算法在科学研究中的集体影响力和演化规律。研究表明，算法的兴衰与其在网络中的结构位置密切相关，从核心地位的丧失到关联强度的减弱是算法影响力衰退的典型路径。该工作为理解人工智能领域的技术演进提供了全新的网络视角，并为后续研究算法、学者与任务间的复杂关联奠定了基础。

Abstract: Algorithms have become central to scientific research in the era of artificial intelligence (AI). Although algorithm mentions in papers are often used to indicate popularity and influence, existing studies usually evaluate individual algorithms in isolation and pay limited attention to the collective influence formed through their interconnections. This study constructs large-scale algorithm co-occurrence networks in natural language processing (NLP) based on the full text of academic papers and investigates algorithm influence from a network perspective. Using deep learning models, we extract algorithm entities and build overall, cumulative, and annual co-occurrence networks. We analyze their structural characteristics and apply multiple centrality measures to assess the group influence of algorithms across the whole field and over time. The results show that algorithm networks display typical features of complex networks, with increasingly dense connections developing over approximately two decades. Classic, high-performing algorithms and those located at the intersections of different research periods tend to have high popularity, control, centrality, and balanced influence. When the influence of an algorithm declines, it usually loses its core network position first, followed by weaker associations with other algorithms. This study is the first large-scale analysis of algorithm co-occurrence networks. Covering more than four decades of academic publications, it provides a temporal and structural view of algorithm influence and offers a foundation for future research on networks linking algorithms, scholars, and tasks.

Abstract: Multi-step reasoning with Chain-of-Thought (CoT) prompting remains fragile: logical errors or hallucinations in early steps silently propagate, producing confident but incorrect conclusions. Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) can produce clinically fluent recommendations for type 2 diabetes while failing to satisfy guideline constraints or explicitly justify lifestyle-related glycemic claims. ### [80] [The Geometry Behind Diffusion and Flow Matching: Gradient Flows and Geodesics in Wasserstein Space](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24157)
*Yian Yao,Weiwei Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文利用Wasserstein几何统一了扩散模型与流匹配：前者是自由能的梯度流，后者是Wasserstein空间的最优传输测地线，两者通过不同的路径实现生成任务，并解释了为何流匹配能实现更高效的采样。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的生成模型（如DDPM、DDIM、NCSN和流匹配）通常被视为独立的理论，缺乏统一的数学描述。本文旨在通过Wasserstein空间几何揭示不同生成模型背后的共同结构与内在联系。

Method: 利用最优传输理论（Optimal Transport）和Wasserstein几何，将扩散模型（Fokker-Planck方程及JKO离散化）与流匹配（Benamou-Brenier公式下的测地线路径）统一在 $\mathcal{P}_2(\mathbb{R}^d)$ 空间中，通过对比梯度流（初值问题）与测地线（边值问题）的几何特性进行解析。

Result: 证明了扩散模型本质上是自由能的梯度流（初值问题），而流匹配本质上是Wasserstein空间中的测地线运动（边值问题）。流匹配由于遵循最优传输路径，在生成过程中表现为确定性的ODE轨迹，相比扩散模型能显著减少采样步数。

Conclusion: 扩散模型（基于自由能梯度流）与流匹配（基于Wasserstein测地线）在概率测度空间中具有统一的几何解释。两者虽然遵循不同的动力学路径，但都可以在Wasserstein度量空间框架下进行精确的数学定义与对比。

Abstract: The space $\mathcal{P}_2(\mathbb{R}^d$) of probability measures with finite second moment carries a natural geometry: the quadratic Wasserstein distance W_2 makes it a complete metric space and, following Otto, a (formal) Riemannian manifold whose geodesics are the optimal-transport interpolations. On this manifold, the gradient flow of the free energy F(rho) = KL(rho || π) is exactly the Fokker-Planck equation, and its implicit-Euler discretization is the JKO scheme. This is the geometry underlying diffusion models: the forward process descends the free energy, and each denoising step realizes one JKO step, which recovers DDPM, DDIM, NCSN/SMLD, and Energy Matching; this is one scheme, not separate theories. The same manifold supports a second variational principle. Its geodesics - the minimum-action curves of the Benamou-Brenier formula - are precisely the optimal-transport paths that Flow Matching learns. Fixing both endpoints and following the geodesic, generation becomes a deterministic ODE along a straight line, hence far fewer sampling steps. Placing both families of models on one manifold makes their relationship exact: diffusion follows a free-energy gradient flow, an initial-value problem; optimal-transport Flow Matching follows a Wasserstein geodesic, a boundary-value problem. The two reach the same endpoints along different paths.

</details>


### [81] [An Introduction to Causal Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24160)
*Elias Bareinboim,Junzhe Zhang,Sanghack Lee*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文通过引入“因果强化学习（CRL）”，将因果推断的结构化建模能力与强化学习的决策能力相结合，利用结构因果模型统一了现有的学习范式，并开拓了反事实学习等新研究维度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 因果推断与强化学习长期以来独立发展，缺乏交流。本文旨在探讨两者在“反事实关系”这一核心概念上的本质联系，并希望通过建立两者之间的联系，解决强化学习中传统方法难以处理的复杂学习场景。

Method: 本文采用形式化的数学建模方法，将强化学习环境分解为一组具有不同因果不变性的自治机制，并用“结构因果模型”（Structural Causal Model, SCM）对其进行描述，从而实现因果推断与强化学习的数学统一。

Result: 本文成功论证了强化学习环境隐式地编码了因果结构，并通过因果视角统一了在线学习、离线策略学习和因果演算。此外，还提出了广义策略学习、干预点选择、模仿学习和反事实学习等新类别，拓宽了强化学习的研究范畴。

Conclusion: 本文提出了“因果强化学习”（CRL）这一框架，认为因果推断与强化学习在本质上通过反事实关系紧密相连。通过利用结构因果模型（SCM）对环境进行建模，可以统一现有的各种学习模式，并为处理更复杂的学习任务（如反事实决策、干预选择等）提供理论基础和新的研究方向。

Abstract: Causal inference provides a set of principles and tools that allow one to combine data and knowledge about an environment to reason with questions of counterfactual nature, i.e., what would have happened had reality been different, even when no data of this unrealized reality is currently available. Reinforcement learning provides methods to learn a policy that optimizes a specific measure (e.g., reward, regret) when the agent is deployed in an environment and pursues an exploratory, trial-and-error approach. These two disciplines have evolved independently and with virtually no interaction between them. We note that they operate over different aspects of the same building block, counterfactual relations, which makes them umbilically connected. Based on these observations, novel learning opportunities arise when this connection is explicitly acknowledged and mathematized. To realize this potential, we note that any environment where the RL agent is deployed can be decomposed as a collection of autonomous mechanisms with different causal invariances, parsimoniously modeled as a structural causal model; any standard RL setting implicitly encodes such a model. This formalization allows us to put under a unifying treatment different modes of learning, including online, off-policy, and causal calculus learning, which appear unrelated in the literature. However, these modalities are not exhaustive: we introduce several natural and pervasive classes of learning settings that entail novel dimensions of analysis. Specifically, we introduce and discuss through causal lenses generalized policy learning, where to intervene, imitation learning, and counterfactual learning. These tasks lead to a broader view of counterfactual learning and suggest great potential for studying causal inference and reinforcement learning side by side, which we call causal reinforcement learning (CRL).

</details>


### [82] [Data Scale, Not Latency, Shapes Cross-Lingual Encoder Transfer in Streaming ASR](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24169)
*Nenad Banfic*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文研究了流式语音识别模型在适配新语言时初始化策略的选择问题，发现多语言初始化的优势仅存在于低数据场景，且随数据量增长迅速消失，而延迟和量化决策则可与模型初始化解耦。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在将流式语音识别模型适配至新语言时，通常需要在多语言（ML）编码器和英语（EN）编码器之间做出选择。目前尚不清楚多语言初始化的优势能持续多久、流式延迟是否会放大这种优势，以及该优势在量化部署后是否依然有效。因此，本文旨在系统性地解答这些问题，为实际应用中的初始化选择提供指导。

Method: 作者以 0.6B 参数的缓存感知 FastConformer 转换器模型为基础，在八种欧洲语言上进行了受控实验。实验涵盖了五个不同的数据规模（100 小时至 2500 小时）、三种不同的流式延迟层级以及离线解码，并利用四个公开测试集进行了评估。同时，研究还评估了 4-bit 权重仅量化（weight-only quantization）对模型性能的影响。

Result: 实验表明，多语言初始化的优势受限于数据规模而非延迟。在 FLEURS 数据集上，随着目标语言数据量翻倍，多语言初始化的性能优势大致减半。在 100 小时数据量下，ML 与 EN 的词错误率（WER）差距为 4.21%，但在 2500 小时时降至 0.20%。此外，4-bit 量化虽能将编码器空间占用减少约 3 倍，但仅带来约 0.5% 的 WER 劣化，且其影响与初始化策略无关。

Conclusion: 研究指出，多语言初始化（ML）主要在低数据量场景下具有显著优势，随着目标语言数据量的增加，该优势会迅速衰减并趋于零。因此，在数据量充沛时，选择单语言（EN）还是多语言初始化对性能影响微乎其微；此外，延迟约束和量化决策可以与初始化策略独立进行。

Abstract: Adapting a streaming speech recognition model to a new language requires choosing between two plausible warm starts: a multilingual (ML) encoder or an English-only (EN) encoder. The common intuition is that the multilingual encoder should help most at low data, but it is unclear how long that advantage persists, whether tight streaming latency amplifies it, and whether it survives deployment quantization. We answer these questions with a controlled sweep of a 0.6 B-parameter cache-aware FastConformer transducer across eight European languages, up to five target-language data scales (100 h to 2500 h), three streaming tiers plus offline decoding, and up to four public test sets. The main result is that multilingual initialization is a data-limited advantage, not a latency-limited one. On FLEURS at 160 ms, the mean EN-ML word error rate (WER) gap falls from +4.21 percentage points (pp) at 100 h to +0.20 pp at 2500 h; a power-law fit summarizes this decay, with each doubling of target-language data roughly halving the remaining advantage. Across the three streaming tiers, the across-language mean EN-ML gap is approximately stable at each scale from 100 to 1000 h, and is near zero by 2500 h. Finally, 4-bit weight-only encoder quantization at the matched 560 ms streaming tier reduces the encoder footprint by about 3x, with an average FLEURS WER increase of about 0.5 pp. The resulting guideline is simple: use multilingual initialization in low-data regimes, treat the choice as effectively irrelevant at large data, and make latency and quantization decisions independently.

### [83] [Navigating User Behavior toward Personalized Multimodal Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24196)
*Hengji Zhou,Yufeng Liu,Ye Liu,Yong Xu,Lianghao Xia,Liqiang Nie*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: NaviGen 提出了一种将用户历史行为转化为高质量生成指令的框架，通过双重编码和 SFT+RL 训练，解决了用户描述能力不足与 AIGC 模型精准生成需求之间的错位问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的 AIGC 流水线高度依赖结构完整的提示词，而普通用户往往难以准确描述视觉细节，导致生成内容与用户需求不匹配。研究旨在解决如何将用户交互历史转化为可执行的生成指令这一难题。

Method: 1. 双重标识符（Dual Identifier）：将每个项目表示为“协同代码”和“文本代码”的结合，作为行为基础和语义桥梁。
2. 两阶段训练流程：首先通过进化搜索获取监督信息，进行监督微调（SFT）以学习偏好推理和指令撰写；随后利用分层及自洽奖励机制进行强化学习（RL），实现与用户意图的对齐。

Result: 在产品、游戏和短视频等领域的实验表明，NaviGen 有效提升了个性化图像和视频生成的质量，增强了对用户下一项行为的预测能力，并能产出更具体、相关且视觉可生成性更强的指令。

Conclusion: NaviGen 通过双重标识符表征和两阶段 SFT+RL 训练框架，成功弥合了用户行为历史与高质量生成指令之间的鸿沟，为个性化内容生成提供了一种有效且通用的解决方案。

Abstract: Modern AIGC pipelines deliver high-fidelity images and videos but presuppose a well-formed creation instruction, while end users rarely articulate visual details, leaving generators misaligned with user demand. We study personalized content generation, which turns a user's interaction history into an executable instruction for downstream synthesis, and identify two obstacles: behavior must be encoded in a form legible to language reasoning, and the model must acquire instruction-writing skill absent from both pretraining and behavior data. We propose NaviGen, which represents each item with a dual identifier coupling a collaborative code and a textual code as a behavioral substrate and a semantic bridge in one token stream. On this representation, a two-stage SFT+RL pipeline first distills preference reasoning and instruction writing from evolutionarily searched supervision, then aligns generation with user intent through hierarchical and self-consistent rewards. Experiments across product, game, and short-video domains show that NaviGen improves personalized image and video generation, strengthens next-item prediction, and yields more specific, relevant, and visually generatable instructions. Our code is anonymously released at: https://github.com/iLearn-Lab/NaviGen.

</details>


### [84] [Exploring the relationship between human-centric AI and firm idiosyncratic risks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24224)
