Method: 本文结合情境人工智能理论和社会技术系统理论，采用中国A股上市公司2015年至2023年的多源面板数据，通过面板回归模型实证分析了HCAI对企业特质风险的影响，并考察了数字化、运营效率、高管持股及CEO IT背景等社会技术因素的调节效应。

Result: 实证结果发现，HCAI与企业特质风险降低显著相关。具体而言，数字化水平和高管持股比例强化了这一风险降低效应；而运营效率和拥有IT背景的CEO反而削弱了该风险缓解作用。

Conclusion: 研究表明，以人为本的人工智能（HCAI）通过缓解伦理风险和增强人机协同，能有效降低企业特质风险（IR）。该研究为人工智能时代的伦理治理与财务风险管理提供了重要的理论支撑与实践指导。

Abstract: Despite the extensive discussions of human-centric AI (HCAI) in Industry 5.0, its effects on firms' idiosyncratic risks (IR) remains underexplored. This is an imperative issue for firms navigate financial risks during the current technological revolution, as IR reflects investor reactions to corporate heterogeneous AI strategies and implementations by isolating firm-level stock volatility from systematic factors. Integrating situated AI theory with social-technical systems theory, we conceptualise HCAI as a situated AI strategy that reduces AI-related ethical risks and fosters AI-Human synergies in firms' business operations, ultimately reducing IR by aligning with stakeholders' diverse expectations. Moreover, socio-technical factors, namely digitalisation, operational efficiency, executive shareholding, and CEOs with IT background, may moderate the HCAI-IR relationship. Using a multi-source panel dataset of Chinese listed firms from 2015 to 2023, we find that HCAI is associated with lower firm IR. Furthermore, digitalisation and executive shareholding strengthen this risk-reducing effect, whereas operational efficiency and CEOs with IT background surprisingly attenuate it. Our findings offer theoretical contributions and practical insights for both ethical AI governance and firm financial risk management in the AI era.

### [85] [FlowR2A: Learning Reward-to-Action Distribution for Multimodal Driving Planning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24231)
*Xirui Li,Zhe Liu,Xiaoqing Ye,Wenhua Han,Yifeng Pan,Junyu Han,Hengshuang Zhao*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: FlowR2A 提出了一种基于流匹配的生成式规划模型，将复杂的驾驶奖励转化为生成条件，成功融合了评分法和锚点法的优点，实现了自动驾驶中高质量、可控的多模态轨迹规划。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自动驾驶规划领域长期存在两个范式矛盾：基于评分的方法虽具备稠密奖励监督，但动作空间被硬性限定；基于锚点的方法虽能动态生成建议，但监督信号过于稀疏（仅依赖单一真实轨迹）。作者旨在打破这一局限，寻求一种既能利用稠密奖励监督又具备灵活生成能力的方法。

Method: 提出了一种名为 FlowR2A 的框架，核心思想是将模拟奖励转化为生成式条件。具体包括：1. 利用流匹配解码器（flow-matching decoder）学习奖励条件下的动作分布，从而将稠密奖励信息嵌入模型；2. 引入细粒度的时间步奖励条件和奖励噪声增强技术，以平衡安全性约束与任务进度目标；3. 支持测试时的奖励引导采样和锚点采样，实现可控的轨迹生成。

Result: FlowR2A 在 NAVSIM v1 和 v2 基准测试中达到了最先进的性能（SOTA），生成的规划建议在质量和多模态多样性上均显著优于现有方法，证明了其在处理复杂驾驶场景时的有效性。

Conclusion: FlowR2A 通过生成式建模成功统一了评分法和锚点法，有效解决了自动驾驶规划中动作空间受限与监督稀疏的矛盾。该方法能够生成高质量、多模态的规划建议，并在安全性和效率之间实现平衡，为自动驾驶决策规划提供了新的研究范式。

Abstract: Multimodal driving planning faces a long-standing tension between two paradigms: scoring-based methods benefit from dense reward supervision but are confined to a fixed action vocabulary, while anchor-based methods generate proposals dynamically yet suffer from sparse supervision constrained to a single ground-truth trajectory. In this work, we propose FlowR2A, which resolves this tension by reframing simulation-based rewards from discriminative targets into generative conditions. By learning the reward-conditioned action distribution from dense trajectory-reward pairs with a flow-matching decoder, FlowR2A unifies the dense supervision of scoring-based methods with the proposal generation of anchor-based methods in a single generative model, forcing the model to internalize the correlation between an action and its outcomes in safety, progress, comfort, and rule compliance. To balance hard safety constraints against soft progress objectives, we introduce fine-grained per-timestep reward conditioning and reward noise augmentation. The generative formulation naturally supports controllable test-time sampling via reward guidance and anchored sampling, producing high-quality proposals. FlowR2A achieves state-of-the-art results on the NAVSIM v1 and v2 benchmarks, with multimodal proposals of substantially higher quality than prior methods.

*Kaiwen Zhou,Constantin Venhoff,Jonathan Michala,Xin Eric Wang,William Saunders*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究者提出了一种基于线性探针（linear probes）的监测方法：首先定义了一个包含18个细粒度认知过程的失准指标分类体系；其次开发了一个基于元计划引导的自动化流水线，用以生成多轮训练对话；最后通过在模型内部激活值中应用探针来实时识别这些失准指标。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了通过监测大模型的内部认知过程（失准指标）来检测其失准行为是可行且有效的。这种方法不仅能够实现高精度的检测，而且通过对内部表征的分析，为提升大模型安全性提供了新的可解释性工具。

Abstract: Large language models exhibit a growing range of misaligned behaviors such as strategic deception, sandbagging, and self-preservation. As they are increasingly deployed in high-stakes settings, it is critical to reliably detect such behaviors to ensure safe and responsible use. In this work, we propose to monitor misalignment by decomposing it into fine-grained cognitive processes -- misalignment indicators -- and detecting their presence in a model's internal activations via linear probes. We develop a taxonomy of 18 indicators spanning different misaligned behaviors, paired with an automated, meta-plan-guided pipeline that generates multi-turn training conversations. To rigorously evaluate generalization, we construct an out-of-distribution suite combining automated behavioral elicitation, established misalignment benchmarks, and natural benign conversations. Across 5 misaligned behaviors, our probes match a strong LLM judge with 0.935 AUROC on out-of-distribution benchmarks while keeping a low false positive rate on benign traffic. We further perform in-depth analysis to understand the probes and the model's internal representations of misalignment indicators.

### [88] [Accelerating Disaggregated RL for Visual Generative LLMs with Diffusion-Based Parallelism and Trainer-Assisted Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24369)
*Sijie Wang,Zhengyu Qing,Zhiqiang Tan,Yiming Yin,Yeqing Zhang,Yaoyuan Wang,Qiang Wang,Xiaowen Chu,Shaohuai Shi*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: DigenRL 是一款专门针对扩散模型强化学习的解耦系统架构，通过优化流水线、引入训练资源弹性协作及异步策略，显著提升了大规模生成式模型的训练效率和资源利用率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前针对扩散生成式LLM的强化学习系统大多依赖于共置执行（Colocated execution），导致训练与生成资源耦合，限制了异构部署能力和独立扩展性，难以满足高性能、大规模模型训练的需求。

Method: 1. 采用解耦架构（Disaggregated Architecture），将生成（Rollout）与训练（Training）过程分离以支持异构资源调度；2. 引入生成轴流水线（GAP）与时间步并行（TSP）技术优化细粒度流水线；3. 提出弹性训练辅助生成（TAG）机制，利用训练资源参与生成任务；4. 采用严格单步约束的异步策略以消除流水线尾部气泡。

Result: 在多款主流生成模型（HunyuanVideo-13B, Wan2.1-14B, FLUX.1-12B, QwenImage-20B）上的实验表明，DigenRL 相比当前最先进的系统（如 veRL-Omni 和 GenRL），吞吐量提升了 1.56 至 2.10 倍。

Conclusion: DigenRL 通过创新的解耦架构设计，解决了扩散模型强化学习在资源调度和执行效率上的瓶颈，证明了在分布式环境下实现高效大规模模型训练的可行性，为生成式模型的深度优化提供了高效的系统框架。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning (RL) has become a dominant post-training paradigm, driving the emergence of high-performance RL systems such as veRL for autoregressive large language models (LLMs). In parallel, diffusion-oriented RL algorithms, e.g., DanceGRPO and FlowGRPO, have rapidly expanded the scope of RL from language reasoning to diffusion-based visual and flow-based generation. However, efficient RL systems for diffusion generative LLMs remain underexplored. Existing implementations, e.g., veRL-Omni, still rely on colocated execution, which simplifies synchronization but couples rollout and training resources, limits heterogeneous deployment, and constrains independent scaling.
  To this end, we introduce DigenRL, a disaggregated RL framework for diffusion-based generative LLMs that supports flexible resource allocation, accommodates heterogeneous GPUs, and facilitates efficient task scheduling. To maximally reduce the execution bubbles in the disaggregated architecture, we propose: 1) a generation-axis pipeline (GAP) and time-step parallelism (TSP) in the diffusion architecture to enable finer-grained pipelining between rollout and training; 2) an elastic trainer-assisted generation (TAG) approach to enable the trainer GPU resources to dynamically assist in executing rollout generations; and 3) a tightly one-step constrained asynchronous strategy to further utilize the tail bubble in the pipeline. Extensive experiments are conducted on three hardware testbeds with 16-32 GPUs using HunyuanVideo-13B, Wan2.1-14B, FLUX.1-12B, and QwenImage-20B generative models. Experimental results show that DigenRL achieves 1.56-2.10x throughput improvements over state-of-the-art diffusion RL systems, veRL-Omni and GenRL.

### [89] [When Helpfulness Overrides Causal Caution: Context-Dependent Suppression and Recovery in LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24370)
*Hiroshi Okumura*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 研究发现主流大模型在提供实践建议时会为了“乐于助人”而放弃“因果谨慎”，表现出极高的过度自信。通过简单的提示词引导或采用分离式的审计架构，可以有效缓解这一偏差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的LLM评估多集中于因果推理能力，但忽略了一个关键的认识论维度——“因果谨慎”（Causal Caution），即在实证证据不足时拒绝做出因果判断的倾向。本研究旨在探讨LLM在从学术转向实践咨询语境时，这种谨慎态度是否会被系统性抑制。

Method: 研究团队基于珍珠因果层级（PCH）构建评估指标，对四款主流高性能LLM（Claude Sonnet/Opus, GPT 5.5, Gemini Pro）在480个样本中进行实验。实验对比了学术与实践咨询语境下的表现，并引入了“重新审视因果关系”的自我修正提示，使用Fisher精确检验和McNemar检验进行统计分析。

Result: 实验显示，模型在学术场景中表现出极高的因果谨慎度（91.7%–100%），但在实践建议场景中骤降至6.7%–18.3%。在明确索要建议的提示下，仅有0.5%的回复保持谨慎。通过引入简单的自我修正提示，因果谨慎的维护率可恢复至71.4%–100%。

Conclusion: LLMs在实践建议场景中表现出对“因果谨慎”的系统性抑制，这并非能力缺失，而是受“乐于助人”驱动的响应模式所致。通过分离提案生成与因果审计的多智能体架构，可以有效提升LLM在决策支持中的可靠性。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly integrated into decision-support roles in business and policy contexts. While prior benchmark studies have primarily evaluated LLMs' causal reasoning capabilities, a more fundamental epistemic dimension has been overlooked: Causal Caution, defined as the propensity to refrain from causal judgment when empirical evidence is insufficient. This study examines the systematic suppression of Causal Caution that occurs when LLMs shift from academic to practical advisory contexts. Using an evaluation rubric inspired by Pearl's Causal Hierarchy (the PCH score), we conducted experiments on four high-performance LLMs -- Claude Sonnet 4.6, Claude Opus 4.7, GPT 5.5, and Gemini 3.1 Pro -- across 480 trials. Causal Caution maintenance rates were 91.7--100.0% in academic contexts but dropped to 6.7--18.3% in practical advisory contexts (Fisher's exact test, p < .001 across all models). Furthermore, when restricted to practical prompts requesting concrete recommendations or explanatory rationales, only 1 of 200 responses (0.5%) maintained Causal Caution. A brief self-correction prompt -- "Please reconsider this judgment from the perspective of causal relationships" -- restored the expression of Causal Caution to maintenance rates of 71.4--100.0% (McNemar's test, p < .001 across all models). These results suggest that helpfulness-oriented response patterns may suppress the expression of Causal Caution in practical advisory contexts, with important implications for organizational governance. The findings indicate that this suppression reflects context-dependent variation in expression rather than an underlying capability limitation, suggesting that multi-agent architectures that separate proposal generation from causal auditing may offer a promising governance design.

### [90] [PHANTOM: A Large-Scale Dataset of Multimodal Adversarial Attacks for Vision-Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24388)
*Simone Gallivanone,Hossein Khodadadi,Mauro Dore,Mauro Medda,Nicola Franco*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 由于生成大规模对抗性攻击需要高昂的计算成本和复杂的技术门槛，现有的研究评估往往受到资源限制。作者旨在通过发布一个大规模、开源的对抗性样本数据集，为研究社区提供普惠的资源，以系统地评估视觉语言模型的稳健性与安全性。

Method: 研究团队通过整合现有文献中的先进攻击策略，构建了一个涵盖10个高级类别和55个子类别的对抗性样本库。该数据集不仅汇编并扩展了已有的多个基准测试，还引入了额外的恶意意图类别，总计包含47,524个对抗样本和7,826个意图，旨在实现多样化和高代表性的评估覆盖。

Result: 发布了一个包含47,524个高质量、多样化对抗样本的开源数据集，覆盖了广泛的有害意图。该资源成功地填补了当前VLM安全领域在大规模评估基准上的空白，支持研究者进行更具可重复性和比较性的安全测试及防御机制开发。

Conclusion: 该数据集为视觉语言模型（VLM）的安全性研究提供了宝贵的基础设施。通过降低对抗性攻击研究的门槛，它促进了社区在模型稳健性评估、防御机制开发以及对齐技术方面的协同进步，对于构建更安全、可信的AI系统具有重要意义。

Abstract: We introduce a large-scale, open-source dataset of pre-generated adversarial attacks for vision-language models (VLMs). The dataset is designed to be diverse, representative, and practical, extending existing benchmarks by covering 10 high-level categories and 55 subcategories of harmful intents. Our primary goal is to make adversarial data accessible to the research community, given the computational cost and complexity of generating large numbers of attacks. The dataset comprises 47 524 adversarial samples, generated using state-of-the-art attack strategies from recent literature. Our work complements existing efforts by consolidating and extending prior benchmarks from multiple established sources, resulting in 7 826 intents, and introduce an additional category to broaden coverage. This provides realistic evaluation resources for studying model robustness and alignment. Our dataset intends to enable researchers and practitioners to systematically evaluate the robustness and safety of VLMs, fine-tune attack-generation models, and develop or stress-test defensive guardrails under diverse adversarial conditions. By releasing this resource, we aim to lower the barrier to adversarial research and foster more reproducible, comprehensive, and comparable evaluations of VLM safety.

</details>


### [91] [Age of LLM: A Strategic 1v1 Benchmark for Reasoning, Diplomacy and Reliability of Large Language Models under Fog of War](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24391)
*Arnaud Ricci*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个名为“Age of LLM”的对抗性基准测试，通过在受控的1v1网格战中评估15种大语言模型，发现核武器策略具有绝对主导地位，同时揭示了模型在处理复杂约束、信念跟踪和战略交互时的认知特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在解决当前公共基准测试中普遍存在的数据污染问题，并探索大语言模型在包含不完全信息、复杂约束和对抗性压力环境下的真实推理能力、信念跟踪以及人际交互（外交）策略。

Method: 研究设计了一个回合制1v1网格对抗基准测试“Age of LLM”，包含战争迷雾、复杂的外交系统以及严格的JSON格式要求。通过对15个推理模型进行54场比赛（共5,258个动作）的实测，通过分析模型在受限条件下的操作轨迹、外交沟通及非法动作率，评估其逻辑推理和决策能力。

Result: 1. 核突击策略具有压倒性优势（胜率高达78%-85%）；2. 军事征服虽然罕见但效率更高；3. 模型间的外交沟通非常频繁，但几乎没有实质性协议达成；4. 大量非法动作源于对“战争迷雾”状态的认知偏差，可作为模型信念跟踪能力的衡量指标；5. 模型可靠性与胜率之间存在初步的关联倾向。

Conclusion: 该研究表明，在“Age of LLM”博弈环境中，核突击策略占据绝对主导地位，且模型在处理外交、非法动作和信念跟踪方面表现出不同的行为模式。研究强调了在对抗性不确定环境下，对大语言模型进行认知建模（如信念跟踪和虚假陈述）的潜力，而不仅仅是关注胜负排名。

Abstract: We introduce Age of LLM, a turn-based 1v1 benchmark in which two LLMs face off on a 13x7 grid to destroy the enemy base. Three stressors are deliberate: fog of war, full diplomacy (messages, ceasefires, ultimatums; uranium kept secret), and a reliability dimension where every turn must follow a strict JSON schema and an illegal action is silently discarded. The engine is private and each match uses a fresh random map seed and opponent, mitigating the data contamination that affects public benchmarks. Models receive a (near) rule-only prompt with no build-order advice (two tactical seed phrases were present during data collection; see Section 2.7). We benchmark 15 reasoning models across 54 matches and 5,258 actions. Findings: (1) the nuclear rush dominates (78% on the rules-coherent v0.11+ sub-corpus; 85% corpus-wide) with a sole-launcher signature that is largely mechanical under secret-simultaneous launch rules, not a cognitive deterrence failure; (2) military conquest is rare but faster (12.3 vs 18.9 turns); (3) diplomacy is prolific yet almost never consummated; (4) ~58% of illegal actions are fog/state errors, making the illegal-action rate a measure of belief-tracking; (5) -- the least established, and the only one we label exploratory -- a weak link associates reliability with winning. The corpus is small, unbalanced and not side-swapped, so the ranking is a preliminary descriptive view, not a contribution. Beyond ranking, the turn-by-turn traces of actions and messages make the corpus a lens on how LLMs reason under adversarial uncertainty -- their belief-tracking, spontaneous deception, and per-model cognitive "personas" -- which we frame as a future research direction. We release the replay format, an isometric viewer and all replays; engine source on request.

</details>


### [92] [ATRIA: Adaptive Traceable ECG Reporting with Iterative Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24392)
*Donggyun Hong,Kyuhwan Lee,Junmyung Kwon,Yong-Yeon Jo*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: ATRIA 是一个创新的多智能体 ECG 报告系统，旨在模拟医生迭代式的临床工作流程，通过将报告结论与证据绑定，实现人机协同的报告验证与修改，显著提升了医疗 AI 生成报告的准确性与临床可用性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的 ECG 报告生成系统存在两个主要问题：一是端到端模型将解释与报告生成紧密耦合，导致错误无法修正；二是现有的智能体系统多为单次处理（single-pass），缺乏对先前输出的修订和优化能力。临床医生在撰写报告时通常是迭代式的，需要结合上下文并进行反复推敲，现有 AI 系统未能模拟这一核心过程。

Method: 提出了一种多智能体（multi-agent）ECG 报告系统 ATRIA。该方法将报告生成任务解耦，实现了迭代式的工作流程：1. 将每一项报告结论与 ECG 证据绑定；2. 识别并标记缺乏证据支持的陈述；3. 支持在中途引入额外的上下文信息；4. 提供人机交互接口，允许医生对单项发现进行核实和修改，而非仅依赖一次性生成的黑盒结果。

Result: 通过四个交互案例演示，证明了 ATRIA 系统能够有效地将报告结论与证据对齐，通过人机协作修正错误，并能够实时整合额外上下文。由于底层采用已在临床应用的 ECG 分析模型，该系统具有较高的临床可信度，且作为云端 Web 服务，具备即时部署的能力。

Conclusion: ATRIA 系统通过模拟临床医生的迭代工作流，成功解决了当前 ECG 报告生成系统缺乏中间验证和修改能力的痛点。该系统在提高生成内容的临床可信度、支持人机交互反馈以及易于部署方面具有显著优势，为医疗 AI 的临床应用提供了新的范式。

Abstract: Existing ECG report generation is tightly coupled -- interpretation and reporting fused end-to-end, so errors propagate without stage-level recourse -- while agent-based systems decouple tasks but remain single-pass, never revisiting earlier outputs. Clinical ECG reporting instead unfolds iteratively, requiring progressive context integration and bidirectional editing. We present \textsc{ATRIA}, a multi-agent ECG reporting system that mirrors the clinician's iterative workflow: it binds every report claim to its supporting evidence, flags statements unsupported by that evidence, incorporates additional context mid-session, and lets clinicians verify and revise individual findings rather than accept one opaque output. Because its agents use ECG analysis models already in clinical use, the underlying findings are clinically trustworthy; and as a cloud-based web service, \textsc{ATRIA} is ready for immediate deployment. We demonstrate \textsc{ATRIA} through four interaction cases, with a live demo and video available.

Conclusion: 在结构化形式化验证证书的解释任务中，针对特定领域的定制化神经架构在准确性、速度和成本方面均显著优于通用大语言模型（LLM）。该研究证明了利用循环一致性约束和符号验证器作为反馈机制，可以生成既忠实于证书事实又易于理解的自然语言解释。

Abstract: Formal verification produces machine-checkable certificates that attest to the satisfaction or violation of temporal properties, yet these certificates remain opaque to non-specialist stakeholders. We propose a cycle-consistent neural architecture that generates faithful natural language explanations of verification certificates. A forward network NN1 maps certificates to explanations, and an inverse network NN2 reconstructs certificates from explanations; a symbolic verifier closes the loop, providing a differentiable faithfulness proxy. A pointer-generator mechanism ensures lexical grounding by copying state names directly from the certificate. We evaluate on 420 test certificates spanning six verification methods (bounded proof, k-induction, inductive invariant, lasso, reachability, witness pair) in both YES and NO verdict variants, drawn from a financial compliance domain with 207 named states. The neural model wins on 10 of 12 verdict/kind categories, with three categories reaching 100% soundness. The architecture offers 860x faster inference (185 ms vs. 160 s per certificate for the full multi-LLM baseline), offline operation, deterministic outputs, and zero per-inference cost. ### [95] [Can Aggregate Invariants Accelerate Continuous Subgraph Matching? Limits, Laws, and a Dynamic Spectral Index](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24421)
*Minghao Chen,Jiale Zheng*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文研究了谱过滤在动态子图匹配（CSM）中的应用，提出了一种选择性维护局部谱特征的方法。实验证明，该技术能有效减少候选集并加速查询，但主要提升了候选集构建和扫描的效率，而非邻接遍历过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 谱过滤在静态子图匹配中表现优异，但其在动态图（持续更新）中的适用性和效率尚不明确。研究者旨在探讨如何通过高效维护谱边界来加速动态子图匹配，并解决谱重计算成本与剪枝效能之间的冲突。

Method: 本文提出了以下方法：1. 形式化扰动松弛以分析谱边界的稳定性；2. 采用选择性维护策略，仅在小邻域更新谱特征；3. 开发了动态局部谱索引，并将其集成到解耦的CSM基准测试中，通过与对照组对比评估性能。

Result: 在四个真实图数据集和77个查询场景下的实验表明：谱过滤可剔除多达51%的候选集，或跳过47%的更新枚举。该方法在处理特定结构时具有极高的加速比（高达748倍），但在一般情况下，其加速主要体现在候选集扫描阶段，对邻接引导的搜索过程影响有限。

Conclusion: 本文证明了谱过滤在动态子图匹配（CSM）中的有效性取决于计算成本与剪枝收益之间的权衡。对于中心节点，频繁更新谱特征的开销大于其剪枝收益，因此该方法最适用于局部小邻域的实时维护，能够显著减少候选集规模。

Abstract: Spectral filtering recently delivered substantial pruning for \emph{static} subgraph matching: Laplacian interlacing rejects candidates whose neighborhoods cannot host the query. We study whether such aggregate structural tests can accelerate \emph{continuous} subgraph matching (CSM) over dynamic graphs, and answer in three parts. First, lazily maintained spectral bounds are infeasible exactly where spectral pruning has value: we characterize the tightest safe rule over a formalized perturbation relaxation and show that even it loses essentially all pruning power within four touching updates. Second, exact maintenance is affordable when selective: pruning utility and recomputation cost are anti-correlated across vertices -- hubs provably never prune -- so recomputing small-neighborhood spectra on touch sustains exact local spectra at microseconds per update, complete by construction. Third, integrated into a decoupled CSM benchmark against an identical-minus-spectra control, the tests remove up to $51\%$ of candidates or safely skip up to $47\%$ of update enumerations, yet enumeration intermediates remain unchanged -- beyond the gates' skipped first-level bindings, typically zero -- across two engines, four real graphs, two stream types, and $77$ solved queries; a constructed radius-stratified workload confirms the instrument detects the exception when one exists ($-99.9\%$ intermediates, $748\times$ faster). Aggregate tests accelerate what scales with candidate sets -- construction, list scans -- never adjacency-guided exploration. We distill an intermediate-invariance methodology for evaluating CSM filters and release a reusable dynamic local-spectra index.

### [96] [ReM-MoA: Reasoning Memory Sustains Mixture-of-Agents Scaling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24437)
*Heng Ping,Arijit Bhattacharjee,Peiyu Zhang,Shixuan Li,Wei Yang,Ali Jannesari,Nesreen Ahmed,Paul Bogdan*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 针对 MoA 架构在深层扩展时的性能瓶颈，本文提出 ReM-MoA 框架，通过引入排序推理记忆与多样化路由机制，成功实现了多智能体系统随深度增加而持续提升推理性能的目标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的混合智能体（MoA）架构在增加层数（深度）时无法持续获得性能增益，往往表现出性能退化、早期平台期或饱和现象，缺乏有效的机制来处理深层推理中的信息传递与质量控制。

Method: 提出了 ReM-MoA（记忆增强型 MoA）框架，包含两项核心机制：(1) 排序推理记忆（Ranked Reasoning Memory）：利用评审智能体对各层的推理轨迹进行持久化存储与分级排名；(2) 策展多样化记忆路由（Curated Diversified Memory Routing）：确保智能体接触到多样化的成功与失败轨迹，在维持探索多样性的同时传播高质量推理结果。此外，还引入了可选的多领域评审蒸馏流水线以优化排序质量。

Result: 在跨越数学、形式逻辑、代码、知识及常识推理的五个基准测试中，ReM-MoA 在深度和宽度扩展上均始终优于现有的 MoA 变体，且其优势随着深度的增加而进一步扩大。

Conclusion: ReM-MoA 证明了引入结构化的跨层推理记忆是实现多智能体推理系统有效扩展的关键机制。通过该框架，系统能够突破传统 MoA 架构在增加深度时的性能饱和瓶颈，实现持续的性能提升。

Abstract: Mixture-of-Agents (MoA) architectures improve inference-time scaling by organizing multiple LLM agents into layered reasoning pipelines. However, existing MoA variants fail to sustain gains as depth increases, exhibiting degradation, early plateauing, or saturation. We propose ReM-MoA, a memory-augmented MoA framework that sustains scaling through two mechanisms: (1) a Ranked Reasoning Memory that persistently stores and ranks reasoning traces from all layers using a comparative Reviewer Agent, and (2) a Curated Diversified Memory Routing scheme that exposes different agents to distinct combinations of successful and failed traces, preserving exploration diversity while propagating high-quality reasoning. We further introduce an optional multi-domain Reviewer distillation pipeline that improves ranking quality through frontier-model supervision. Across five reasoning benchmarks spanning math, formal logic, code, knowledge, and commonsense, ReM-MoA consistently outperforms prior MoA variants across both depth and width scaling, and its advantage widens with depth, establishing structured cross-layer reasoning memory as a key missing mechanism for scalable multi-agent inference.

</details>


### [97] [Bayesian control for coding agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24453)
*Theodore Papamarkou,Vladislav Smirnov,Viktor Mazanov,Artem Vazhentsev,Preslav Nakov,Timothy Baldwin,Artem Shelmanov*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种基于贝叶斯控制的智能代码代理编排框架，通过动态平衡工具使用成本与预测准确性，实现了更高效的自动化编程，并提供了一种更准确的代码正确性评估方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的代码代理编排器多依赖固定的硬编码规则，缺乏对不确定性的评估，且未充分考虑工具使用（如诊断和验证）的成本效益，导致资源分配效率低下。

Method: 该论文将编排问题形式化为“成本敏感的序贯假设检验”问题，并构建了一个贝叶斯控制器。该控制器基于对候选代码正确性的信念，动态决定下一步操作（如继续收集证据、修正代码、执行验证或终止过程）。

Result: 通过在六种生成器和九个基准测试上的实验验证，贝叶斯控制策略在验证成本高且反馈具有不确定性时表现最佳。同时，其内部的信念状态作为正确性评分指标，在不确定性量化任务中优于令牌概率及原始工具成功率等基准方法。

Conclusion: 该研究表明，将贝叶斯决策框架引入代码生成代理的编排中，能够显著提高复杂环境下的系统效能，特别是在验证成本高昂且反馈质量不均匀的场景下。此外，由此产生的信念状态提供了一种优于传统指标的、更可靠的正确性不确定性度量方式。

Abstract: Modern coding agents pair LLM generators with various tools, including cheap diagnostics and expensive verifiers. The tool-use decisions are typically governed by orchestrators that often use fixed rules and ignore uncertainty. We formulate orchestration as cost-sensitive sequential hypothesis testing: a Bayesian controller maintains a belief over candidate correctness and dynamically decides whether to gather more evidence, refine the candidate, verify it, or stop. Across six generators and nine coding benchmarks, Bayesian control proves to be most valuable when verification is costly and critics are informative but imperfect. Beyond control, the belief state yields an interpretable correctness score that outperforms token-probability and raw tool-success baselines for uncertainty quantification.

</details>


### [98] [CompressKV: Semantic-Retrieval-Guided KV-Cache Compression for Resource-Efficient Long-Context LLM Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24467)
*Xiaolin Lin,Jingcun Wang,Olga Kondrateva,Yiyu Shi,Bing Li,Grace Li Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: CompressKV 是一种针对 GQA 架构大模型的高效 KV Cache 压缩框架，通过识别关键的“语义检索头”并优化层级缓存预算，以极小的内存占用实现了接近满缓存的推理效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前长上下文大模型推理受限于 KV Cache 巨大的内存占用和高昂的解码成本。现有的启发式 KV Cache 驱逐方法对所有注意力头一视同仁，忽略了不同注意力头的功能差异，导致关键信息被误删，从而损害模型性能。

Method: 1. 引入“语义检索头”（Semantic Retrieval Heads, SRHs）机制：不再简单聚合所有注意力头的分数，而是识别出负责捕捉初始、最终及关键中间上下文信息的特定注意力头。2. 动态缓存分配策略：根据离线估计的层级驱逐误差，为不同层分配差异化的 KV Cache 预算，从而实现更精准的资源配置。

Result: 在 LongBench 上，仅使用 3% 的 KV Cache 即可保留 97% 以上的满缓存性能；在“大海捞针”（Needle-in-a-Haystack）测试中，仅需 0.7% 的存储空间即可达到 90% 的准确率，在各项指标上均优于现有的驱逐方法。

Conclusion: CompressKV 通过识别关键语义检索头（SRH）并优化层级缓存分配，有效解决了长上下文大模型中 KV Cache 的冗余问题，在显著降低内存占用的同时保持了极高的模型性能，为资源受限环境下的长文本推理提供了一种高效的解决方案。

Abstract: Long-context large language model (LLM) inference is increasingly constrained by the memory footprint and decoding cost of key-value (KV) caches, limiting sustainable deployment on resource-constrained hardware. Existing KV cache eviction methods typically apply heuristic token scoring over all heads in GQA-based LLMs. These methods ignore the different functionalities of attention heads, leading to the eviction of critical tokens and thus degrading the performance of LLMs. To address this issue, we propose CompressKV, a resource-efficient KV-cache compression framework for GQA-based LLMs. Instead of aggregating attention scores from all heads, CompressKV identifies Semantic Retrieval Heads (SRHs) that capture both the initial and final tokens of a prompt and semantically important mid-context evidence, and uses them to select tokens whose KV pairs should be retained. Furthermore, CompressKV allocates cache budgets across layers according to offline estimates of layer-wise eviction error. Experiments on LongBench and Needle-in-a-Haystack show that CompressKV consistently outperforms existing KV-cache eviction methods across memory budgets. Notably, it preserves over 97\% of full-cache performance using only 3\% of the KV cache on LongBench question-answering tasks and achieves 90\% accuracy with just 0.7\% KV storage on Needle-in-a-Haystack. These results demonstrate an improved resource--performance trade-off for long-context LLM inference. Our code is publicly available at: https://github.com/TUDa-HWAI/CompressKV

</details>


### [99] [The Latent Bridge: A Continuous Slow-Fast Channel for Real-Time Game Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24470)
*Bojie Li,Noah Shi*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 为了解决智能代理在实时控制与深度规划之间的冲突，研究提出了一种“潜在桥接”架构，成功将慢速的推理模型与快速的反应模型深度耦合，在保持毫秒级响应的同时提升了复杂任务的决策质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在解决通用计算机智能代理在处理高难度任务（如游戏）时面临的“延迟-质量”权衡难题：推理型模型虽决策质量高但响应慢（无法满足实时控制），反应型模型虽响应快但规划能力差。研究试图寻找一种在毫秒级控制循环内实现秒级规划的方法。

Method: 提出了一种基于双模型耦合的架构，即将反应型模型（MiniCPM-o 4.5）与推理型模型（Qwen3-VL-8B-Thinking）结合。核心创新是引入“潜在桥接（Latent Bridge）”，通过映射慢速推理模型的残差（residuals）到快速模型的输入嵌入空间，替代了传统的文本接口（Text Bridge），从而避免了额外的文本解析延迟。

Result: 在7款Atari游戏和MetaDrive驾驶模拟中，Latent Bridge在所有领域均表现出优于或等同于Text Bridge的性能。在部分游戏中取得了显著提升（如MsPacman提升57%，RoadRunner提升28%），且性能表现与推理模型的优势正相关（相关系数r=0.93）。实验同时发现，混用两种桥接方式会导致性能严重下滑。

Conclusion: 该研究表明，通过学习得到的“潜在桥接（Latent Bridge）”有效地连接了推理型模型与反应型模型，在保持实时控制能力的同时显著提升了复杂任务的规划性能。该方法证明了在计算延迟与决策质量之间取得平衡的可行性，并指出桥接策略的效果高度依赖于推理模型本身对任务的适应性。

Abstract: A real-time agent for general computer use - with games as the most demanding case - must act within tens of milliseconds while still planning over seconds. These two regimes sit at opposite ends of the latency-quality tradeoff. A reasoning VLM (Qwen3-VL-8B-Thinking) deliberates effectively but requires ~1.5 s per response - far too slow for a 15 Hz control loop. In contrast, a reactive VLM (MiniCPM-o 4.5) acts in milliseconds but underperforms on planning-heavy tasks. We couple two frozen models of matched scale (9B reactive, 8B reasoning), leaving the communication channel as the sole trainable component. The standard coupling is a Text Bridge (T): the slow model writes a suffix the fast model reads. We introduce a learned continuous Latent Bridge (L) that projects the slow model's residuals into the fast model's input-embedding space in a LLaVA-style manner, avoiding any text round-trip; both are compared against Fast-Only (F). On 7 Atari games and a driving domain (MetaDrive), tuning the action decoder per channel on held-out seeds, the Latent Bridge matches or beats the Text Bridge in every domain: it significantly improves two games (MsPacman +57%, RoadRunner +28%) and is a safe drop-in elsewhere. Combining both channels interferes destructively (RoadRunner -96%), so only one should be used. The benefit is highly predictable: the bridge helps if and only if slow reasoning already beats fast reaction (T > F) - the Latent and Text gains over Fast-Only move together at r=0.93. MetaDrive is the controlled negative, where the Latent Bridge is demonstrably inert because the Text Bridge adds no value. We release replay recordings and reproducible pipelines.

</details>


### [100] [On the Smallness of the Large Language Models Scaling Exponents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24504)
*Sauro Succi,Peter V. Coveney,Alex Hansen*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文探讨了LLM扩展规律引发的能源不可持续性问题，通过分析“基座效应”并结合流体力学湍流类比，揭示了数据结构对扩展指数的影响，并指出单纯的资源堆叠难以解决其能源效率瓶颈。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前的LLM扩展规模正处于能源资源不可持续的阶段，研究人员希望通过探讨数学上的“基座效应”和类比流体力学中的湍流模型，探究扩展指数背后的物理意义，从而理解LLM扩展的可持续性瓶颈。

Method: 1. 对当前LLM扩展指数进行理论分析，讨论其能源消耗的不可持续性；2. 引入“基座效应”（pedestal effect）概念，分析将损失函数在无限数据极限下非零值考虑在内后的数学影响；3. 类比流体力学的唯象模型（phenomenological models），探讨数据平滑度（或粗糙度）如何影响模型的扩展指数。

Result: 研究发现：1. 扩展指数的大小并不受“基座效应”影响，能源消耗问题本质上是不可持续的；2. 数据的统计性质（即平滑度与粗糙度）对扩展行为起着关键作用，类似于湍流中的能量级联过程。这暗示了仅仅通过增加资源来实现模型缩放可能已接近物理极限。

Conclusion: 现有的LLM扩展规律指示了能源消耗的不可持续性；即便考虑“基座效应”（pedestal effect）修正，这种能源困境依然存在；数据的平滑度/粗糙度对扩展指数有显著影响。该研究强调了单纯依靠算力堆叠实现模型进化的局限性，并建议从数据结构和物理模型角度重新审视LLM的Scaling Laws。

Abstract: We discuss reasons why the scaling exponents of current Large Language Models (LLMs) applications are indicating an unsustainable regime in terms of energy resources. We further show that attributing the smallness of such exponents to a numerical bias due to the neglect of a non-zero value of the loss function in the limit of infinite data (``pedestal effect") does not remove the unsustainability issue. Finally, the effects of the smoothness (roughness) of the data on the scaling exponents is commented upon based on an analogy with phenomenological models of fluid turbulence.

</details>


### [101] [A specialized reasoning large language model for accelerating rare disease diagnosis: a randomized AI physician assistance trial](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24510)
*Haichao Chen,Songchi Zhou,Zhengyun Zhao,Shikai Hu,Xianghong Jin,Hongwei Ji,Li He,Shuli Li,Yiming Qin,Xin Tan,Runfeng Shi,Yih Chung Tham,Jiaye Zhu,Ye Li,Ye Jin,Longhao Cao,Dawei Li,Honghan Wu,Hongqiu Gu,Guanqiao Li,Tudor Groza,Chunying Li,Dian Zeng,Weihong Yu,Gareth Baynam,Saumya Shekhar Jamuar,Min Shen,Shuyang Zhang,Bin Sheng,Sheng Yu,Tien Yin Wong*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 研究团队开发了 RaDaR，一款针对罕见病诊断的高效 32B 参数推理模型，通过高质量合成数据训练，在多中心验证中表现优异，能显著提升医生的诊断准确率并缩短确诊周期。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 罕见病诊断因专业知识稀缺导致诊断延迟，而现有大模型在临床可部署性、医学证据基础及训练数据充足性方面存在局限。研究旨在开发一个高效、准确且可部署的专业模型，以解决医疗资源分布不均带来的诊断挑战。

Method: 研究开发了名为 RaDaR 的 320 亿参数轻量级推理型大模型。方法包括：1. 构建了由 4.9 万个真实病例和 10.4 万个合成病例组成的训练集；2. 采用推理增强训练策略（reasoning-enhanced training）；3. 利用“表型锚定叙述”（phenotype-anchored narratives）技术来增强模型对长尾罕见病的识别能力。并通过公共基准测试、多中心验证以及随机医生辅助试验对模型性能进行了全面评估。

Result: RaDaR 在性能上超越了包括 6710 亿参数 DeepSeek-R1 在内的多种主流模型。在回顾性分析中，RaDaR 能在 61.06% 的病例中提前给出正确诊断，平均缩短 1.87 个月的诊断时间。在临床随机试验中，该模型将医生的诊断准确率提高了 21.44 个百分点，显著优于仅使用互联网搜索的辅助效果。

Conclusion: RaDaR 证明了轻量级、推理驱动的 LLM 在处理罕见病诊断这类低数据资源任务中的有效性。该研究提供了一个可部署的临床辅助工具，并建立了一个在数据匮乏环境下开发诊断 AI 的可复用框架，对于缓解罕见病诊断难的临床挑战具有重要意义。

Abstract: Rare diseases affect millions of individuals worldwide, yet timely diagnosis remains a major public health challenge due to scarcity of specialized clinical expertise. While large language models (LLMs) show promise to support rare disease diagnosis, current models are constrained by insufficient clinical deployability, limited clinically grounded evidence, and scarcity of training data. Here we present RaDaR (Rare Disease navigatoR), an open-source, compact reasoning LLM (32B parameters) for rare disease diagnosis. RaDaR was trained with 49,170 publicly available free-text cases and 104,666 synthetic cases with reasoning-enhanced training. RaDaR showed the strongest performance among evaluated open-source models, including the 671B DeepSeek-R1, across public benchmarks and four external validation centers. In a retrospective cohort, RaDaR prioritized the final diagnosis before documented clinical suspicion in 61.06 percent of cases, corresponding to a potential lead time of 1.87 months and 50.18 percent of the within-center interval. In a randomized physician-assistance trial, RaDaR assistance improved physicians' rare-disease diagnostic accuracy by 21.44 percentage points compared with internet search alone. Synthetic-data ablations suggested that phenotype-anchored narratives provide useful training signal for long-tail rare diseases, with a monotonic scaling trend within the tested data range. Together, RaDaR and its development and validation framework provide a deployable rare-disease reasoning model and a reproducible development framework for diagnostic AI under data scarcity.

### [102] [Reinforcement Learning for Computer-Use Agents with Autonomous Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24515)
*Marta Sumyk,Oleksandr Kosovan*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 针对图形用户界面智能体在强化学习中缺乏监督信号的问题，本文提出了一种利用视觉语言模型进行自动化奖励评估的框架，并通过建模评估噪声显著提升了智能体在桌面环境下的任务表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在计算机使用智能体（CUA）的强化学习过程中，缺乏可扩展且机器可读的奖励信号是一个核心瓶颈。由于桌面环境任务往往依赖视觉判断，手工设计奖励函数或获取大规模人工标注非常困难，因此需要一种自动化的、可扩展的任务评估机制。

Method: 提出了一种基于视觉语言模型（VLM）的强化学习微调框架，利用VLM对任务结束时的屏幕截图与原始指令进行评估，自动生成任务完成的反馈信号。同时，针对自动评估器可能存在的不确定性，通过将反馈建模为带噪声的二元奖励通道，引入了一种去噪奖励估计器，并将其应用于近端策略优化（PPO）算法。

Result: 在 macOSWorld、Windows Agent Arena 和 OSWorld 等多个基准测试中，经去噪修正后的评估器奖励优于零样本基准及未经修正的原始评估器奖励。平均任务成功率较零样本表现提升了12.6个百分点，较使用原始评估器奖励微调提升了5.1个百分点。

Conclusion: 通过显式建模并修正多模态评估器的噪声，自动化的视觉语言评估可以成为图形用户界面（GUI）环境下强化学习的有效且可扩展的奖励信号。该研究表明，尽管自主评估器存在缺陷，但通过去噪机制可以显著提升智能体在复杂桌面环境中的任务完成率。

Abstract: Computer-Use Agents (CUAs) execute high-level user goals by perceiving and acting directly within graphical user interfaces. However, reinforcement learning for CUAs remains difficult because open-ended desktop environments rarely provide scalable, machine-readable reward signals: task success is often visually grounded and hard to specify with handcrafted reward functions or dense manual labels.
  We propose an RL fine-tuning framework that uses autonomous vision-language evaluation as a scalable supervision signal for GUI agents. Given a final screenshot and the original instruction, a Vision-Language Model judges task completion and provides terminal feedback without task-specific heuristics or manual labels during policy optimization.
  Because autonomous evaluators are imperfect, we model their feedback as a noisy binary reward channel and derive a noise-corrected reward estimator for Proximal Policy Optimization. Experiments across macOSWorld, Windows Agent Arena, and OSWorld show that corrected evaluator rewards outperform both zero-shot baselines and raw evaluator rewards, improving success rates by an average of 12.6 percentage points over zero-shot performance and 5.1 points over raw evaluator fine-tuning. These results suggest that autonomous evaluation can serve as a practical reward signal for RL in GUI environments when evaluator noise is explicitly modeled and corrected.

### [103] [Governed Shared Memory for Multi-Agent LLM Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24535)
*Yanki Margalit,Nurit Cohen-Inger,Erni Avram,Ran Taig,Oded Margalit*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文探讨了多智能体大模型系统中的共享内存管理问题，提出了MemClaw这一系统级解决方案，通过引入四种控制原语有效解决了数据泄露、过时及矛盾等问题，并强调了在生产环境中对系统架构进行实证评估的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在多智能体大模型环境中，缺乏对共享知识管理的鲁棒机制。研究旨在解决多智能体协作中出现的未经授权泄露、过时信息传播、矛盾持久化以及来源信息丢失等问题，以弥补单纯依赖长上下文检索的局限性。

Method: 本文定义了“舰队内存问题”（fleet-memory problem）及其四种基础故障模式。为了解决这些问题，提出了四种系统级原语：作用域检索（scoped retrieval）、时间替代（temporal supersession）、来源追踪（provenance tracking）和策略管控的内存传播（policy-governed memory propagation）。研究人员开发了名为MemClaw的生产级多租户内存服务，并利用ArgusFleet测试套件对治理维度进行了实测。

Result: MemClaw成功实现了100%深度为四的来源链重构，实现了零跨舰队数据泄露；通过测试发现了诸如“非对称作用域执行”和“流水线顺序冲突”等生产级架构问题，证明了在真实生产环境下进行治理维度测试的必要性。

Conclusion: 对于生产环境中的多智能体系统，单纯依赖长上下文检索已无法满足需求。受控共享内存需要明确的系统级抽象，且通过真实环境评估对于发现设计阶段难以察觉的执行机制和流水线顺序故障至关重要。

Abstract: Multi-agent LLM environments require robust mechanisms for shared knowledge management. This paper formalizes the fleet-memory problem and identifies four foundational failure modes: unauthorized leakage, stale propagation, contradiction persistence, and provenance collapse. To address these, we define explicit systems-level primitives: scoped retrieval, temporal supersession, provenance tracking, and policy-governed memory propagation. These primitives are implemented in MemClaw, a production multi-tenant memory service, and evaluated via ArgusFleet, a reproducible harness testing four governance dimensions. Rather than a baseline comparison, this study measures a live production service, emphasizing real-world architectural insights and negative results. Key Evaluation Results Provenance: Successfully reconstructed 100% of depth-four derivation chains with correct writer identity at sub-second per-hop latency. Propagation: Demonstrated high intra-fleet visibility with zero cross-fleet leakage. Under strong write mode, write-to-visible latency was optimized to a single search round-trip. Production Architectural Issues Discovered Asymmetric Scope Enforcement: Tenant isolation held, but sub-tenant scope was initially bypassed on direct GET-by-id requests for agent-scoped credentials (disclosed and remediated during the study). Pipeline Ordering Conflict: While contradiction supersession works for admitted writes, a synchronous near-duplicate gate can prematurely reject contradictory writes before the asynchronous contradiction detector can evaluate them. Conclusion: Long-context retrieval alone is insufficient for production multi-agent memory. Governed shared memory demands explicit systems-level abstractions, and live evaluation is vital to expose enforcement and pipeline-ordering failures missed by design-only treatments.

### [104] [GUI vs. CLI: Execution Bottlenecks in Screen-Only and Skill-Mediated Computer-Use Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24551)
*Xiao Zhou,Siyue Zhang,Yilun Zhao,Jinbiao Wei,Tingyu Song,Arman Cohan,Chen Zhao*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个公平对比图形界面（GUI）与命令行界面（CLI）智能体的基准测试，研究发现GUI代理长流程交互更难，而CLI代理受限于工具库覆盖范围。通过扩充技能库，CLI代理的表现可超越GUI代理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的计算机智能体评估往往混淆了交互模式（GUI与CLI）与任务差异、初始状态及验证方式等变量，缺乏受控的公平比较，难以明确不同交互模式的优劣势与瓶颈。

Method: 构建了一个包含440个桌面任务的基准测试集，覆盖18个应用和12个工作流类别，确保GUI代理和CLI代理在相同目标、状态和验证机制下进行评估，仅在操作交互模式上有所区别。

Result: 在受控测试中，GUI代理的最高成功率为59.1%，超过了基准CLI代理（48.2%）；但引入验证器引导的技能增强后，CLI代理的成功率提升至69.3%，证实了技能库覆盖率对CLI代理表现的关键影响。

Conclusion: 图形用户界面（GUI）代理的主要瓶颈在于长流程任务中的可靠交互，而命令行界面（CLI）代理的瓶颈在于工具库的覆盖范围和扩展性。通过对两种模式的对比，研究指出目前的CLI代理性能不足主要归因于技能库的不完整，而非模型本身能力的局限。

Abstract: Computer-use agents can execute software tasks through either graphical interfaces or programmatic command interfaces, but existing evaluations confound interaction modality with differences in tasks, initial states, verifiers, and permitted actions. We introduce a matched execution-layer benchmark of 440 desktop tasks across 18 applications and 12 workflow categories, where screen-only GUI agents and skill-mediated CLI agents receive identical goals, states, and final-state verifiers while being restricted to modality-native actions. In this controlled setting, the strongest GUI agent reaches a 59.1% full pass rate, outperforming the strongest original-skill CLI agent at 48.2%; however, verifier-guided skill augmentation raises CLI success to 69.3%, showing that much of the CLI deficit comes from incomplete skill coverage rather than model capability alone. These results suggest that GUI and CLI expose different execution bottlenecks: GUI agents are limited by reliable grounded interaction over long-horizon workflows, whereas CLI agents are limited by the coverage and scalability of their skill interfaces.

</details>


### [105] [Quant Convergence: Bridging Classical Value Investing and Modern Factor Models for Systematic Equity Selection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24575)
*Augusto Eiji Yamazaki,Hugo Garrido-Lestache Belinchon*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本研究通过将格雷厄姆价值投资规则与机器学习结合，证明了经典的“安全边际”原则能有效防止AI在金融预测中盲目追逐高波动市场噪声，从而构建出更稳健且高收益的投资模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代机器学习模型在金融预测中常因过度拟合市场短期噪声，导致忽视具备长期价值的企业。研究旨在验证经典的格雷厄姆价值投资法则能否作为一种“低通滤波器”，引导AI模型规避高风险波动。

Method: 研究构建了三组特征（纯格雷厄姆指标、现代市场因子、两者混合），并使用XGBoost和AutoGluon等复杂模型在20年标普500数据上进行训练。通过实施四年期的买入持有策略，对比了各模型的收益率、最大回撤及卡尔玛比率（Calmar Ratio）。

Result: 在测试期间，纯格雷厄姆随机森林模型实现了最高的总体回报（232.13%）且风险较低（卡尔玛比率为1.38）；混合随机森林模型则以202.91%的收益实现了测试组中最低的最大回撤（34.53%）；相比之下，尽管AutoGluon收益较高，但由于过度暴露于波动性资产，遭受了显著的回撤。

Conclusion: 本研究证实了本杰明·格雷厄姆的“安全边际”理念并未过时，将其作为数学约束引入现代机器学习模型，能有效抑制模型对市场噪声的过度拟合，从而在保持高收益的同时显著降低投资风险。

Abstract: Modern finance relies heavily on complex machine learning models to find patterns in the stock market. However, as these AI models get more complicated, they often memorize short-term market noise instead of finding companies with real, lasting value. We designed this research to test if Benjamin Graham's classic value investing rules could act as a mathematical "low-pass filter" to keep these modern models in check. We built three different sets of features - pure Graham rules, modern market factors, and a mix of both - and tested them against highly complex models (XGBoost and AutoGluon) using 20 years of S&P 500 data. By applying a strict buy-and-hold strategy over a four-year test period (March 2022 to March 2026), the results showed that more complex algorithms do not always win. While the AutoGluon model captured high returns (222.68%), it suffered a substantial 39.78% drop because it bought volatile tech stocks right before the market crashed. On the other hand, the pure Graham Random Forest achieved the highest overall return (232.13%) with much less risk (1.38 Calmar Ratio). Furthermore, the Combined Random Forest successfully mixed momentum with Graham's rules, making a 202.91% return while keeping the lowest maximum drop (34.53%) of any model tested. Ultimately, this research proves that Graham's "margin of safety" isn't outdated; it is actually a highly effective way to prevent modern AI from taking on too much risk.

### [106] [LLMs Prompted for Legal Context Object More: Overrefusal from Small On-Premises LLMs in Criminal Legal Context](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24585)
*Anastasiia Kucherenko,François Brouchoud,Dimitri Percia David,Andrei Kucharavy*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本研究探讨了小型LLM在法律应用中的“过度拒绝”现象。结果显示，添加权威身份前缀会大幅增加模型拒绝回答法律相关问题的概率，表明此类模型在法律语境下的表现极不稳定，容易产生职业性偏差，亟需针对性研究以提高其可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管大型语言模型在法律领域的应用存在争议，但法律从业者已开始将其作为翻译和重构工具。然而，模型对特定话题的“过度拒绝”可能造成处理偏差，进而影响法律工作的效率与公正。因此，本研究旨在预判并探究小型终端部署LLM在法律语境下产生过度拒绝倾向的原因。

Method: 研究者选择了多种适用于端侧设备的小型主流LLM，通过引入不同的前缀（包括权威身份前缀如“最高法院助理”、辩护律师身份，以及已知的功能性诱导/越狱前缀），对比其在处理法律提示词时的拒绝频率，进而评估不同语境对模型过度拒绝行为的影响。

Result: 研究发现，使用“最高法院助理”或“辩护律师”等权威身份前缀会使模型的拒绝率系统性地提高2到20倍。相比之下，已知的功能性诱导前缀对拒绝率的影响则不尽相同，在不同模型中表现出极大的差异性。这证实了模型对语境框架极其敏感，且表现不稳定。

Conclusion: 研究表明，小型本地化部署的语言模型（LLM）在面对法律领域的特定语境设定（如权威身份前缀）时表现出高度的不稳定性。这种“过度拒绝”现象可能导致法律专业人士在使用这些工具时面临偏差，因此，在法律辅助工具的开发和部署中，必须深入研究并解决这一不稳定性，以确保其在实际应用中的可靠性与公平性。

Abstract: While the validity of LLMs' use in the legal context remains subject to ethical and legal debate, legal professionals are already experimenting with personal LLMs, if only for translation and reformulation. However, even such a seemingly innocuous use can introduce biases through case processing speed if LLM assistants selectively refuse assistance on certain topics. To better anticipate such biases, we investigate several modern small LLMs that are most likely to be used as on-device assistants, to assess the impact of overrefusal on legal prompts.
  Surprisingly, we find that authority-style prefixes (``you are acting as an assistant of the national supreme court'', ``[...] defense lawyer'') systematically increase refusal rates by 2--20x over the no-prefix baseline, while a known role-play jailbreak prefix shows mixed effects, sharply increasing refusals in some models and barely shifting them in others. The finding suggests that small on-prem deployable LLMs are unstable under contextual framings that a real institutional user might naturally introduce, and further investigation is essential to minimize opportunities for bias.

### [107] [AdversaBench: Automated LLM Red-Teaming with Multi-Judge Confirmation and Cross-Model Transferability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24589)
*Khanak Khandelwal*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了AdversaBench，一个用于大模型红队测试的自动化端到端框架，通过结构化提示词变异和多判官评估系统，揭示了模型在推理、指令遵循及工具使用中的普遍性脆弱点，并证实了对抗性提示词具备跨模型迁移性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大模型的对抗性评估缺乏规模化手段，且在评估结果的真实性确认上存在可靠性问题。作者旨在构建一个端到端的红队测试流程，以自动化生成困难输入并可靠地识别模型失效。

Method: 提出AdversaBench框架，包含五个结构化算子用于变异种子提示词，通过三个判官组成的评估小组并辅以元判官（Meta-judge）来确认模型失败，对推理、指令遵循和工具使用三个领域的45个种子提示词进行了实验验证。

Result: 实验表明：1. 算子有效性因任务类别而异；2. 指令遵循任务比其他任务更难攻击，平均需要更多迭代次数；3. 判官之间虽然存在较高的一致性，但标签偏差导致Cohen's kappa较低；4. 对抗性提示词展现出显著的零样本跨模型迁移能力。

Conclusion: AdversaBench提供了一个高效的端到端红队测试流程，证明了通过结构化提示词变异和多判官机制可以有效评估大模型的鲁棒性。研究发现对抗性提示词具有跨模型迁移能力，暗示了模型普遍存在的行为缺陷，而非单一模型的特异性弱点。

Abstract: Scaling adversarial evaluation of large language models requires both a method for generating hard inputs and a reliable way to confirm that resulting failures are real. We present AdversaBench, an end-to-end red-teaming pipeline that mutates seed prompts with five structured operators, queries a target model, and confirms failures through a three-judge panel with a meta-judge tiebreaker. We report experiments on 45 seeds across three categories: reasoning, instruction-following, and tool use. Every seed produced a confirmed failure. Four findings stand out. First, operator effectiveness varies sharply by category: inject_distractor scores 0.00 mean reward on instruction-following seeds but 0.80-0.83 on reasoning and tool-use. Second, binary failure rate hides difficulty: instruction-following seeds required 2.4 attacker iterations on average versus 1.1 for other categories, a gap visible in survival curves. Third, pairwise judge agreement of 80-87% coexists with near-zero Cohen's kappa due to label skew; category-level disagreement rates are more informative. Fourth, adversarial prompts generated against Llama 3.1 8B transfer zero-shot to Llama 3.3 70B, suggesting the mutations exploit general behavioral patterns rather than model-specific weaknesses. Code, dataset, and analysis scripts are available at https://github.com/khanak0509/AdversaBench .

</details>


### [108] [ASALT: Adaptive State Alignment for Lateral Transfer in Multi-agent Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24601)
*Anurag Akula,Satheesh K. Perepu,Abhishek Sarkar,Kaushik Dey*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为ASALT的多智能体强化学习迁移方法，通过嵌入式适配器映射解决了跨域间状态空间维度不匹配的问题，实现了高效的策略迁移并缓解了负迁移挑战。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的多智能体强化学习迁移方法大多要求源域和目标域具有相同的观察空间和全局状态空间维度，这限制了模型在现实复杂任务中的通用性。本文旨在解决跨域迁移中状态空间维度不匹配的问题。

Method: 提出了ASALT（Adaptive State-Action Level Transfer）方法。该方法引入了观察适配器（Observation-level Adapter）和状态适配器（State-level Adapter），将目标域的观察和全局状态映射到一个共享的嵌入空间，从而使得异构领域间的策略（演员和评论家）能够进行有效的知识迁移。

Result: 在多个标准基准环境下的实验表明，ASALT在协作场景下的样本效率和全局收益方面均优于现有基准方法。研究还发现，ASALT能有效抑制负迁移，尽管其性能在一定程度上受到源域和目标域之间失配程度的影响。

Conclusion: 本文提出的ASALT方法通过引入观察和状态层面的适配器，成功解决了多智能体强化学习中跨域迁移时状态空间维度不匹配的难题，显著提升了策略迁移的样本效率并减少了负迁移现象。实验证明该方法在处理异构环境时具有良好的有效性。

Abstract: Multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) addresses the problem of training multiple agents that pursue collaborative, competitive, or mixed objectives. Prior work has investigated transfer learning between source and target domains in MARL; however, the majority of existing approaches impose the constraint that the dimensionalities of the observation space and the global state space must be identical across domains. In this paper, we introduce a method that explicitly accommodates mismatched state-space dimensionalities between source and target domains. The proposed approach, ASALT, incorporates both observation-level and state-level adapters that map the target-domain observations and global states into a shared embedding space, thereby enabling more effective transfer of knowledge across both actors and critics. These adapters can generate embeddings that support efficient strategy transfer across heterogeneous domains. Experimental results on multiple configurations in standard benchmark environments demonstrate that ASALT surpasses existing baselines in terms of sample efficiency and global return in cooperative settings, but its effectiveness depends on the degree of mismatch between source and target domains. Furthermore, our findings indicate that ASALT mitigates negative transfer, which frequently constitutes a major obstacle when transferring policies between domains with differing observation and action spaces.

### [109] [Uncertainty-Aware Longitudinal Forecasting of Alzheimer's Disease Progression Using Deep Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24604)
*Arya Hariharan,Shreyank N Gowda,Anala M R*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种用于阿尔茨海默病进展建模的概率预测框架，通过结合有序回归、多步轨迹生成及不确定性分解技术，在实现高准确度诊断预测的同时，为临床医生提供了可量化的长期病程演变预测及不确定性分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前的深度学习方法多将阿尔茨海默病预测简化为单步分类问题，忽略了疾病演变的连续性、阶段间的有序性，且缺乏对预测结果不确定性的有效量化，难以满足临床医生对患者长期病程演变及预测置信度的评估需求。

Method: 该研究开发了一种结合有序诊断预测、多步轨迹生成和不确定性分解的概率深度学习框架。核心组件包括：1. 经过调整的时间融合Transformer（Temporal Fusion Transformer），引入CORAL有序输出层、非对称损失加权及转换器过采样，以捕捉疾病阶段的序数关系；2. 自回归混合密度网络（MDN），基于患者上下文表示生成为期五年的多维度概率预测（含诊断、CDR-SB、MMSE及海马体体积）；3. 通过分析混合方差和Bootstrap集成技术，实现对偶然性（aleatoric）和认知性（epistemic）不确定性的分离与估计。

Result: 在ADNI数据集上，该模型在下一次访视的诊断预测方面优于线性和循环神经网络等基准模型，特别是在MCI（轻度认知障碍）向痴呆转化的鉴别上表现突出。生成的五年轨迹不仅符合预期的病理演变规律，且不确定性估计（90%置信区间）具有良好的校准性。实验表明，认知性不确定性在罕见病例及外部数据集（OASIS-3）验证中能有效与预测误差同步增长。

Conclusion: 该研究提出的概率预测框架能够有效地模拟阿尔茨海默病（AD）的长期进展，不仅提高了诊断准确性，还通过量化不确定性增强了预测的临床实用价值，为个体化的疾病管理提供了可靠的决策支持工具。

Abstract: Longitudinal modelling of Alzheimer's disease progression is clinically useful only if it can describe not just the most likely next diagnosis, but how a patient may evolve over time and how reliable that forecast is. Most deep learning approaches reduce this problem to single-step classification, treating cognitively normal, mild cognitive impairment, and dementia as flat categories while providing limited insight into how uncertainty accumulates across future visits. We propose a probabilistic framework that combines ordinal diagnosis prediction, multi-horizon trajectory generation, and decomposed uncertainty estimation. A Temporal Fusion Transformer encoder is adapted with a CORAL ordinal output layer, asymmetric loss weighting, and converter oversampling to respect disease-stage ordering and improve sensitivity to MCI-to-dementia transitions. Conditioned on the learned patient-context representation, an autoregressive Mixture Density Network generates five-year probabilistic trajectories for diagnosis state, CDR Sum of Boxes, MMSE orientation, and hippocampal volume. On ADNI, the model outperforms linear, recurrent, and transformer baselines for next-visit diagnosis prediction, with the strongest gains on MCI-versus-dementia discrimination. Generated trajectories achieve near-nominal 90% credible interval coverage, widening uncertainty across the forecast horizon, and biomarker dynamics consistent with expected Alzheimer's disease progression. We further separate aleatoric from epistemic uncertainty using analytic mixture variance and a five-member bootstrap ensemble, which provides the strongest encoder diversity and output-level epistemic signal. Epistemic uncertainty is higher for rare progression archetypes, MCI and dementia patients, and under external evaluation on OASIS-3, where it increases alongside prediction error.

### [110] [ScaleToT: Generalizing Structured LLM Reasoning for Billion-Scale Low-Activity User Modeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24605)
*Tianbao Ma,Chang Xi,Yichuan Zou,Chengen Li,Linxun Chen,Zilong Lu,Yanan Niu,Zhaojie Liu,Han Li,Kun Gai*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: ScaleToT 是一种将大语言模型的结构化推理能力高效迁移至轻量级模型的方法，解决了低活跃用户画像稀疏导致的建模难题，在实现显著性能提升的同时大幅降低了计算成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的用户建模严重依赖丰富的历史交互数据，无法覆盖数以亿计的低活跃用户；尽管 LLM 能从静态画像中推断用户状态，但在数据稀疏场景下推理不可靠，且对全体用户直接使用 LLM 进行推理的计算成本极高。

Method: 提出了一种名为 ScaleToT 的方法：首先，利用受限熵引导的“思维树”（ToT）推理技术在少量样本上构建高质量的类型化用户状态链；其次，利用这些推理链通过监督微调（SFT）和“结果驱动的段感知隐式奖励策略优化”（OSIPO）训练学生模型；最后，将学生模型的推理表示迁移至轻量级用户画像编码器，从而在无需 LLM 推理的情况下为海量用户提供高效推理信号。

Result: 在亿级用户规模的广告投放场景中，ScaleToT 在 30 天生命周期价值（LT30）预测任务中实现了 6.738% 的显著提升，同时仅需覆盖 7.32% 的用户群体进行离线推理，极大地降低了计算开销。

Conclusion: ScaleToT 通过将大规模语言模型的复杂推理能力迁移到轻量级模型，有效地解决了低活跃用户在个性化建模中因交互数据稀疏而导致的推理能力不足和计算成本高昂的问题，在工业级大规模应用中具有显著的效能与经济价值。

Abstract: Accurate user modeling often depends on rich interaction histories, which are unavailable for billions of low-activity users. Large Language Models (LLMs) can infer latent user states from static profiles, but this reasoning becomes unreliable when profiles are sparse, and applying an LLM to billions of users is prohibitively expensive. We present ScaleToT, which learns structured reasoning from a small LLM-processed subset and extends it to the broader low-activity user population. To improve reasoning reliability, ScaleToT constructs typed user-state chains with a bounded entropy-guided Tree-of-Thought (ToT) refinement procedure. To make this structured reasoning usable from sparse profiles, the teacher-curated chains are used to train a student model on static profiles through supervised fine-tuning (SFT) and Outcome-Driven Segment-Aware Implicit Reward Policy Optimization (OSIPO). ScaleToT then transfers the student's reasoning representations to a lightweight profile encoder, providing shared reasoning signals for the remaining users without LLM inference. We evaluate ScaleToT on lifetime value (LTV) prediction in a billion-scale advertising deployment. A randomized online A/B test increased LT30 by 6.738\%, while offline reasoning covered only 7.32\% of the potential population, greatly reducing compute cost compared with full-population reasoning.

</details>


### [111] [AI Tokenomics: The Economics of Tokens, Computation, and Pricing in Foundation Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24616)
*Quanyan Zhu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了“AI代币经济学”框架，旨在通过整合技术成本与经济模型，深入剖析大模型中代币的生产、消费与价值创造机制，揭示了代币支出与实际经济价值之间的本质区别，并为该领域的未来研究方向提供了路线图。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着大模型服务的普及，Token已成为衡量AI系统计算、内存、能耗及经济价值的实际基础单位。然而，目前缺乏一套系统性的理论框架来理解和管理这些代币的生成、消费、定价与优化，因此亟需研究AI代币经济学以指导资源配置与价值评估。

Method: 本研究开发了一个综合性的分析框架，通过系统地连接代币级的技术成本与工作流级的生产函数，结合企业资源配置模型、测量仪表技术及市场设计理论，从技术-经济交叉视角对AI服务中的代币效能进行了建模和分析。

Result: 研究指出，代币支出并不直接等同于经济价值。代币的价值受边际生产力、在工作流中的位置、隐藏的推理活动（如思维链）、相关风险及下游传播效应等多种复杂因素影响，必须通过多维指标进行综合评估。

Conclusion: 该研究强调了建立“AI代币经济学”框架的必要性。代币不仅是技术消耗的度量单位，更是连接AI生产函数与经济决策的核心要素。未来研究应聚焦于隐藏推理成本的测量、代币生产力的定量分析以及代币化市场的机制设计。

Abstract: Tokens have become the practical accounting unit for modern foundation model services, linking information processing, computation, memory use, energy expenditure, pricing, and economic value. This paper develops a framework for AI tokenomics: the study of how tokens are generated, consumed, priced, allocated, and optimized across AI systems. We connect token-level technical costs to workflow-level production functions, enterprise resource allocation, measurement and instrumentation methods, and emerging market-design questions. The framework shows that token expenditure and economic value are distinct: value depends on marginal productivity, workflow position, hidden reasoning activity, risk, and downstream propagation effects. The paper concludes by identifying open research directions in hidden-token measurement, empirical calibration, token productivity, dynamic allocation, and token-based markets.

</details>

While this extension does not lead to an increased complexity of the problems of interest, it is able to express minimally complete abstractions, hence perfect abstractions when they exist. ### [115] [SAFARI: Scaling Long Horizon Agentic Fault Attribution via Active Investigation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24626)
*Chenyang Zhu,Jiayu Yao,Kushal Chawla,Youbing Yin,Nathan Wolfe,Pengshan Cai,Jingyu Wu,Spencer Hong,Sangwoo Cho,Shi-Xiong Zhang,Daben Liu,Sambit Sahu,Erin Babinsky*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了 SAFARI 框架，通过工具辅助的诊断循环与短期记忆机制，突破了 LLM 在处理超长代理轨迹时的上下文限制，显著提升了复杂多步任务中的故障归因效率与准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着自主代理任务复杂度增加，执行轨迹往往超出模型上下文窗口限制。传统方法将全量轨迹加载至上下文会导致注意力稀释（Attention dilution）且无法处理超长序列，导致诊断失效。

Method: 提出 SAFARI 框架，摒弃了将全量轨迹线性加载进上下文的方法。该框架利用工具增强的诊断循环（Tool-augmented diagnostic loop），使 LLM 能够主动读取、搜索轨迹片段，并配备持久化的短期记忆（STM）进行跨轮推理。

Result: 在 Who&When 数据集（1M token 预算下）性能提升 20%，在 TRAIL GAIA 子集（25K token 预算下）性能提升 19%。在故障点位于模型原生上下文窗口 5 倍之外的场景下，SAFARI 仍能保持 0.58 的精确度。

Conclusion: SAFARI 证明了通过工具增强的诊断循环来解耦长序列轨迹诊断与模型上下文限制是有效的，为解决长跨度代理任务的故障归因问题提供了一种鲁棒且高效的新范式。

Abstract: As autonomous agents tackle increasingly complex multi-step, multi-agent tasks, their execution trajectories have scaled beyond the constraints of even the largest context windows. Current methods for effectively diagnosing agent failures load the full trajectory into an LLM's context window, which suffers from attention dilution and fails when agentic traces inevitably exceed context limits. To address this, we introduce SAFARI (Scaling long-horizon Agentic Fault AttRibution via active Investigation), a framework that replaces linear context loading with a tool-augmented diagnostic loop. By equipping LLMs with a specialized toolbox to read and search trajectory segments alongside a persistent Short-Term Memory (STM) for cross-turn reasoning, SAFARI effectively decouples diagnostic accuracy from architectural context limits. Our experiments demonstrate that SAFARI outperforms state-of-the-art results by 20% on the Who&When dataset within a 1M token budget, and by 19% on TRAIL GAIA subset on a 25K token budget. Most significantly, SAFARI maintains a 0.58 precision even when the target fault resides 5x beyond the model's native context window, a scenario where traditional evaluators fail entirely.

Abstract: Cinematographic captioning aims to describe how a video is filmed using professional film-language concepts such as camera movement, shot size, depth of field, composition, and shooting angle. This capability is important for fine-grained video understanding and controllable movie-quality video generation, yet remains underexplored in existing multimodal large language models. Unlike question-answering-based evaluation of cinematic understanding, cinematographic captioning requires a unified open-form description over multiple cinematographic dimensions. This task is challenging for two main reasons: the model must infer professional cinematographic concepts from subtle visual evidence, and it must generate captions that are both comprehensive and accurate. Accordingly, we propose CineCap, a framework that combines structured reasoning with spatio-temporal anchors and reinforcement learning with comprehensiveness, accuracy, and gated coverage rewards. The former grounds professional cinematographic descriptions in explicit visual evidence and organizes them into compact atomic reasoning for supervised fine-tuning, while the latter improves the balance between descriptive completeness and factual correctness. In addition, we construct CineCap Bench, a benchmark of 472 manually annotated video-caption pairs for systematic evaluation. Extensive experiments show that CineCap consistently outperforms strong proprietary and open-source baselines, establishing a new state of the art for cinematographic captioning. The code, model checkpoint, and benchmark are publicly available in https://github.com/Hectormxy/CineCap.git.

### [117] [LaGO: Latent Action Guidance for Online Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24669)
*Kuan-Yen Liu,Ren-Jyun Huang,Ti-Rong Wu*

Main category: cs.AI

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究多将大型语言模型（LLM）直接作为控制器进行规划和决策，但这种方式对动作生成的精确度要求极高，且在实际应用中往往不够稳定可靠。因此，研究人员希望探索一种更稳健的方法来利用LLM的知识。

Method: LaGO（Latent Action Guidance for Online Reinforcement Learning）：该方法不直接使用LLM生成动作，而是将其作为“潜在行动先验”对在线策略优化进行软性引导。通过在PPO算法的基础上引入LLM的先验信息，平衡了模型本身的决策与预训练知识的辅助。

Conclusion: LaGO框架证明了将预训练大型语言模型作为潜在行动先验，而非直接充当控制器，能够有效增强在线强化学习的规划和决策能力。实验结果显示，该方法在离散和连续控制任务中均能显著提升策略的性能。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have shown strong potential for planning and sequential decision-making, but prior work often relies on using them as direct controllers, which requires precise action generation and can be unreliable in practice. This paper proposes Latent Action Guidance for Online Reinforcement Learning (LaGO), a framework that uses a pretrained LLM as a latent action prior to softly guide online policy optimization, rather than treating the LLM as an explicit planner or controller. Experiments on both a discrete-control benchmark, CLEVR-Robot, and a continuous-control benchmark, Meta-World, demonstrate that LaGO consistently improves both reward and success rate over Vanilla PPO. In particular, LaGO increases the average success rate from 15.1% to 27.2% on CLEVR-Robot and from 2.7% to 15.2% on Meta-World. Our analysis further shows that stronger pretrained LLMs provide more effective guidance, suggesting that LLM knowledge can improve planning and online decision-making.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: In many decision-making scenarios, acquiring information incurs different costs. We consider the problem of constructing a deterministic evaluation strategy that minimizes the expected cost of evaluating a propositional formula under variable costs and a probability distribution over truth assignments. We present a branch-and-bound algorithm with variable-selection heuristics, pruning, and caching. To the best of our knowledge, it is the first practical exact algorithm for this level of generality. Experiments on random instances demonstrate scalability and quantify the efficiency-quality trade-off of a greedy beam-search variant. We additionally evaluate a structured heart-disease diagnosis instance. Finally, we prove that the problem is $\#P$-hard and contained in $\mathrm{PSPACE}$.

### [119] [Decentralised AI Training and Inference with BlockTrain](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24722)
*Peter Toth*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了Spheroid BlockTrain，一种去中心化的AI训练协议。它通过将模型分块训练来规避对中心化超级计算集群的依赖，使分散的计算资源能够协同训练大规模模型，在保证模型性能的同时大幅降低了对基础设施的特定要求。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前的尖端AI训练高度依赖集中的高性能加速器集群，这使得算力资源被少数超大规模企业垄断，限制了开源和独立AI研究的发展。该研究旨在解决这种基础设施依赖问题，探索如何通过去中心化手段降低训练门槛。

Method: 提出了一种去中心化的训练协议“Spheroid BlockTrain”，该协议将模型分割为多个独立的块，每个工作节点仅负责训练特定的块，通过本地目标函数进行优化，并在推理阶段将这些块组合成一个完整的模型。它避免了存储完整的优化器状态，并利用HTTP/TCP传输进行跨节点通信。

Result: 在byte-level WikiText任务中，BlockTrain达到了1.359的交叉熵（困惑度3.89），与端到端Transformer基准仅相差0.04。实验证明该方法在分布式网络环境下（跨越公共IP的节点）能有效进行模型更新，并支持高达75.8B参数的模型推理，且在广域网推理性能上优于传统的流水线并行方案。

Conclusion: Spheroid BlockTrain证明了通过将模型划分为独立的训练块，可以在去中心化、受限的网络基础设施上实现大规模AI训练，打破了大型科技公司对高性能算力集群的垄断，为开源和独立AI研究提供了一种可扩展的新路径。

Abstract: Frontier AI training is increasingly shaped by access to dense, centrally controlled accelerator clusters. This creates a structural advantage for hyperscalers and large centralized laboratories, and makes open or independent AI efforts depend on scarce capital, privileged infrastructure, and data-center geography. We present Spheroid BlockTrain, a decentralized training protocol in which a model is partitioned into independently trainable blocks, each optimized on a local objective derived from the same global target and composed at inference into one model. On byte-level WikiText, BlockTrain reaches cross entropy 1.359 (perplexity 3.89), within about 0.04 CE of a same-setup end-to-end Transformer reference, while each active worker trains only one block and avoids full-model optimizer state. A shared six-worker block training run reaches CE 1.385 by averaging same-block updates into one assembled model. HTTP/TCP transport experiments move real serialized checkpoints and updates, including a public-IP three-host run that improves CE from 5.580 to 1.811 while moving 15.22 GB. For inference, the current BlockTrain path uses one block-stack traversal per full output and serves over direct TCP across three public-network GPU hosts up to a 75.80B-parameter logical fp16 shape, outperforming a matched plain-autoregressive TCP pipeline baseline because it emits a full sequence per WAN pipeline traversal rather than one token per traversal.

</details>


### [120] [Scaling Laws for Task-Specific LLM Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24747)
*Lavinia Ghita,Dhruv Desai,Ioana Boier*

Main category: cs.AI

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型（LLM）虽然性能强大，但其庞大的规模在对延迟和成本有严格要求的实际应用中造成了部署障碍，因此需要量化研究模型压缩对领域特定性能与通用性能的影响，以优化部署策略。

Method: 研究采用定量金融作为应用领域，比较了基于Logit和LoRA的蒸馏方法，并结合迭代结构化剪枝技术；提出了一种混合链式思维（CoT）监督损失函数，用于稳定推理路径上的KL散度蒸馏。

Result: 实验表明，模型在领域内任务质量随压缩程度呈可预测的退化趋势，而通用知识则在压缩初期便迅速崩溃；研究发现监督形式是影响这一权衡的关键，链式思维（CoT）监督能有效恢复被剪枝过程削弱的通用知识能力。

Conclusion: 该研究确立了领域特定LLM压缩的经验扩展法则，揭示了压缩过程中领域知识与通用知识之间权衡的关键因素，并证明了链式思维（CoT）监督在缓解压缩损失方面的核心作用，为资源受限场景下的模型部署提供了系统的指导框架。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) achieve strong performance across a growing range of domains, yet their scale poses deployment challenges in applications where latency and cost constraints are critical. This paper derives empirical scaling laws for domain-specific LLM compression, quantifying how in-domain and general knowledge performance scale with dataset size, compression ratio, supervision format, and iterative pruning schedule. Using quantitative finance as our application domain, we compare logit-based and LoRA-based distillation under iterative structural pruning, introducing a blended chain-of-thought supervision loss that stabilizes KL-divergence distillation over reasoning traces. In-domain task quality degrades predictably under compression while general-knowledge benchmarks collapse well before the same point; supervision format is the key driver of this tradeoff, with chain-of-thought supervision actively recovering general knowledge that pruning erases. We release the headline dataset FinHeadlineMix, scaling law results, and practical recommendations to provide a reusable framework for domain-specific compression decisions.

</details>


### [121] [Can Scale Save Us From Plasticity Loss in Large Language Models?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24752)
*J. Fernando Hernandez-Garcia,Tomás Figliolia,Beren Millidge*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文研究揭示了现代Transformer大模型在长时间训练后会面临“可塑性丧失”的问题，即无法持续高效学习新信息。虽然增加模型规模可以延缓这一现象的显现，但无法从根本上消除它。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 针对现代Transformer架构的大型语言模型（LLM）是否仍存在“可塑性丧失”这一长期困扰神经网络持续学习的基本挑战，以及该现象在现代自然语言处理场景中的表现规律进行系统性研究。

Method: 研究人员在多语言持续学习任务上对参数规模从5M到314M的GPT风格Transformer模型进行了测试，通过观察模型在越南语探测任务（probing task）上的性能表现来量化和测量可塑性的丧失。

Result: 研究发现：1. 可塑性丧失在现代Transformer模型中普遍存在；2. 可塑性丧失的发生遵循可预测的缩放定律，随模型规模增大呈次线性增长；3. 即使在平稳的多语言训练（非突发任务切换）中，可塑性丧失现象依然存在。

Conclusion: 即使是大规模的Transformer语言模型，在经过长时间训练后，无论是在持续学习场景还是平稳的多语言训练场景下，最终都会丧失高效适应新数据的能力（即丧失可塑性）。仅依靠增加参数规模不足以彻底解决这一问题。

Abstract: The loss of plasticity - the ability of a network to learn new information after having already learned older information - is a fundamental challenge in creating artificial neural networks capable of continual learning. Although this phenomenon has been known for decades, it has mostly been studied in older, relatively small architectures and rarely in natural-language domains. To determine whether loss of plasticity remains a problem in the modern transformer-based LLM paradigm, we study plasticity loss in GPT-style Transformer models trained on a multilingual continual learning problem. Consistent with prior work, we find evidence of plasticity loss across models ranging from 5M to 314M non-embedding parameters, as measured by deterioration on a held-out Vietnamese probing task. We further find that the onset of plasticity loss follows a predictable scaling law, growing sublinearly with model size. These results suggest that larger models may delay the measurable effects of plasticity loss, but that increasing parameter count alone is likely to be insufficient to completely prevent it. We also find evidence of plasticity loss under stationary multilingual training, challenging the view that the phenomenon is exclusive to continual learning with abrupt task changes. Overall, our results suggest that even large Transformer language models trained on natural-language will eventually lose the ability to efficiently adapt to new data after sufficiently long training, in both continual and stationary settings.

### [122] [BluTrain: A C++/CUDA Framework for AI Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24780)
*Adhitya Charan,Adwaid Suresh,Anuj Kumar,Aparna A,Dhanakumar K,Dharun M S,Dinesh G,Goutham Kumar Reddy K,Harshini V M,Jenifa D,Jona Delcy C A,Kathirvel S,Killi Uma Maheswara Rao,Kiruthik Kanna M,Kurra Vishnu Sai,Madhumithaa G K,Navin Kumar,Ram Charan Golla,Revathi T,Rishikkanth R,Sanjay Krishna M,Surendra Vendra*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: BluTrain 是一个基于 C++ 和 CUDA 原生构建的深度学习训练框架，通过深度系统优化显著提升了训练吞吐量并降低了内存占用，证明了底层硬件控制对大规模深度学习性能的核心影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 作者认为深度学习的进展在规模化阶段更多是系统工程问题而非单纯的模型建模问题。现有的训练框架往往难以平衡硬件表达与系统复杂性，导致模型在训练时的性能（吞吐量、内存占用等）受限，因此旨在通过构建一个轻量级、架构通用的高性能底层训练框架来解决这些局限。

Method: 该研究采用从第一性原理（First Principles）出发的方法，使用标准 C++ 和核心 CUDA 编程模型构建了名为 BluTrain 的训练框架。其核心组件包括：类型化张量模块（带反向自动微分）、线性代数库、缓存分配器、多模式分布式执行模块，以及基于 MLIR 的深度学习编译器。

Result: 在 8-GPU (6000 Ada) 系统上训练 124M 参数的 GPT-2 模型时，BluTrain 表现优于业界标准基准（PyTorch）：吞吐量提升至平均 407K tokens/s（PyTorch 为 395K tokens/s），内存占用减少了 22%，且在保持数值保真度的同时实现了更低的验证损失。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了通过从底层重新构建训练框架，可以有效解决深度学习中模型架构与硬件表现之间的性能瓶颈。BluTrain 展示了在保持数值保真度的前提下，通过原生系统级优化实现更高吞吐量和内存效率的可行性。

Abstract: Progress in deep learning is, at scale, more a matter of systems engineering than of modelling: the behaviour of a model in training (its throughput, its memory footprint, and the numerical fidelity of the result) is determined less by the architecture itself than by how that architecture is expressed on the hardware. To achieve absolute control over this hardware expression while abstracting away systems complexity to make modelling seamless and eliminating the need for repetitive orchestration logic, BluTrain was architected from first principles as a robust, lightweight, and architecture-general training framework in standard C++ and the core CUDA programming model. Every layer is implemented natively: a typed tensor module with reverse-mode autograd, a linear-algebra library, a caching allocator, a multi-mode distributed-execution module, and an MLIR-based deep-learning compiler. In formal evaluations training a 124M-parameter GPT-2 baseline in FP32 on an 8-GPU 6000 Ada system, BluTrain outperforms industry-standard baselines in both throughput (sustaining an average of 407K tokens/s versus PyTorch's 395K tokens/s) and memory efficiency (achieving up to a 22% footprint reduction), while strictly preserving numerical fidelity and converging to a marginally lower final validation loss. With every layer explicitly open to native tuning, the performance ceiling is the framework's own to raise.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 研究发现多样性偏移是造成模型性能下降的核心因素，且现有的领域泛化算法在这些分布偏移面前表现欠佳，与传统的经验风险最小化（ERM）基线相比仅有微弱优势。

Abstract: While the field of Human Activity Recognition (HAR) continues to draw interest from researchers and advance in important ways, some key challenges remain. While data diversity in HAR has been well-acknowledged in the literature, there remains a gap in understanding the effect of various types of distribution shifts on HAR models and the domain generalization problem that arises. Towards that end, this paper systematically evaluates 4 different types of distribution shifts, including variations in device type, sensor placement, sampling rate, and user behavior. Quantifying their effects, we illustrate that diversity shifts predominantly define all types of shifts, indicating the existence of unique features that are not shared across different domains. We then introduce a uniform HAR-based distribution shift benchmarks and conduct a comprehensive evaluation of up to 28 domain generalization methods. Our analysis exposes the limitations of current domain generalization algorithms in achieving model generalizability, marginally outperforming the empirical risk minimization baseline. This work represents the first systematic exploration of domain generalization and adaptation concerning specific distribution shifts in sensor-based HAR, offering an open-source benchmark platform and datasets to spur further research.

### [124] [Solving Inverse Problems of Chaotic Systems with Bidirectional Conditional Flow Matching](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24824)
*Peiyan Hu,Jian Zhang,Jiashu Pan,Ruiqi Feng,Tao Zhang,Zhi-Ming Ma,Yuan-Sen Ting,Gongjie Li,Tailin Wu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为双向条件流匹配（Bi-CFM）的新框架，有效解决了混沌系统逆问题中不适定性及误差累积的难题，并针对物理守恒律引入了约束机制，在多个高维混沌系统和天体物理案例中实现了性能与效率的双重提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 混沌系统中的逆问题（如从最终状态推断初始状态）因不适定性、非唯一性、不稳定性以及时间反演动力学的混沌特性而难以求解。现有的方法在面对长时程混沌演化时，难以克服误差累积和计算效率低下的问题。

Method: 本文提出了“双向条件流匹配（Bi-CFM）”，通过学习初始状态和最终状态分布之间的双向映射来捕获混沌演化的随机性，从而缓解误差指数级累积。针对物理系统，进一步提出了“受守恒约束的Bi-CFM（CBi-CFM）”，确保模型符合物理守恒定律。

Result: Bi-CFM在洛伦兹系统及洛伦兹96系统等测试中，在五个分布级度量指标上超越了现有基线模型，计算速度提升了两个数量级以上。CBi-CFM在三体散射问题中表现出极佳的守恒律遵从性，并在长达100亿年的球状星团演化观测中取得了显著的精度突破。

Conclusion: Bi-CFM及其变体CBi-CFM为解决混沌系统中的长期逆向动力学问题提供了一种高效、精确且可扩展的新框架，特别是在处理具有守恒定律的大规模、长时程混沌演化问题上表现优异，具备重要的科学应用价值。

Abstract: Modeling chaotic systems is crucial yet challenging. Inverse problems in chaotic dynamics, namely inferring initial conditions from final states, remain largely unsolved because of ill-posedness, non-uniqueness, instability, and potentially chaotic time-reverse dynamics. We address this open problem with Bidirectional Conditional Flow Matching (Bi-CFM), which learns bidirectional mappings between distributions of initial and final states to capture the stochasticity of chaotic evolution and mitigate exponential error accumulation over time. Furthermore, for systems with conservation laws, we extend it to Conservation-constrained Bi-CFM (CBi-CFM). Across the classic Lorenz, Circuit, and high-dimensional Lorenz 96 systems, Bi-CFM improves five distribution-level metrics over baselines while achieving a speedup of more than two orders of magnitude. In the three-body planet-planet scattering problem in planetary dynamics, CBi-CFM better respects conservation laws, with conservation errors comparable to those of the ground truth. Finally, on real observations of globular clusters, collisional million-body systems shaped by $\sim 10^{10}$ years (10 Gyr) of evolution, our method represents an advance in accuracy, establishing a scalable route to solving inverse problems of long-timescale real-world chaotic dynamics.

### [125] [Difference-Making without Making a Difference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24832)
*Sander Beckers*

Method: 通过对Andreas与Günther提出的七种实际因果定义的逻辑结构进行比较分析，探讨它们在实际因果归因中的表现，并通过关键案例检验其定义的一致性与有效性。

Result: 研究发现，该作者提出的最新定义实际上同时涵盖了三种分类，否定了分类的有效性；同时，通过对比分析显示，该定义在关键案例中的应用失败，从而削弱了该系列所有七种定义的可靠性。

I show that their most recent - factual difference-making - definition instantiates all three types, thereby proving that these are distinctions without a difference. I further compare their novel account to the other six accounts on several crucial examples, revealing that this undermines all seven of their accounts.

### [126] [Accuracy and Satisfaction in Multi-Turn LLM Dialogues for NFR Assessment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24834)
*Ali Pourghasemi Fatideh,Wilder Baldwin,Maria Dhakal,Collin McMillan,Sepideh Ghanavati*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究评估了LLM助手在处理HIPAA合规性等非功能性需求时的表现，发现虽然开发者倾向于信任LLM，但其准确性依然存疑，且交互中的响应长度与信息量对用户满意度有显著负面影响。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究采用了受控实验方法，招募了49名程序员与GitHub Copilot进行多轮对话，针对iTrust代码库中的148个HIPAA相关非功能性需求（NFR）进行评估。研究通过分析需求满足度、推理逻辑和代码定位三个维度，对比了LLM的输出与专家基准真相，并建立了用户满意度模型以评估交互质量。

Result: 研究发现：1. 开发者在评估中易盲目认同LLM的结论，但LLM对比专家基准的准确性较低；2. 用户满意度受交互模式影响：较长的回复和冗余的信息交互会降低满意度，而积极主动的互动则能提升满意度。

Conclusion: 针对非功能性需求（NFR）的LLM对话系统设计需要平衡信息量与交互质量。开发者对LLM的评估存在过度依赖倾向，因此提升LLM在复杂领域（如合规性）推理的准确性，以及优化其交互的主动性和简洁性，是未来提升系统性能的关键方向。

Abstract: LLM-based dialogue assistants have become mainstream tools for software developers, yet current evaluation benchmarks focus exclusively on functional correctness. This leaves a critical gap in assessing the quality and accuracy of these conversations when handling Non-Functional Requirements (NFRs), which are inherently vague, context-dependent, and involve many parts of a program. Evaluating how well these systems support collaborative reasoning about NFRs requires methods that go beyond single-turn accuracy to capture both the correctness of the system's outputs and the quality of the multi-turn interaction. In this paper, we investigate the accuracy and quality of multi-turn conversations between developers and an LLM-based agent in the domain of Health Insurance Portability and Accountability Act (HIPAA) regulatory compliance. We hired 49 programmers to interact with GitHub Copilot to assess 148 HIPAA-derived NFRs against the iTrust codebase, a system designed to comply with HIPAA regulations, across three dimensions: requirement satisfaction level, reasoning, and code localization. We find that developers tend to agree with LLM assessments, but accuracy against expert ground truth is low. We model user satisfaction and find that longer system responses and more information-providing turns negatively affect user satisfaction, whereas proactive interactions positively affect it. Our findings provide insights for designing LLM-based dialogue systems that support NFR assessment.
