### [164] [NeuroSonic: Conditional Flow Matching for EEG-to-Speech Reconstruction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24087)
*Wenhao Gao,Yifan Wang,Yijia Ma,Carl Yang,Wen Li,Chenyu You*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: NeuroSonic是一种基于条件流匹配的EEG转语音重建框架，通过学习确定性的概率流轨迹而非传统的随机生成，显著提高了跨受试者语音重建的鲁棒性、频谱保真度和感知质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 直接从头皮脑电图（EEG）重建连续语音极具挑战性，因为EEG信号微弱、空间弥散且高度多变，与具有复杂结构的语音信号之间存在严重的语义映射不匹配问题。现有的波形回归和随机生成方法在面对伪影和主体差异时容易变得不稳定。

Method: 提出了一种名为NeuroSonic的条件流匹配框架。该方法将EEG和音频嵌入到共享的令牌空间中，利用时间条件门控Transformer参数化常微分方程，学习从噪声状态到清晰语音的确定性概率流速度场，从而避开了迭代随机采样过程。

Result: 在CineBrain和EAV基准测试中，NeuroSonic在跨受试者评估中表现优于现有的GAN、扩散模型和均值流模型，整体感知质量提升高达26.3%，尤其在伪影严重且条件变化显著的片段中表现出极强的鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 确定性条件传输（NeuroSonic）为EEG驱动的语音重建提供了一种比传统随机生成模型更稳定、更有效的方法，特别是在处理含噪和高度变化的EEG信号时具有显著优势。

Abstract: Reconstructing continuous speech from scalp electroencephalography (EEG) remains fundamentally challenging. EEG provides a weak, spatially diffuse, and highly variable measurement of distributed cortical activity, whereas speech is organized as a coherent acoustic trajectory with strong harmonic and temporal structure. The resulting mismatch makes waveform regression unstable and causes stochastic multi-step generation to be sensitive to artifact-dependent conditioning and subject variability. We introduce NeuroSonic, a conditional flow-matching framework for EEG-to-speech reconstruction. Instead of predicting waveforms directly or refining them through stochastic denoising, NeuroSonic learns a deterministic probability-flow velocity field that transports a noise-corrupted acoustic state toward clean speech under EEG conditioning. EEG and audio are embedded into a shared token space and processed by a time-conditioned gated Transformer that parameterizes the transport ordinary differential equation. This formulation models trajectory evolution explicitly while avoiding iterative stochastic sampling. We evaluate NeuroSonic on the CineBrain and EAV benchmarks under cross-subject evaluation. Across both datasets, the proposed method improves distributional realism, spectral fidelity, and perceptual quality over representative GAN-, diffusion-, and mean-flow baselines, with up to a 26.3\% gain in overall perceptual quality. The performance gap is most evident in artifact-heavy segments, where conditioning variability is strongest. These findings indicate that deterministic conditional transport provides a stable and effective formulation for EEG-driven speech reconstruction. Code is available at https://github.com/Y-Research-SBU/NeuroSonic/ .

</details>


### [165] [FedUP: One-Shot Federated Unlearning via Centroid-Guided Plug-in Filters](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24113)
*Feihong Nan,Zhengyi Zhong,Pan Wang,Weidong Bao,Xiongtao Zhang,Quan Wen,Ji Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了 FedUP，一种基于轻量级插件过滤器的单次联邦去学习框架，通过冻结模型参数和使用差分隐私质心样本，解决了传统去学习方法在处理延迟、性能损失和可逆性方面的难题，实现了高效、精准且可逆的知识遗忘。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的联邦去学习（FU）方法在处理“被遗忘权”合规性时，往往需要在非目标知识损失（模型性能下降）与高去学习请求延迟之间进行权衡，且通常涉及复杂的计算和通信成本。作者旨在解决这一性能与效率的矛盾，以满足实际场景对快速、精准去学习的需求。

Method: 提出了一种名为 FedUP 的单次联邦去学习框架。该方法通过冻结原始模型参数，在服务端使用经过差分隐私（DP）保护的类别质心样本训练轻量级“插件式”过滤器（Knowledge Funnel），从而过滤掉目标数据，无需进行多轮客户端-服务端交互或复杂的重新训练。该插件化设计同时也保证了去学习过程的可逆性。

Result: 实验证明，FedUP 将去学习延迟从分钟级缩短至秒级。在多个图像和文本任务上，该方法有效地减少了非目标知识的损失，并展现出了卓越的去学习精度和计算效率。此外，其可逆性特性允许通过移除过滤器即时恢复模型性能，具有良好的应用前景。

Conclusion: FedUP 提供了一种高效、可逆且隐私友好的联邦去学习方案，通过轻量级过滤器实现了高性能与低延迟的平衡，为解决联邦学习中的“被遗忘权”合规性问题提供了切实可行的路径。

Abstract: Federated unlearning (FU) is critical for complying with legal mandates like the right to be forgotten in decentralized systems, yet current methods face a persistent dilemma between non-target knowledge loss and high request latency. To resolve these issues, we propose FedUP, a one-shot federated unlearning framework utilizing lightweight pluggable filters that act as a "knowledge funnel" to screen out target data while preserving original model performance. By freezing original model parameters and training filters at the server side using differentially private (DP)-protected class centroid samples, FedUP bypasses the need for multi-round client-server communication and complex retraining, reducing unlearning latency from minutes to mere seconds. Additionally, the framework's pluggable architecture ensures inherent reversibility, enabling the seamless restoration of forgotten knowledge by simply removing the filters. Extensive experiments on diverse image and text tasks demonstrate that FedUP effectively reduces non-target knowledge loss and achieves superior unlearning precision and efficiency across various scenarios. Code is available at: https://github.com/suows/FedUP-code.

### [166] [When Top-1 Fails: Calibrating LoRA Monitors for Masked Diffusion LMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24119)
*Lucky Verma,Pratik Yadav*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究发现，离散扩散语言模型微调时常用的top-1置信度指标无法预警模型坍缩，建议采用最大LoRA梯度范数作为早期监测手段。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 离散扩散语言模型（DLM）的微调过程中，尽管可以使用去噪时间的置信度监视器进行诊断，但这些指标在参数高效微调（PEFT）场景下的有效性尚未经过验证。该研究旨在探究是否存在可靠的早期指标来预测DLM微调中的坍缩风险。

Method: 研究人员通过816种不同的LoRA/PEFT配置，测试了三种DLM家族。首先评估了top-1 argmax置信度（作为坍缩警告）的有效性，随后评估了最大LoRA梯度范数（一种基于参数端的信号），并通过训练优化的阈值在LLaDA模型族上验证了其区分高损耗配置的能力，并将其与自回归基线进行了对比。

Result: top-1 argmax置信度指标的准确率为0，存在严重的“虚报”问题，即该指标在训练初期就已饱和，无法反映后续的坍缩情况。相反，监测最大LoRA梯度范数在LLaDA系列上表现出较好的判别能力，其F1分数达到0.79，精确度为0.68，显著优于top-1 baseline。

Conclusion: 在离散扩散语言模型（DLM）的PEFT微调中，基于token生成的top-1 argmax置信度指标无法有效预警模型坍缩，因为它存在预平衡饱和问题。相比之下，监测LoRA梯度范数能够更好地反映训练稳定性，可作为一种早期预警信号。研究建议放弃使用top-1指标，转而采用梯度范数并根据模型家族校准阈值来评估训练状态。

Abstract: Discrete diffusion language model (DLM) fine-tuning inherits inexpensive diagnostics from denoising-time confidence monitors, but their PEFT-training meaning is untested. We test top-1 argmax concentration as a collapse warning. Across 816 LoRA/PEFT configurations from three DLM families, the warning fires for every configuration while logs record 0/816 actual collapses at the 200 step horizon, giving zero precision. The cause is pre-equilibrium saturation: top-1 concentration is already high before optimization and quickly becomes insensitive to final training stability. We then evaluate max LoRA gradient norm, a parameter-side signal that samples gradient routing rather than token concentration. On a pooled held-out LLaDA-family split, a train-optimized threshold identifies top-decile final-loss configurations with precision 0.68 and F1=0.79, above the all-positive top-1 baseline even at the lower split-bootstrap confidence bound. Autoregressive controls and cross-family threshold failures bound the result to short-horizon DLM-LoRA inspection rather than a universal collapse detector. Workflow: drop top-1 as a PEFT alarm, log max-gradient early in training, and calibrate thresholds per DLM family before routing runs for inspection.

### [167] [Holistic Data Scheduler for LLM Pre-training via Multi-Objective Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24133)
*Chenhao Dang,Jing Ma,Mingjie Liao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: HDS是一种利用强化学习和多目标奖励函数（数据、损失、模型权重）进行在线数据混合的新型框架，在大幅提升训练效率的同时，显著优化了大模型的最终性能。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的在线数据混合（ODM）方法大多局限于单一的优化视角，忽略了大型语言模型预训练中数据构成的复杂性和动态性。为了解决这一局限，作者旨在开发一种能够从多维度视角动态调整数据混合比例的综合调度框架。

Method: 提出了一种名为“整体数据调度器”（HDS）的在线数据混合框架。该方法将数据调度建模为连续空间中的强化学习问题，并利用软演员-评论家（SAC）算法进行求解。其核心在于一个多目标整体奖励函数，该函数综合了数据质量（数据驱动）、跨领域影响（损失驱动）以及权重范数（模型驱动）三个关键维度。

Result: 在The Pile基准测试中，HDS以减少44%训练迭代次数的代价达到了现有最佳方法的验证困惑度水平；同时在MMLU 0-shot任务中取得了7.2%的性能提升，并在多个基准测试中表现出持续的性能优势。

Conclusion: HDS证明了通过多维度奖励函数和强化学习进行在线数据调度，能够显著提升大语言模型的训练效率和最终性能，为复杂预训练任务中的数据策略优化提供了新的范式。

Abstract: The composition of training data, governed by the diversity of sources and their mixing strategy, is a cornerstone of Large Language Model (LLM) pre-training. Online Data Mixing (ODM), the technique of adaptively adjusting data mixtures during training, has emerged as a promising direction to improve efficiency. However, existing methods are constrained by their reliance on a singular optimization perspective, which fundamentally overlooks the need for complex LLM pre-training to consider the dynamic data composition from multiple dimensions. To overcome this limitation, we introduce the Holistic Data Scheduler (HDS), a novel online data mixing framework. HDS formulates the data scheduling challenge as a reinforcement learning problem in a continuous control space and leverages the Soft Actor-Critic (SAC) algorithm for its stability and sample efficiency in exploring the high-dimensional policy space. At the core of HDS lies a novel multi-objective, holistic reward function that integrates three critical perspectives: a data-driven reward for quality, a loss-driven reward capturing inter-domain influence, and a model-driven reward based on weight norms. To validate our design and determine its optimal configuration, we conducted systematic experiments on LLMs of various sizes. On The Pile benchmark, HDS reaches the final validation perplexity of the next best method with 44% fewer training iterations. Furthermore, it achieves a 7.2% improvement on the MMLU 0-shot task along with consistent gains on other benchmarks, showcasing its ability to enhance both training efficiency and final model capability.

### [168] [A Time-Reparameterized Cumulative Intensity Extrapolation Sampler for Discrete Flow Matching](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24140)
*Feiyang Fu,Hehe Fan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种针对离散流匹配（DFM）的高效采样算法TR-CIE，通过时间重参数化和累积强度外推优化采样过程，在不增加计算开销的前提下，显著提升了有限函数评估次数（NFE）限制下的生成质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 离散流匹配（DFM）在离散状态空间生成建模方面表现优异，但在实际应用中，常用的τ-leaping采样方法在有限函数评估次数（NFE）限制下，采样效率和质量仍有很大提升空间。现有研究缺乏针对低NFE预算下高效采样算法的深入探索。

Method: 提出了“时间重参数化累积强度外推”（TR-CIE）采样器。该方法包含两部分：1. 基于时间表的重参数化（Time Reparameterization），通过缩放时间网格吸收噪声计划中的增长项，缓解终端采样阶段的刚性问题；2. 累积强度外推更新规则（Cumulative-Intensity Extrapolation），利用历史模型输出缓存来优化非均匀时间网格上累积强度的近似精度。

Result: 实验结果显示，TR-CIE在合成任务、文本生成及文本转图像等多个基准测试中，在极低NFE的限制下均优于标准的τ-leaping采样方法。在保持与τ-leaping相同NFE（每步一次）的情况下，能够更准确地逼近目标分布，提升生成样本的质量。

Conclusion: TR-CIE是一种针对离散流匹配（DFM）的高效采样框架。通过时间重参数化和累积强度外推技术，该方法在不增加额外模型评估次数（NFE）的前提下，显著提升了低NFE预算下的采样质量。理论分析证实了其局部误差界限及收敛性，实验证明了其在离散生成任务中的优越性。

Abstract: Discrete flow matching (DFM) provides a principled framework for generative modeling on discrete state spaces via continuous-time Markov chain dynamics. In practice, sampling for DFM commonly employs discretizations such as $τ$-leaping, yet efficient sampling methods under a limited number of function evaluations (NFE) remain less studied. To address this gap, we propose the Time-Reparameterized Cumulative Intensity Extrapolation (TR-CIE) sampler, which aims to improve sampling quality when function evaluations are restricted. TR-CIE consists of two components. First, a schedule-based time reparameterization rescales the time grid according to the noise schedule. Under standard factorized DFM rate parameterizations, this transformation of variables absorbs the schedule-dependent growth term and mitigates stiffness near the terminal sampling stage. Second, we introduce a cumulative-intensity extrapolation updating rule. By reusing cached model outputs from the previous step as a history term, this improves the approximation of stepwise cumulative intensities on the resulting non-uniform time grid. We provide a theoretical analysis that bounds the local approximation error of cumulative intensities and establishes convergence results. The resulting sampler requires one NFE per step and introduces no additional model evaluations compared to the standard $τ$-leaping sampler. Extensive experiments on synthetic tasks, text generation, and text-to-image benchmarks demonstrate that our method improves sampling quality under limited NFE.

### [169] [AsyncOPD: How Stale Can On-Policy Distillation Be?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24143)
*Wonjun Kang,Kevin Galim,Seunghyuk Oh,Minjun Kang,Sanghyun Park,Donghoon Kim,Minjae Lee,Minseo Kim,Rishabh Tiwari,Yuchen Zeng,Hyung Il Koo,Kangwook Lee*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本论文研究了在大语言模型异步策略蒸馏（OPD）中引入的陈旧数据问题。研究发现，选择不同的KL散度方向对陈旧数据具有不同的鲁棒性，并提出了一种名为AsyncOPD的异步流水线，通过优化梯度估计和缓存策略，在保持模型精度的同时，将训练吞吐量最高提升了3.8倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 策略蒸馏（OPD）在大语言模型后训练中日益重要，但其在线训练模式存在严重的系统瓶颈，即 rollout 生成过程拖累训练速度。虽然异步训练可缓解此问题，但会引入“陈旧数据（stale-policy data）”问题，目前学术界缺乏对异步OPD中陈旧数据影响的系统性研究。

Method: 1. 对比分析了前向KL与反向KL在陈旧策略数据下的表现；2. 针对反向KL的脆弱性，验证了在学习器端重新计算梯度信号的有效性；3. 分析了有限教师评分缓存带来的偏差-方差权衡，并引入多采样蒙特卡洛（MC）估计器；4. 构建并开源了AsyncOPD异步训练流水线。

Result: 实验结果表明，AsyncOPD相比严格同步训练，在达到同等精度的前提下，训练吞吐量提升了1.6倍至3.8倍。此外，研究证实前向KL在处理陈旧数据时表现更为鲁棒，而对于反向KL，在学习器端重算信号是一种简单且有效的改进方式。

Conclusion: 本研究通过系统分析异步策略蒸馏（OPD）中的陈旧数据问题，提出了针对不同KL散度方向的优化策略，并引入了多采样蒙特卡洛方法来平衡偏差与方差。研究成果AsyncOPD在不损失模型准确性的前提下，显著提升了训练吞吐量，为大规模语言模型的离线策略蒸馏提供了一种高效且可扩展的解决方案。

Abstract: On-policy distillation (OPD) trains a student on its own rollouts guided by teacher feedback and is becoming increasingly important for large language model (LLM) post-training. Like reinforcement learning (RL), however, OPD faces an on-policy systems bottleneck, as rollouts can dominate training time for reasoning workloads. Asynchronous training pipelines can alleviate this bottleneck by decoupling rollout generation from learner updates, but doing so introduces stale-policy data. While prior work has studied stale data in asynchronous RL, its effects in OPD remain underexplored. We present the first systematic study of staleness in asynchronous OPD, focusing on a practical setting where teacher feedback is implemented through local KL losses and full-vocabulary teacher logits are too expensive to store or transfer, necessitating finite teacher-score caches. We first show that KL direction changes the stale-data problem: teacher-weighted forward KL is more robust to stale rollouts, whereas student-weighted reverse KL is vulnerable. Second, for this vulnerable reverse-KL case, we study whether methods designed to stabilize asynchronous RL can mitigate OPD staleness. In our experiments, they do not improve over a simpler OPD-specific surrogate: recomputing the reverse-KL signal under the current student at learner time. Third, we analyze how finite teacher-score caches create a bias-variance tradeoff for sparse and sampled reverse-KL OPD estimators. This motivates multi-sample Monte Carlo (MC), which preserves MC correctability while reducing one-sample variance. Finally, we present and open-source AsyncOPD, a fully asynchronous OPD training pipeline built from these estimator choices. Experiments show that AsyncOPD improves training throughput by $1.6\times$ to $3.8\times$ over strict synchronous training while reaching comparable accuracy.

</details>

Abstract: On-device fault detection enables real-time diagnostics without cloud dependency, but deploying machine learning models on resource-constrained hardware demands careful tradeoffs between accuracy, latency, and model size. We evaluate classification performance (F1-score, AUC), model size, and CPU inference latency, and further assess INT8 dynamic quantization and a two-stage adaptive inference pipeline. Our results reveal that on well-separated sensor data (C-MAPSS), lightweight transformers match traditional ML at 87.8% F1 but at 100x the model size and 9000x the latency. TinyBERT-4L emerges as the most deployment-friendly transformer at 55 MB and 18 ms CPU latency. INT8 quantization reduces size by 25% while preserving 86.9% F1. Our adaptive pipeline, routing 97.9% of predictions through a quantized triage model and only 2.1% to a larger expert, achieves 87.6% F1 at 19.5 ms average latency. On severely imbalanced datasets (SECOM, UCI-PM), both traditional and transformer methods struggle significantly, highlighting fundamental limitations of current approaches for extreme class imbalance in fault detection. All code is publicly available.

### [171] [Project Ariadne: Prompt-Conditioned Route Generation for Synthesis Planning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24184)
*Anton Morgunov,Victor S. Batista*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Ariadne是一个新型的端到端逆合成路线生成器，它通过统一的提示词引导，能在无需重新训练模型的情况下，根据深度和起始物料等约束条件高效规划合成路径，实现了性能与计算效率的显著提升。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的逆合成规划通常依赖于迭代的单步反应模型或复杂的搜索算法，且往往需要针对不同的约束条件调整模型架构或训练专门的模型，这限制了方法的灵活性与通用性。研究者希望通过序列生成范式，构建一个能够根据提示词灵活规划合成路线的通用模型。

Method: 提出了一种名为Ariadne的仅解码器（decoder-only）架构的序列生成模型。该模型将目标分子、可选的约束条件以及最终的合成路线整合为一个单一的提示-补全（prompt-completion）序列，从而实现端到端的路线生成，无需为不同的约束规格训练专门的模型。

Result: 在RetroCast/PaRoutes基准测试中，Ariadne表现出色：通过引入提示词，其深度约束Solv-0指标提升了13.7个点，特定起始物料约束提升了31.2个点；在计算效率上，Ariadne以约24分钟的GPU时间超越了需要6.8小时的DESP规划器；在标准重建任务中，其性能与DMS Explorer XL相当，但推理速度快了一倍。

Conclusion: Ariadne证明了基于提示词的序列生成模型在逆合成路线规划中具有巨大潜力，能够通过单一架构灵活处理不同的约束条件（如路线深度和起始物料限制）。尽管在某些指标上尚未完全超越传统的蒙特卡洛树搜索（MCTS）方法，且路线验证工具仍是该领域的主要瓶颈，但该工作为构建更通用的、可控的逆合成预测系统开辟了新路径。

Abstract: Retrosynthetic planning seeks to connect a target molecule to commercially available starting materials through a multistep route. Classical planners construct such routes by iteratively applying single-step reaction models within a search procedure; constrained variants often require specialized algorithms or architectural changes. Direct route generation reframes retrosynthesis as sequence generation, but existing direct-generation methods still train separate models for different planning specifications. We introduce Ariadne, a decoder-only route generator that represents the target, optional constraints, and route in one prompt-completion sequence. On the RetroCast/PaRoutes mkt-cnv-160 benchmark family, one 24-layer checkpoint follows route-depth and required-starting-material prompts: adding the corresponding prompt fields raises Solv-0 by 13.7 points for depth constraints and 31.2 points for required-leaf constraints. Ariadne also improves over DESP, a bidirectional search planner, on required-leaf Top-10 and Solv-0 in 24 GPU-minutes versus 6.8 GPU-hours. On standard reconstruction, Ariadne is comparable to DMS Explorer XL at about half the reported inference time. Across additional target-only benchmarks, Ariadne's clearest gains are on route-holdout reconstruction, whereas AiZynthFinder MCTS remains stronger on several Solv-0 comparisons. These results extend sequence generation from specialist retrosynthesis models to prompt-conditioned structural route generation. We release the codebase and training scripts to support further work, but do not introduce Tier-1--3 route checkers; those remain the main bottleneck before models of this kind can become useful to experimental chemists.

### [172] [Managing Task Execution for Unknown Workloads in Batteryless IoT: A Hardware-Agnostic Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24340)
*Samer Nasser,Henrique Duarte Moura,Ritesh Kumar Singh,Maarten Weyn,Jeroen Famaey*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对无电池物联网设备的能量管理难题，本文提出了两种无需先验信息的动态调度策略（强化学习和近似预测），并分析了其在不同硬件资源约束下的适用性与性能权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 物联网（IoT）正向无电池、能量收集架构转型。然而，由于能源供给极度不稳定且传统调度器依赖静态阈值或预先设定的任务配置文件，难以应对日益复杂的边缘计算工作负载。因此，研究旨在开发无需先验能源信息的通用动态调度策略以增强系统韧性。

Method: 提出了两种硬件无关的动态调度策略：1. 基于模型无关的强化学习（RL）代理，用于平衡生存能力与执行效率；2. 实时近似预测（AP）方法，通过黑盒方式动态处理任务。研究采用真实的太阳能数据和LoRa传输剖面，通过高保真模拟框架进行评估。

Result: 研究表明，AP方法在任务吞吐量上接近最优（near-oracle），且计算开销轻量；RL智能体具备灵活的生存与执行平衡调节能力；AsTAR策略在应对长周期的能量中断方面表现优异。研究揭示了各种策略在不同硬件配置下的性能权衡。

Conclusion: 论文指出不存在一种通用的最优策略，调度方法的选择应取决于系统的硬件约束。在电容较小的受限系统中，RL或AP等高级调度策略对于维持弹性至关重要；而在具备较大能量缓冲的设备中，简单的静态策略因计算开销更低反而更为高效。

Abstract: In recent years, the Internet of Things (IoT) paradigm has been shifting toward batteryless, energy-harvesting architectures. Sustaining reliable operation in these systems requires intelligent management of highly volatile stored energy. As edge applications grow in complexity, traditional energy-aware schedulers struggle with unpredictable workloads due to their reliance on static execution thresholds or pre-measured, hardware-specific task profiles. To overcome this, we propose two novel, hardware-agnostic dynamic scheduling strategies treating applications as a "black box," requiring no prior energy information: a model-free Reinforcement Learning (RL) agent and an on-the-fly Approximated Prediction (AP) method. We evaluate these methods against an adaptive task rate approach (AsTAR) and optimized static thresholds using a custom-built, physically accurate simulation framework driven by real-world solar data and dynamic LoRa transmission profiles. Rather than claiming universal superiority, our analysis exposes the distinct operational trade-offs of each method: the AP approach delivers lightweight, near-oracle task throughput; the RL agent provides tunable survival-execution balancing; and AsTAR excels at execution pacing across long energy gaps. Finally, we demonstrate that while these advanced strategies provide critical resilience for severely constrained systems with small capacitors, devices with larger energy buffers can efficiently rely on simpler, less computationally expensive static policies.

### [173] [Parallel Manifold Steering: Efficient Adaptation of Large Associative Memories via Residual Energy Shaping](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24396)
*Kanishk Awadhiya*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对大型 Transformer 模型适配过程中的“可塑性-稳定性”挑战，本文提出了 H-Res 机制，通过在激活流形上施加残差引导，无需修改权重即可实现高性能任务适配，兼顾了记忆稳定性与计算效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型 Transformer 模型作为密集联想记忆（DAMs）存在，但在适配新任务时面临“可塑性-稳定性”困境：直接修改权重（如 LoRA）容易导致灾难性遗忘，而使用静态提示符（如 VPT）则会占用序列长度并降低联想容量。论文旨在寻求一种既能实现高效适配，又能保持模型原始记忆架构稳定性的新方法。

Method: 提出了一种名为“分层残差引导（Hierarchical Residual Steering, H-Res）”的机制。该方法将适配过程建模为激活流形上的控制问题，通过学习一个依赖于状态的向量场，将 Token 的轨迹引导至特定任务的吸引盆中，而不修改全局权重或增加序列长度。

Result: 实证结果表明，H-Res 在联想检索任务中比全局权重修改方法性能提升了 26%，消除了基于提示符方法的额外计算开销，并能有效扩展到结构化领域，同时在理论上证明了其能保持模型的注意力熵并促进神经坍缩（Neural Collapse）。

Conclusion: H-Res 提供了一种高效且稳定的模型适配方案。通过在激活流形上进行操作，它在不改变基础模型权重的前提下实现了精准的任务控制，既解决了“可塑性-稳定性”困境，又实现了理论上的最优性（促进神经坍缩），在保持原始模型检索能力的同时提升了适配性能。

Abstract: Large Transformer models function as Dense Associative Memories (DAMs), retrieving knowledge via high-dimensional attractor dynamics driven by the self-attention mechanism \citep{ramsauer2020hopfield, wu2024attention}. However, adapting these frozen memory systems to new tasks presents a fundamental ``Plasticity-Stability'' dilemma. Current methods either risk catastrophic interference by modifying synaptic weights directly (e.g., LoRA) \citep{hu2021lora} or degrade associative capacity by clogging the retrieval buffer with static prompt tokens (e.g., VPT) \citep{jia2022vpt}. In this work, we propose \textbf{H-Res} (Hierarchical Residual Steering), a mechanism that modulates the effective energy landscape of the Transformer without altering its global equilibrium or expanding its sequence length. By formulating adaptation as a control problem on the activation manifold \citep{chen2018neuralode}, H-Res learns a state-dependent vector field that steers token trajectories into task-specific basins of attraction. We formally prove that H-Res preserves the attention entropy of the foundation model and facilitates Neural Collapse \citep{papyan2020prevalence}. Empirically, Manifold Steering outperforms global weight modification by 26\% on associative retrieval tasks and eliminates the computational overhead of prompt-based methods, scaling effectively to structured domains \citep{zha2023vtab}.

</details>


### [174] [Natural Identifiers for Privacy and Data Audits in Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24408)
*Lorenzo Rossi,Bartłomiej Marek,Franziska Boenisch,Adam Dziedzic*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出利用训练数据中自然存在的随机字符串（NID）作为替代性canary和同分布数据，实现了对已训练大模型进行无需重新训练的隐私审计和数据集推断。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的差分隐私审计方法大多需要在训练阶段植入人工canary数据，导致无法对已训练模型进行审计；而数据集推断方法通常依赖于难以获取的同分布留存数据集（hold-out data），这限制了大规模、后验式隐私审计的实施。研究旨在解决这些实际应用中的局限性。

Method: 提出了一种基于“自然标识符”（Natural Identifiers, NIDs）的隐私审计方法。NIDs是指训练数据中自然存在的结构化随机字符串（如哈希值、短链接）。研究利用其分布特性，将其作为模型训练中的“替代性canary”进行差分隐私审计，并将其作为同分布的对照组数据进行数据集推断（dataset inference），从而无需重新训练模型或额外收集私有留存数据集。

Result: 实验结果表明，利用NID方法，研究人员可以在无需重新训练模型的情况下对已完成训练的模型进行差分隐私审计，并能在没有私有非成员留存数据集的情况下，对包含NID的受疑数据集成功执行数据集推断。

Conclusion: 本研究提出的NID方法通过利用大规模语言模型训练数据中天然存在的结构化随机字符串，有效解决了隐私审计中对训练前插入canary数据或获取同分布留存数据集的依赖，为大模型隐私审计提供了一种可扩展、后验式的解决方案。

Abstract: Assessing the privacy of large language models (LLMs) presents significant challenges. In particular, most existing methods for auditing differential privacy require the insertion of specially crafted canary data during training, making them impractical for auditing already-trained models without costly retraining. Additionally, dataset inference, which audits whether a suspect dataset was used to train a model, is infeasible without access to a private non-member held-out dataset. Yet, such held-out datasets are often unavailable or difficult to construct for real-world cases since they have to be from the same distribution (IID) as the suspect data. These limitations severely hinder the ability to conduct scalable, post-hoc audits. To enable such audits, this work introduces natural identifiers (NIDs) as a novel solution to the above-mentioned challenges. NIDs are structured random strings, such as cryptographic hashes and shortened URLs, naturally occurring in common LLM training datasets. Their format enables the generation of unlimited additional random strings from the same distribution, which can act as alternative canaries for audits and as same-distribution held-out data for dataset inference. Our evaluation highlights that indeed, using NIDs, we can facilitate post-hoc differential privacy auditing without any retraining and enable dataset inference for any suspect dataset containing NIDs without the need for a private non-member held-out dataset.

### [175] [Data Augmentation: A Fourier Analysis Perspective](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24418)
*Behrooz Tahmasebi,Melanie Weber,Stefanie Jegelka*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 论文通过数学证明表明，部分数据增强可以在统计泛化性能上达到与全数据增强相当的效果，从而在保证模型效果的前提下大幅降低大规模对称群带来的计算成本，但也指出了严格对称性约束对全群增强的必要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 全数据增强虽然能利用群对称性提升模型泛化能力，但在群规模较大时计算成本极高。论文旨在探讨部分数据增强（即仅对群的一个随机子集进行增强）是否能在保持统计性能的同时，显著降低计算开销。

Method: 采用傅里叶分析（Fourier analysis）和有限群的表示论（Representation theory of finite groups）作为数学工具，推导了数据增强在泛化误差和样本复杂度方面的统计界限，并对比了全群增强与部分随机采样增强的效果。

Result: 研究发现，对于一类广泛的学习问题，只要采样规模足够，部分数据增强能达到与全增强相同的极小极大（minimax）收敛率。同时证明了，若要实现严格的群不变性，必须涵盖整个群，任何严子集都无法实现。

Conclusion: 该研究通过傅里叶分析和表示论揭示了部分数据增强与全数据增强在统计性能上的权衡：在统计泛化方面，随机采样的小规模子集即可达到接近全增强的极小极大风险率；但在强制执行严格不变性时，必须对整个群进行平均。这为在计算效率和统计最优性之间寻找平衡提供了理论基础。

Abstract: Data augmentation is a simple and model-agnostic approach for exploiting known invariances in learning problems. Given a group acting on the input space, one augments the training set with transformed copies of each sample. Because it exploits symmetries without modifying the underlying learning algorithm, data augmentation can be applied broadly across learning methods. However, this universality comes at a computational cost: when the group is large, full group-sized augmentation quickly becomes computationally infeasible. This raises a fundamental question: Can partial data augmentation achieve the same statistical benefits as full augmentation in terms of generalization and sample complexity? We develop a general framework for investigating this question using Fourier analysis and the representation theory of finite groups. We show that, for a broad class of classical learning problems, partial data augmentation based on a randomly sampled subset of group elements achieves the same minimax rates as full augmentation, up to an approximation error that vanishes as the subset size increases. Our results provide a theoretical explanation for why partial augmentation can retain the statistical benefits of full augmentation despite enforcing symmetry only approximately, and shed light on a recently raised question in learning with symmetries: whether statistically optimal learning under general group invariances can be achieved using computationally scalable methods. Moreover, we prove a complementary impossibility result: enforcing exact invariance via data augmentation requires averaging over the entire group, and cannot be achieved by any strict subset when the hypothesis space is sufficiently expressive. Together, these results provide a unified perspective on full and partial data augmentation, as well as exact and approximate symmetry enforcement.

</details>

Existing approaches address these issues in isolation and rely on implicit feature alignment, limiting effectiveness under concurrent challenges. This paper proposes a knowledge-guided two-stage transfer learning framework that employs a lightweight GPT-2-style Transformer with causal self-attention for hierarchical feature extraction from vibration signals, establishing explicit pathways where pre-trained encoder weights and fault prototype embeddings serve as knowledge carriers from multi-source pre-training to target adaptation. The framework addresses the dual-shift challenge through multi-source learning for generalizable representations, prototype-based knowledge modulation for target adaptation, and taxonomy-adaptive classification for seamless transfer across heterogeneous fault categories. ### [178] [Reasoning as Attractor Dynamics: Latent Memory Retrieval via Gibbs-Weighted Energy Minimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24543)
*Kanishk Awadhiya*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究提出将大语言模型的推理视为寻找“能量景观”中稳健吸引子的过程，通过基于谱熵的加权采样算法，显著提升了模型在数学推理任务中的准确率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统观点认为大语言模型仅是自回归生成器。研究者提出将大模型视为高维稠密关联记忆，认为正确推理对应于潜在空间中深而宽的“平坦极小值”（吸引子盆地），而幻觉则对应于尖锐且不稳定的局部极小值。为了利用这一几何特性，研究旨在通过模拟物理系统中的能量平衡来提升推理准确性。

Method: 提出了基于轨迹谱熵的吉布斯测度检索机制。具体而言：1. 通过采样生成多条推理路径；2. 将推理链视为关联记忆的能量景观，利用逆能量加权（$P \propto e^{-βE}$）对路径进行采样；3. 通过这种物理启发的方法“松弛”系统，引导模型收敛至更稳健的逻辑解（深而宽的“平坦极小值”）。

Result: 实验结果显示，该物理启发机制在 GSM8K 数据集上将 Microsoft Phi-3.5 的性能显著提升了 5.38%（从 84.7% 提升至 90.1%），验证了该方法在抑制幻觉和增强推理鲁棒性方面的有效性。

Conclusion: 大型语言模型的推理过程应被建模为向吸引子盆地趋近的动态稳定过程，而非简单的贪婪预测。该研究证明了利用能量景观视角可以有效识别并剔除幻觉，提升复杂逻辑推理任务的性能。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) are traditionally viewed as autoregressive generators. However, from the perspective of collective computation, they function as high-dimensional Dense Associative Memories that store complex reasoning patterns as latent attractors. In this work, we investigate the energy landscape of mathematical reasoning. We posit that correct reasoning chains correspond to deep, wide attractor basins ("flat minima") in the model's output distribution, whereas hallucinations manifest as sharp, unstable local minima. To exploit this geometry, we introduce a retrieval mechanism based on a Gibbs measure of the trajectory's spectral entropy. By sampling multiple reasoning paths and weighting them by their inverse energy ($P \propto e^{-βE}$), we approximate the equilibrium distribution of the associative memory, effectively ``relaxing'' the system into a robust solution. Empirically, this physics-inspired mechanism improves Microsoft Phi-3.5 performance on GSM8K by 5.38\% (84.7\% $\to$ 90.1\%), demonstrating that inference is better modeled as a dynamic settling process into an attractor basin rather than greedy next-token prediction.

</details>


### [179] [QC-SMOTE: Quality-Controlled SMOTE for Imbalanced Classification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24625)
*Parth Upman,Shreyank N Gowda*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: QC-SMOTE 是一种新型质量控制过采样框架，它通过评估少数类样本的可靠性并根据局部数据特征动态调整生成策略，有效解决了传统方法在噪声区域生成低质量样本的问题，从而显著提升了不平衡数据的分类性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的过采样方法（如 SMOTE）在处理存在噪声或类别重叠的数据集时，往往会产生低质量的合成样本，从而导致分类器决策边界偏移或性能下降。因此，需要一种能够评估样本可靠性并自适应地生成高质量合成样本的框架。

Method: 提出了一种名为 QC-SMOTE 的质量控制过采样框架：1. 使用复合邻域信任度分数（结合局部密度、安全水平及与多数类别的隔离度）评估少数类样本的可靠性；2. 采用 IPQ 引导的“K 个中挑选最优”策略生成合成样本，并根据局部数据几何结构动态调整插值范围；3. 当邻域纯度低于自适应阈值时，自动将低质量合成样本替换为原始少数类样本的副本。

Result: 在 30 个不平衡数据集上的实验结果表明，与现有的过采样方法相比，QC-SMOTE 在平均 AUC-ROC 和 Macro F1 指标上均取得了最优表现，特别是在中度和重度不平衡的情况下，提升效果最为明显。

Conclusion: 通过引入质量感知和几何自适应的过采样机制，QC-SMOTE 能够有效处理类别不平衡问题。研究表明，在噪声或类别重叠区域通过质量控制和灵活的生成策略，能够显著提升分类器的稳健性和性能，特别是在重度不平衡数据集中表现突出。

Abstract: Class imbalance poses a significant challenge in classification, where existing methods such as SMOTE often generate low-quality synthetic samples in regions with noise or class overlap. We propose QC-SMOTE, a quality-controlled oversampling framework that estimates minority sample reliability using a composite neighbourhood trustworthiness score combining local density, safe-level, and isolation from the majority class. Synthetic candidates are generated using an IPQ-guided best-of-K strategy that evaluates midpoint purity and, when required, majority clearance, with allocation guided by sample reliability and boundary informativeness. Generation behaviour adapts across overlap--imbalance regimes, adjusting interpolation range and selection criteria to match local data geometry. Low-quality synthetic samples are replaced with original minority duplicates when neighbourhood purity falls below an adaptive threshold, providing graceful degradation by reverting to duplication in severely noisy regions. Experiments on 30 imbalanced datasets using repeated stratified cross-validation show that QC-SMOTE achieves the strongest average AUC-ROC and Macro F1 among the compared oversampling methods, with particularly clear gains under moderate and severe imbalance. These results demonstrate the importance of quality-aware, geometry-adaptive synthetic sampling for robust imbalanced classification.

### [180] [FlowPipe: LLM-Enhanced Conditional Generative Flow Networks for Data Preparation Pipeline Construction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24679)
*Kunyu Ni,Lei Cao,Jie He,Xiaotong Zhang,Jianfeng Jin,Junyu Dong,Yanwei Yu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了 FlowPipe，一个基于条件生成流网络（C-GFlowNets）的自动化数据准备流水线生成框架，通过结合 LLM 语义调制与失败感知搜索，显著提升了流水线构建的精度与效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 数据准备流水线自动构建面临组合爆炸和评估成本高昂的挑战。现有基于 Multi-DQN 的最先进方法存在三个瓶颈：长程信用分配能力弱、数据集上下文信息利用不足、以及在稀疏空间中探索效率低下。因此，研究旨在开发一种更高效、更具语义理解能力的自动化构建框架。

Method: FlowPipe 采用了一种基于条件生成流网络（C-GFlowNets）的统一框架。主要技术手段包括：1. 利用轨迹平衡（Trajectory Balance）目标函数实现从终端奖励到早期决策的信用分配；2. 引入基于 FiLM 的深度语义调制机制，将 LLM 推导的逻辑先验注入模型以增强对数据集语义的理解；3. 在流目标中加入失败感知（failure awareness）机制，通过避免无效状态来提升搜索效率。

Result: 在涵盖 74 个真实世界数据集的两个基准测试中，FlowPipe 表现优异，平均模型准确率提升了 11.96%，且训练收敛速度较现有先进基线提高了 12.5 倍。

Conclusion: FlowPipe 通过将管道构建建模为条件概率流生成任务，有效解决了传统方法在长程信用分配、上下文感知及搜索效率方面的局限性。该研究证明了利用 GFlowNets 和 LLM 先验知识进行自动化机器学习流水线生成的巨大潜力。

Abstract: Data preparation pipelines improve data quality in machine learning by transforming raw tables into learning-ready data through sequential cleaning and feature transformation operators. However, automatically constructing such pipelines is computationally difficult because operator sequences are combinatorial and end-to-end evaluation is expensive. Existing state-of-the-art (SOTA) Multi-DQN methods still face three key limitations: decoupled value estimators weaken long-horizon credit assignment, dataset context is only weakly injected into the policy, and exploration is inefficient in a sparse search space with many invalid states. To address these issues, we propose FlowPipe, a unified framework that formulates pipeline synthesis as conditional probabilistic flow generation over a directed acyclic graph. FlowPipe uses Conditional Generative Flow Networks (C-GFlowNets) with a Trajectory Balance objective to connect terminal validation rewards with early pipeline decisions. It further introduces Deep Semantic Modulation through Feature-wise Linear Modulation (FiLM), allowing LLM-derived logical priors to condition the policy's internal activations according to dataset semantics. In addition, FlowPipe incorporates failure awareness into the flow objective to avoid invalid states and concentrate search on high-potential regions. Experiments on two benchmark suites with 74 real-world datasets show that FlowPipe outperforms SOTA baselines, improving accuracy by 11.96% on average and achieving 12.5x faster training convergence. Source code is available at https://github.com/KunyuNi/FlowPipe.

### [181] [Grad Detect: Gradient-Based Hallucination Detection in LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24790)
*Anand Kamat,Daniel Blake,Brent M. Werness*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为Grad Detect的梯度分析方法，通过捕获大模型推理时的内部梯度模式，在无需额外推理成本的情况下，有效检测模型输出的幻觉，并能精准定位失效源头。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型虽然能力强大，但在高风险应用场景中容易产生幻觉。现有的检测方法主要依赖输出置信度或采样一致性，往往难以有效捕捉模型内部的错误征兆，因此需要一种能够深入模型内部、利用梯度信息来提升检测可靠性的方法。

Method: Grad Detect方法：利用推理过程中单次前向-反向传播（forward-backward pass）产生的层级梯度模式来预测幻觉。该方法通过分析梯度结构而非仅仅依赖输出层信号，并结合层级消融研究，确定了最后五层包含了超过97%的判别性梯度信号，从而实现了低开销的高效部署。

Result: 实验结果表明，Grad Detect在多个问答基准测试中的幻觉检测和模型弃权预测任务上，均持续优于基于置信度和采样的方法。通过在四个架构家族的11个模型上进行测试，证明了该方法具有良好的跨模型通用性，且在仅使用最后五层梯度的情况下，依然能保持极高的性能。

Conclusion: 本文提出的Grad Detect是一种高效且可解释的幻觉检测框架。研究证明，大模型的内部梯度模式包含关于输出正确性的关键信息，且这些判别性信号高度集中在模型的最后几层。该方法不仅在幻觉检测和模型弃权预测任务上表现出色，还为理解模型失效的机制提供了新的视角。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) have demonstrated remarkable capabilities across diverse tasks, yet they remain prone to generating hallucinations. Detecting these hallucinations is critical for deploying LLMs reliably in high-stakes applications. We present Grad Detect, a gradient-based approach for predicting hallucinations by analyzing layer-wise gradient patterns from a single forward-backward pass during inference. Our method shows that the internal gradient structure of a model carries rich information about the correctness of its output. This information is not accessible through output-level signals alone. We evaluate Grad Detect on several Q&A benchmarks across both hallucination detection and model abstention prediction, where it consistently outperforms confidence-based and sampling-based baselines. Through comprehensive layer ablation studies across all eleven models from four architectural families, we find that the final five layers concentrate over 97% of the discriminative gradient signal, enabling efficient deployment with minimal performance loss. Grad Detect provides a unified framework for predicting multiple dimensions of LLM reliability, offering strong predictive performance alongside interpretable insights into where and how model failures originate.

### [182] [Real vs. Complex Spectral Bases for Neural Operators: The Role of Green's Function Alignment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24851)
*Jason Sulskis,Sathya Ravi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为哈特利神经算子（HNO）的新型算子模型，作为FNO的实值镜像。研究发现，谱基的选择应与偏微分方程算子的对称性相匹配：HNO适用于处理自伴随椭圆型方程，而FNO因其复数相位表征能力更适合处理时变型方程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 傅里叶神经算子（FNO）在处理实值偏微分方程时，由于复数FFT的共轭对称性存在表征冗余。作者旨在探索一种更高效的实值算子表示方法，并探究算子谱基（实数域的哈特利基底 vs. 复数域的傅里叶基底）与偏微分方程算子性质（如对称性、相位特征）之间的深层数学联系。

Method: 本文提出了一种名为“哈特利神经算子”（HNO）的新架构。HNO使用离散哈特利变换（DHT）替代了FNO中的快速傅里叶变换（FFT）。由于哈特利变换完全基于实数空间，不存在共轭对称性导致的冗余，因此HNO在相同参数量下能保留两倍的频率分量。通过在不同类型的偏微分方程（椭圆型与时变型）上进行对比实验，验证了其在不同对称性下的性能差异。

Result: 实验结果证实了性能与算子相位内容之间的单调关系：HNO在处理泊松方程、双调和方程等自伴随椭圆型方程时表现优异；而随着算子相位内容的增加（如波动方程、伯格斯方程、纳维-斯托克斯方程），FNO的优势逐渐显现。对于无相位的热传导方程，两者表现接近。HNO在实数计算上实现了更高的存储与计算效率。

Conclusion: 本文提出并没有所谓的“通用最优”算子，最佳的谱基选择取决于算子本身的数学对称性。研究表明，哈特利神经算子（HNO）在处理具有实对称格林函数的自伴随椭圆型方程时更具优势，而傅里叶神经算子（FNO）凭借复数乘法对相位的表征能力，在处理具有相位演化特征的时变型偏微分方程时表现更佳。研究强调了根据偏微分方程算子的对称性选择合适谱基的重要性。

Abstract: Fourier Neural Operators (FNO) learn solution operators of partial differential equations by parameterizing global convolutions in the complex Fourier domain. For real-valued PDE solutions, the complex FFT carries representational redundancy through conjugate symmetry. We introduce the Hartley Neural Operator (HNO), the exact real-valued mirror of FNO: it replaces the FFT with the purely real Discrete Hartley Transform and learns a single real multiplier per retained spectral mode, with no complex arithmetic. Because the real Hartley spectrum is not halved by conjugate symmetry, HNO retains twice as many frequency corners as FNO but one real weight where FNO carries a complex pair, so the two operators are iso-parametric at equal width and differ only in spectral basis. Our central thesis is that the best basis is a property of the operator. Self-adjoint elliptic operators (Poisson, biharmonic) have real, symmetric Green's functions that the real Hartley multiplier diagonalizes exactly, and HNO is favored there. Time-dependent operators carry phase, from oscillation in the wave equation to transport in advection, Burgers, and Navier-Stokes, which a real diagonal multiplier cannot represent, so FNO is favored there, and increasingly so with the operator's phase content, leaving the phaseless heat equation as the borderline case. Training both operators identically and benchmarking across PDE classes, initial-condition families, and boundary conditions, we find an elliptic-versus-time-dependent split that is monotone in operator phase content and matches the Green's-function theory we develop. Rather than a universal winner, our findings give a predictive rule: match the spectral basis to the symmetry of the solution operator.

### [183] [Weight-Space Geometry of Offline Reasoning Training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23740)
*Aleksandr Nikolich,Igor Kiselev,Vladimir Platonov,Karina Romanova*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究对比了六种离线强化学习方法在模型蒸馏中的机制差异，发现虽然RFT/RIFT在更新方向上与SFT高度重合，但DPO通过在正交子空间进行权重优化，显著提升了模型的数学推理准确率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前离线强化学习（RL）损失函数（如RFT, DPO等）常被用于将推理能力从大模型蒸馏到小模型，但业界通常仅通过下游准确率来评估这些方法。作者旨在探究这些方法在机制上是否具有本质区别，还是最终收敛到了相似的权重更新路径上。

Method: 研究人员以Qwen3-4B为基础模型，采用attention-only LoRA微调方式，在相同的数学推理数据集上训练了六种主流方法（SFT、RFT、DFT、RIFT、Offline GRPO、DPO）。通过余弦相似度、主角子空间分析、线性模式连通性及CKA（Centered Kernel Alignment）等技术手段，深入分析了这些方法产生的权重更新增量（deltas）。

Result: 1. SFT、RFT和RIFT的权重更新高度共线，性能表现相似；2. DFT的更新方向与其它奖励加权方法存在明显偏差；3. Offline GRPO在SFT损失盆地内产生了显著的正交方向分量；4. DPO表现出明显的独特性：其更新位于近乎正交的子空间，表现出模式连通性壁垒，并在GSM8K和AIME26任务上均显著超越了其他方法。

Conclusion: 研究表明，尽管多种离线强化学习方法（如RFT、RIFT、DPO等）在数学推理任务上被广泛使用，但它们在权重更新机制上存在显著差异。DPO表现出最强的性能，其更新方向与SFT接近正交，且处于不同的参数损失盆地中；相比之下，RFT和RIFT在机制上与SFT高度重合。这一发现强调了在选择对齐算法时，不仅要看下游准确率，还需深入理解其权重空间的演化特性。

Abstract: Offline reinforcement-learning losses (RFT, RIFT, DFT, Offline GRPO, DPO) are widely used to distill reasoning from large teachers into smaller students, and are typically compared on downstream accuracy alone. We ask whether they are mechanistically distinct or converge to a similar weight update. Training six methods (SFT, RFT, DFT, RIFT, Offline GRPO, DPO) on identical math rollouts from a single base model (Qwen3-4B) with attention-only LoRA, we analyze the resulting deltas via cosine similarity, principal-angle subspace analysis, linear mode connectivity, and CKA. We observe: (i) SFT, RFT, and RIFT have nearly colinear weight deltas (cosine >= 0.97, top-1 principal angle ~7 deg median over 144 modules) and comparable GSM8K accuracy (87-88%, n=1319; pairwise McNemar p >= 0.15); (ii) DFT diverges further in direction than any reward-weighted method despite using the same data; (iii) Offline GRPO adds a substantial component orthogonal to the SFT direction (~67% globally, up to ~86% in late layers) while staying in the SFT loss basin; (iv) DPO sits in a near-orthogonal subspace, shows a mode-connectivity barrier, and collapses late-layer CKA to ~0.46. DPO also reaches the highest accuracy in our protocol on both GSM8K (93.5%, McNemar p < 10^-9 vs. each other method) and AIME26 (30.0% vs. 3.3-10.0%); its training uses a 10x smaller learning rate than the others (the standard convention), so the update-norm and accuracy gaps reflect loss-function and optimizer choices jointly, and a learning-rate-matched DPO comparison is left for future work.

### [184] [A Survey on Federated Causal Discovery and Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23741)
*Xianjie Guo,Yuwei Wang,Guodu Xiang,Xiaoli Tang,Kui Yu,Han Yu,Qiang Yang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文是首篇关于联邦因果推理（FCI）与联邦因果发现（FCD）的系统性综述，通过构建多维分类法和统一的逻辑流水线，深入分析了在隐私保护前提下如何进行跨机构因果分析，并为未来的研究指明了方向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 本文采用系统综述的方法，通过多维分类法对联邦因果发现（FCD）与联邦因果推理（FCI）进行梳理：针对FCD，基于结构学习方式、数据划分方式及结构知识获取三个核心决策维度进行分类；针对FCI，基于目标估计量及估计策略（如加权法与深度生成架构）进行分类，并将两者整合为统一的联邦因果推理流水线。

Conclusion: 本文通过构建统一的联邦因果推理流程框架，明确了联邦因果发现（FCD）与联邦因果推理（FCI）之间的互补关系，并指出了隐私保护、通信效率、理论保证及实际应用等方面的未来研究方向与挑战，为跨学科研究者提供了清晰的路径。

Abstract: Causal reasoning, which encompasses the discovery of causal structures and the inference of causal effects, is fundamental to data-driven decision making. In practice, data for reliable causal analysis are often distributed across institutions and cannot be centralized due to privacy regulations or communication constraints. Federated learning (FL) addresses this by enabling collaborative analysis without raw data sharing, giving rise to the rapidly growing field of federated causal discovery (FCD) and inference (FCI). However, the interdisciplinary nature of this field and the absence of a comprehensive survey present barriers to entry for researchers. This paper bridges that gap by providing a systematic review through multi-dimensional taxonomies. Grounded in the three core design decisions underlying any FCD solution, namely how structures are learned, how data are partitioned, and what structural knowledge each party obtains, we organize FCD along three axes: methodological paradigm, federation topology, and structural scope. We further examine key practical dimensions, including temporal dynamics, data heterogeneity, missing data, and non-identical variable sets. For FCI, we categorize methods by target estimand (average versus individualized/conditional treatment effects) and by estimation strategy, from classical weighting methods to modern deep generative architectures. Unlike prior works that treat FCD and FCI separately, we formalize their connection as complementary stages of a unified federated causal reasoning pipeline, where FCD supplies the structural knowledge required for valid effect estimation in FCI. Finally, we highlight their shared concerns regarding privacy, communication efficiency, theoretical guarantees, and application domains, and conclude by identifying open challenges for future research.

### [185] [Low-power analogue neural networks with trainable nonlinear connections for continuous control](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23742)
*Ian T. Vidamour,Fernando Aguirre,Thomas J. Hayward,Matthew O. A. Ellis,Charles Swindells,Alexander McDonnell,Martin Trefzer,Finley Robins,Luca Manneschi,Susan Stepney,Tony Kenyon,Oliver J. Sutton,Jack C. Gartside,Ivan Y. Tyukin,Adnan Mehonic,Eleni Vasilaki*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究引入了一种受KAN启发的物理神经网络架构，通过将可训练的非线性函数置于连接处，在处理连续、平滑的任务时实现了极高的参数效率与微瓦级超低功耗计算，但在分类任务中优势有限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统物理神经网络受限于将非线性物理响应简化为标量权重，这限制了其表示能力和能效。研究旨在通过在连接处引入可学习的非线性算子，克服这一局限，利用模拟物理特性实现更高效的机器学习。

Method: 受柯尔莫哥洛夫-阿诺德网络（KAN）启发，作者提出在物理神经网络的连接处部署可训练的非线性函数，而非仅仅将其作为标量权重使用。研究利用现场可编程模拟阵列（FPAA）实现模拟带通滤波器作为这些函数，并通过仿真验证了忆阻器实现该架构的可行性。

Result: 实验表明，该架构在机器人运动学、连续控制及光伏最大功率点跟踪等平滑连续函数映射任务中，相比多层感知机（MLP）大幅减少了节点和连接需求。硬件迁移验证了约35,000个连接的高保真度，且CMOS实现方案的功耗预计可低至30微瓦。但在分类任务等非平滑决策边界上，该方法未表现出参数效率优势。

Conclusion: 本研究证明了将可训练的非线性函数置于物理神经网络连接处是提升计算效率的关键，而非依赖于特定的物理器件。这种架构在处理平滑、连续的目标任务时具有显著的参数效率优势，并为实现超低功耗（微瓦级）的物理人工智能硬件铺平了道路。

Abstract: Physical neural networks promise low-power machine learning by computing directly with analogue device physics, but most architectures force nonlinear device responses to act as scalar weights. Inspired by Kolmogorov-Arnold networks, we place trainable nonlinear functions on the connections, making each physical connection a learnable computational element. Realising these functions as analogue band-pass filters on field-programmable analogue arrays, we find that the benefit is task-dependent and follows from the smoothness of the physical basis: the networks represent smooth, continuously valued targets, including robotic kinematics, continuous control, and photovoltaic maximum-power-point tracking, with far fewer nodes and connections than multilayer perceptrons, but offer no parameter-efficiency advantage on classification-like decision boundaries. Trained networks transfer to hardware across approximately 35,000 connections with quantified fidelity, and a dedicated CMOS implementation is projected to operate at approximately 30 microwatts. A memristive realisation reproduces the same behaviour in simulation, indicating that the advantage comes from placing trainable nonlinearity on connections, rather than from a particular device.

</details>


### [186] [ARIA: Adaptive Region-Based Importance Allocation for Conditional Diffusion Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23898)
*Loay Mualem,Vinh Tong,Samir Darouich,Mathias Niepert*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: ARIA是一种用于条件扩散模型蒸馏的自适应训练框架，通过在线监控并动态分配资源至师生模型差异较大的条件区域，实现了在保持蒸馏目标的同时，显著提升模型在未见和稀缺分布下的泛化性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 条件扩散模型的知识蒸馏在处理海量条件空间（如文本提示）时存在瓶颈。现有的方法虽然通过切换条件来扩大训练覆盖面，但缺乏对训练资源的高效分配机制。当数据有限或计算资源受限时，如何确定训练重点以覆盖更广泛的分布区域成为核心挑战。

Method: 提出了一种名为ARIA的框架。该方法通过将条件空间划分为多个粗粒度区域，并在线维护每个区域的“师生差异（teacher-student discrepancy）”估计。根据这些差异，ARIA动态调整训练过程中的采样概率，将计算资源集中在那些学生模型表现较差、 misalignment（失准）严重的区域，同时保持原始的蒸馏目标不变。

Result: 实验结果表明，ARIA在多种架构和设置下均优于现有的RC（Random Condition）方法。特别是在未见过的（unseen）和样本不足（underrepresented）的区域，ARIA表现出了显著的性能提升。此外，理论分析证实了其追踪机制在受限方差和漂移假设下能够有效收敛。

Conclusion: ARIA通过自适应调整条件空间的训练分配，解决了条件扩散模型蒸馏中效率低下和分布外泛化能力不足的问题。该研究证明了在线追踪师生差异的机制不仅能加速收敛，还能显著提升模型在未见或稀缺样本上的表现，为大规模蒸馏任务提供了有效的优化范式。

Abstract: Distilling conditional diffusion models aims to transfer the behavior of a large teacher to a smaller student while preserving alignment across conditioning inputs. Unlike recognition tasks, knowledge distillation in conditional diffusion often struggles to transfer knowledge beyond the training distribution, since the predicted noise strongly depends on the conditioning signal. As a result, effective distillation requires exploring a large conditioning space. In practical settings, this creates a major bottleneck. Paired image-condition data may be limited, and generating synthetic images for every available condition is often computationally infeasible, while the pool of conditions, such as text prompts, can be extremely large. Recent work addresses this issue by switching conditions during training, exposing the student to a broader conditioning space without changing the distillation objective. Yet this raises a complementary question: once a large conditioning corpus is available, how should the training effort be allocated? In this work, we introduce ARIA, a framework that adaptively allocates training effort across coarse regions of the conditioning space. By maintaining online estimates of teacher-student discrepancy at the region level, ARIA focuses updates where misalignment persists while preserving the original distillation objective. Empirically, ARIA improves over RC across most architectures and settings, with the clearest gains observed in unseen and underrepresented regimes. We also provide a theoretical analysis showing that the proposed tracking mechanism follows the evolving discrepancy during training under bounded variance and drift assumptions.

</details>


### [187] [Offline Reinforcement Learning for Warehouse SLAM Throughput Control](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23978)
*Tina Dongxu Li,Mouhacine Benosman,Rajat Kumar,Kevin Tan,Ken Meszaros,Trevor Dardik*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种针对仓储SLAM系统吞吐量优化的离线强化学习框架，通过历史数据训练策略模型，在不干扰在线系统的情况下，实现了吞吐量与下游稳定性的平衡，大幅改善了仓储运行效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 仓储履行环境中的SLAM吞吐量控制直接影响系统拥塞及运行效率。传统方法难以平衡吞吐量最大化与下游处理稳定性，而在线RL探索风险较高。因此，作者旨在利用历史日志通过离线RL寻找一种能够自适应调整节流行为、优化吞吐量的控制策略。

Method: 提出了一套离线强化学习框架：1.构建包含历史信息的系统状态表示；2.设计动作空间抽象以应对控制行为的延迟影响；3.制定兼顾上下游操作指标的奖励函数；4.采用模型无关的方法，整合了三种前沿离线RL算法（如CQL等）；5.使用多维度评估策略，包括回归估计、Fitted Q Evaluation (FQE) 以及基于Deep Koopman动态模型的评估。

Result: 实验结果显示，CQL策略表现最优，在实际测试中将系统健康度提升了22.97%，平均节流时间减少了3.18%，证明了该框架在保障安全的前提下提升仓储运营效率的有效性。

Conclusion: 该研究表明，离线强化学习是优化复杂仓储环境中SLAM吞吐量控制的有效且安全的手段。通过利用历史操作日志，该方法能够在大规模实际部署中显著提升系统稳定性和整体运行效率，为仓储自动化控制提供了可扩展的解决方案。

Abstract: We present an offline reinforcement learning (RL) framework for optimizing SLAM throughput control in a warehouse fulfillment environment. SLAM (Scan/Label/Apply/Manifest) throughput directly influences system congestion and operational efficiency. Our RL-based control approach dynamically recommends SLAM throughput settings that adaptively balance throughput maximization with downstream stability through intelligent adjustment of throttling behavior. We include a history-informed state representation, action space abstraction for delayed-impact control, and a reward function that captures both upstream and downstream operational metrics. Our approach is algorithm-agnostic, enabling integration of multiple offline RL methods under a unified architecture. We instantiate our framework with three state-of-the-art offline RL algorithms, and trained the models offline using de-identified historical operational logs from a large-scale warehouse. Policy performance is evaluated using a comprehensive multi-method strategy. These include model-free approaches including immediate reward estimation via regression models and long-horizon Fitted Q Evaluation (FQE), as well as model-based Deep Koopman dynamics evaluation. Empirical results reveal that the CQL policy consistently outperforms alternatives, improving system health by 22.97% and reducing average throttling duration by 3.18%. These findings demonstrate the potential of offline RL for safe and scalable warehouse throughput control optimization.

</details>


### [188] [Learning to Trigger: Reinforcement Learning at the Large Hadron Collider](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23993)
*Zixin Ding,Shaghayegh Emam,Giovanna Salvi,Cecilia Tosciri,Abhijith Gandrakota,Jennifer Ngadiuba,Nhan Tran,Christian Herwig,David W. Miller,Yuxin Chen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了利用强化学习（GFPO算法）进行大型强子对撞机触发阈值的自适应实时控制，成功解决了静态触发菜单无法应对运行条件漂移的问题，并在真实碰撞数据上验证了其优越的性能与鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型强子对撞机等科研设施依赖实时事件过滤（触发系统），但现有的触发菜单多为静态且人工调整，难以应对探测器条件、堆积（pileup）和背景构成随时间漂移导致的性能下降问题，因此需要一种自适应的动态触发阈值调整机制。

Method: 本文将触发阈值调整建模为序贯决策问题，并采用强化学习（RL）代理进行实时控制。作者适配了分组过滤策略优化（GFPO）算法，并提出了两个变体（GFPO-F和GFPO-FR）以在训练过程中强制执行背景速率的可行性约束，使其适用于高吞吐量、低延迟的流式环境。

Result: 在模拟环境下，该代理相比基线将容差范围内的时间间隔占比分别提高了48%（$H_T$触发器）和28%（异常检测触发器），信号效率提升高达2%。在真实CMS碰撞数据测试中，无需微调即可实现56%和28%的容差提升，且信号效率均有进一步改善。

Conclusion: 本研究首次在大型强子对撞机（LHC）的真实数据上证明了强化学习能够有效优化在线触发系统。通过引入GFPO算法变体，该方法实现了在保证背景速率约束的同时，显著提升信号效率及系统运行的稳定性，为高能物理实验的实时数据过滤提供了新的范式。

Abstract: High-throughput scientific facilities such as the Large Hadron Collider depend on real-time event filtering (\textit{triggering}) under tight constraints on bandwidth, latency, and storage. In practice, trigger menus are largely static and hand-tuned and can become suboptimal as detector conditions, pileup, and background composition drift over time. We cast online threshold tuning as a sequential decision-making problem: a reinforcement learning agent ingests streaming summaries of recent rates and signal-sensitive features and updates trigger thresholds to maximize signal efficiency while tracking a target background rate within a tolerance band. We adapt Group-Filtered Policy Optimization (GFPO) to streaming control and introduce two variants (GFPO-F, GFPO-FR) that enforce background rate feasibility during training. On a benchmark that emulates realistic collider operation, we study two representative triggers: a total transverse energy ($H_{T}$) trigger sensitive to pileup variation, and an anomaly-detection (AD) trigger based on reconstruction loss for rare or non-standard signatures. On Monte Carlo streams, our agent increases the fraction of in-tolerance time intervals by 48\% ($H_T$) and 28\% (AD), with a cumulative gain of up to 2\% in signal efficiency on those in-tolerance intervals. Transferring from simulation to \emph{real} collision data (CMS Run 283408), the same agent, without fine-tuning, achieves a 56\% ($H_T$) and 28\% (AD) in-tolerance improvement over baselines, with further signal-efficiency gain on both triggers. To our knowledge, this is the \emph{first} demonstration of RL-based trigger control on real Large Hadron Collider collision data. Code is available at https://github.com/Zixind/GFPO\_LHC.

</details>
